<pb n="319">

319,1

|| śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ || <lb>
sadbhyo yathārhamabhipūjya sapradakṣiṇaṃ praṇāmaṃ nirmāya |
ātmānaṃ putraviṣayiṇaṃ kartumupakrame medinīnāyakapriyaḥ ||

319,4

bho tatrabhavanto bhavantaḥ pratyekaśo bṛhaspatisamānavaibhavāḥ | tarhi mama saṃpattiratiśāyinī | nāhaṃ dhanasya <lb> vidyamānasya saṃkhyāṃ kalayāmi | paraṃ tu mama tanayo nāsti | kimatra kāraṇam | tatastaiḥ samastairapi saṃbhūya <lb> jagade | haradatta dattakarṇamākarṇayatu bhavān | sarvaṃ jānīte | tarhyetāvadeva jñānasya kimiti gocarata<lb>yā vidhuro 'si | itare padārthāḥ sarve 'pyudyamādhikaraṇasāmagryā prāduṣkārayituṃ śakyāḥ | paraṃ yaśastathā <lb> saṃtatiśca sukṛtasaṃcayavañcanayā na kathaṃcana tadubhayaṃ sādhayituṃ śakyate | <lb>
pañca kāmayate kuntī tatputrāṇāṃ vadhūrapi |
satīṃ vadati loko 'yaṃ yaśaḥ puṇyairavāpyate ||

319,11

manaḥkāṅkṣito manorathastadānīmevāsādyate yadā parameśvare niratiśāyinī bhaktirjāgarti | parameśvarānugrahaṃ <lb> vinā na kāpi kāmanā phalāya kalpate | <lb>
nirantarasukhāpekṣā hṛdaye vartate yadi |
tyaktvā bhavabhavānbhāvānbhavānīvallabhaṃ bhaja ||
pade pade nidhānāni yojane yojane bilam |
aprasanne virūpākṣe kutaḥ kṣīreṇa bhojanam ||

319,17

ityabhihite tena haradattena parameśvaraprītiprakarṣodayasiddhaye vividhadānapuṇyarudrajapakoṭihomādi pramukhakarma <lb> kartumādadhre | tena sukṛtātiśayena tasya tanayaḥ samajaniṣṭa | tasminputrajanidine haradattaḥ paṭahodghoṣapuraḥsaraṃ <lb> yāvanto yācakāstānadaridrānakārṣīt | arthināmavasarātikramo nātighaṭiṣṭa | <lb>
putre jāte vyatīpāte saṃkrāntau grahaṇe tathā |
khalu yajñe vivāhe ca dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ||

319,22

tanayajanane yatkiṃciddānādi sukṛtaṃ vidhīyate tena śreyasā bālakasyāyurvardhate grahāḥ sugrahā bhavanti <lb> sarve 'pyupadravāḥ pradrāvyante | <lb>
mantre tīrthe dvije deve daivajñe bheṣa≤ce≥«je» gurau |
yādṛśī bhāvanā yatra siddhirbhavati tādṛśī ||
<pb n="320">

320,1

bhāvapuraḥsaraṃ manasi vikṣepaṃ bibhrāṇaḥ sāttvikavāsanayā yatsukṛtasaṃcayamārjayati tasya sukṛtasya <lb> phalamadhikatvena bobhavīti | bhāvānusāriṇī siddhiradhigamyate | tadanu tena haradattena daivajñānāhūya <lb> jātakarma niramāyi | madanasena iti nāmadheyaṃ vyadadhat | tataḥ krameṇānnaprāśanacaulakarmavratabandhādikaṃ <lb> vidhāya samastakalākalāpebhyaḥ snātakamakārayat | tato vaṅgadeśanivāsinaḥ kumudakośanāmadheyasya putrī <lb> nāmataḥ prabhāvatī prabhāvitīrṇasamastajananayanāhlādakāriṇī | tāmeṇīdṛśaṃ madanasenaḥ paryaṇaiṣīt | <lb> sarvāṅgasaundaryavibhramavatī sakalakalākovidā saṃgītasāhityarasābhinayavilasadasamaśaraśaranikarahatipa<lb>ravaśā parirambhasaurabhyavijṛmbhamāṇaviṣamaviṣayarasaviṣamañjarī kaṭākṣacchaṭākṣepaparikṣiptajanatā ghanatāpa<lb>saṃpāditānekalokaśokasaṃvardhanaprabhāvatī | tena madanasenena tattadbhāvakalākalāpakuśalena bhṛśamanvarajyata | <lb> tayorapyatiśāyī premabhāvo 'vardhiṣṭa | sukhena tṛtīyapuruṣārthamaseviṣātām | yadi muhūrtārdhamapi parasparaṃ <lb> na dadṛśāte tadānīmanekayugāvagāḍhavirahavedanāvaidhuryamāvirbhāvyate | anayā rītyā tena madanasenena <lb> puruṣārthadvayādviratena garīyaḥ sukhamanubhūya bhūyasānehasā kāmapuruṣārtharasopasevāyāṃ prāvartiṣṭa | <lb>
amṛtaṃ śiśire vahniramṛtaṃ svāmigauravam |
bhāryāmṛtaṃ guṇavatī dhāroṣṇamamṛtaṃ payaḥ ||
vāṇī sārasvatī yasya bhāryā rūpavatī satī |
lakṣmīrdānavatī yasya saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam ||
ramyā rāmā yadi kulavadhūstyāgabhogāya vittaṃ vaktre vāṇī sarasamadhurā śaṃkare cittavṛttiḥ |
sadbhiḥ saṅgo vapuṣi dṛḍhatā satkule janma puṃsāṃ dhigdhigduḥkhaṃ niraśanapadaṃ svargamekāntadurgam ||

320,20

itthaṃ madanasenaḥ samastamapi nijamudyamamapahāya viṣayopabhoga evāśrāntaviśrāntaḥ | tadānīṃ tasya pitrā <lb> śikṣitumādadre | ityabhyadhāyi ca | re madanasena | tvamātmīyaṃ vyāpāraṃ parityajyāharniśaṃ dayitāyatta eva <lb> vartamāno 'si | tarhi tvadīyametadvyavasitamaucityaṃ nānuṣajjate | <lb>
ativyayo na kartavyo nātikāmaṃ parāmṛśet |
atitṛṣṇānapatyaśca avaśyaṃ nihate dhanam ||
atirūpādgatā sītā atigarveṇa rāvaṇaḥ |
atidānādbalirbaddhaḥ sarvatrātiśayaṃ tyajet ||

320,27

asmātkāraṇānnātiśayaḥ kāmasevāyāṃ tvayā kāryaḥ | puruṣeṇa sthāneṣveteṣu saṃtoṣa evādartavyaḥ | <lb>
saṃtoṣastriṣu kartavyo manmathe bhojane dhane |
triṣu caiva na kartavyaḥ tapasi dhyānadānayoḥ ||

320,30

itthaṃ pitrā bahuśo 'nuśāsito 'pi madanaseno viṣayāsaktamānaso na taduditamabhimanute sma | <lb>
na paśyati madāndho 'pi kāmāndho 'pi na paśyati |
cakṣurhīnā na paśyanti cārthī doṣaṃ na paśyati ||
arthāturāṇāṃ na sukhaṃ na bandhuḥ kāmāturāṇāṃ na bhayaṃ na lajjā |
vidyāturāṇāṃ na sukhaṃ na nidrā kṣudhāturāṇāṃ na rucirna pakvam ||

320,35

kāraṇādetasmānmadanaseno na pituḥ śāsanamabhimanutetarām | tato 'yaṃ haradattaḥ putrasyopālambhaṃ tri<lb>vikramanāmānaṃ mitramāśrāvayata | tatastamākarṇya trivikramo haradattamavādīt | śṛṇu sakhe | manmathara<pb>sākrāntasvānto janaḥ kathamekahelayaivānayituṃ śakyaḥ | hṛdayāntaḥsthagitaprathamarasāvasthodgāḍhā na kiṃ sevante | <lb> antaḥkaraṇaguṇahārdabaddhasaṃbandhaśaithilyaparipāṭyā parimṛditaraṇaraṇakatāsamāśraye vyāvahārikī buddhiriya<lb>mupavarṇayitumudarkasaṃparkopayoginī bhavati | ..... trivikrama tvaṃ joṣamāssva | ahameva śanaiḥśanairupapattiviśeṣaistaṃ <lb> śikṣiṣye ityabhidhāya haradatto nijamandiraṃ samāsadat | tadanu haradattaḥ putrasya viṣayopabhoge niratyutkarṣa<lb>viśeṣamabhivīkṣya tadasoḍhatayā dehamātmīyaṃ parityaktuṃ paryaicchat | trivikramo vārttāmapi śuśrāva | tatastvaramā<lb>ṇo haradattopāntamājagmivān | tāvatāsau haradattaḥ samagrāmapi prāyopaveśasāmagrīṃ nirmāyāvasthito <lb> vartate | tataḥ tamaticukopa | haradatta tvāṃ vihāya nānyaṃ kaṃcana mandamatimupalabhe | tvaṃ dehatyāgāya kimarthaṃ <lb> vṛthaiva pravṛtto 'si | deho 'yaṃ kiyatā mahāyāsenāsādyate | dehenānena padārthacatuṣṭayamapi sādhyaṃ <lb> saṃpādyate | asya dehasya kṛte yoginaḥ siddhāḥ sādhakāśca nānārasarasāyanādiṣu paricinvate | <lb>
<pb n="321">
punardārāḥ punarmitraṃ punaḥ kṣetraṃ punaḥ sutāḥ |
punaḥ śubhāśubhaṃ karma na śarīraṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||
āpadarthaṃ dhanaṃ rakṣeddārānrakṣeddhanairapi |
ātmānaṃ satataṃ rakṣeddārairapi dhanairapi ||

321,14

ata eva tvamucitaṃ parijihāno 'si | ākarṇayatu nāma bhavān | putrasya śrama īdṛśastava gṛhītumayuktaḥ | <lb>
jāyamāno haredbhāryāṃ vardhamāno hareddhanam |
mriyamāṇo haretprāṇānnāsti putrasamo ripuḥ ||

321,17

tato haradatto 'pyabhāṣīt | ahametasmātputravyasanajanitaduḥkhāddavīyānbhaviṣyāmi | tādṛśaḥ prakāraḥ kaści<lb>dasti cettadānīmācakṣva | tadānīṃ trivikramastamācaṣṭa | malayaparvate guṇasāgarasaṃjñaḥ śuko 'sti | tathā <lb> himavataḥ śṛṅge malayavatī nāma śārikā vartate | tau dvāvapi muniśāpataḥ pakṣiṇāvajāyetām | tau <lb> dvāvānetavyau | tatastau bhavataḥ putrāya upadeśaṃ dāsyataḥ | tato haradatto 'vādīt | tau kathaṃ pakṣiṇau <lb> jātau | kena doṣeṇa muninā śaptau | tvamapyetatkathaṃ jānīṣe | tadetadvṛttāntamanastamitasāmānyaṃ bhavānavādīt | <lb> tacchrutvā trivikramaḥ śukaśārikayoḥ prathamavṛttāntamabhyuditavān | ākarṇaya mitra rājavaiśyavarya mānasaṃ <lb> sara uttarasyāṃ diśi yojanamātre parvate nivasatyekam | tatra caikastaponidhināmadheyastapodhano bahubhi<lb>rmunibhirupāsitaḥ samāste | sa caikasmindine vidyādhananāmānaṃ śiṣyaṃ devārcanāya puṣpāṇyāhartuṃ prātiṣṭhipat | <lb> sa munīśvarasyājñāsamayamanantarameva niragāt | <lb>
baṇḍaḥ śākuniko mantrī kimekaḥ stambhasevakaḥ |
sadyo 'pavādī rogī ca saptaitānsevakāṃstyajet ||
alasaṃ niṣṭhuraṃ vyarthaṃ krūraṃ vyasaninaṃ śaṭham |
asaṃtuṣṭaṃ kṛtaghnaṃ ca tyajedduṣṭaṃ mahīpatiḥ ||

321,30

tato 'sau puṣpāharaṇāya gacchanpathi puṣpavāṭikāmapaśyat | dṛṣṭvā ca tāṃ puṣpāṇyupacetumantaḥ prāvikṣat | <lb> tatra ca ghanasaṃpiṇḍitaparṇapuñjasaṃpūritaṃ phalasamāhārātsamantato namraṃ mākandataruṃ makarandarasonmadiṣṇu<lb>madanamaṅgalamahodayaṃ manaḥsarvasvāpahārakaṃ locanagocaraṃ cakāra | tasya tale gandharvamithunaṃ dadarśa | sureśva<lb>rapurī gāyako viśvāvasusaṃjñako gandharvarājaḥ | tathā tasya dharmacāriṇī mālāvatyāhvayā | taddvayamapi <lb> krīḍākautukaparavaśaṃ vipañcīṃ gṛhītvā militvā gānaṃ kurvāṇamabhūt | tayorgāyatoḥ sa ko '≤piḥ≥«pi» layaḥ <lb> prādurabhūdyena sākṣācchrīpārvatīnāthaścandramaulireva svayaṃ parituṣyati | tacchrutvā sa vidyādhanaḥ svaṃ vidheyaṃ <lb> vismṛtya tadevākarṇayaṃstatraivātiṣṭhat | <pb>
<pb n="322">
subhāṣitena gītena yuvatīnāṃ ca līlayā |
yasya na dravati svāntaṃ sa vai mugdho 'thavā paśuḥ ||

322,3

itthaṃ tayorvinodaparavaśayorgānaṃ kurvāṇayoḥ kālātikramaḥ prāvartiṣṭa surādhīśasya sevāsamayo 'pacakrāma | <lb> tataḥ pākaśāsanastatrājagāma | śatakratumākrāntasaṃnikṛṣṭapradeśaṃ dṛṣṭvā prabhuḥ kopaṃ kariṣyatīti bhītyā <lb> viśvāvasumālāvatībhyāṃ śukaśārikayoradhāriṣātāṃ rūpe | rūpānyatvaṃ racitamabhivīkṣya sutrāmā sāsūyaṃ <lb> provāca | bhavantau martyaloke rūpābhyāmetābhyāṃ sthāsyataḥ | tatprabhoḥ kopaprakarṣaparuṣaśāparūpaṃ krakacasaṃparkakarka<lb>śaduḥsahaṃ vacanamākarṇya dvāvapyavanatavadanāvatiṣṭhatām | tatastau dīnavadanāvabhivīkṣya divaspatermanastaru<lb>ṇakaruṇābhareṇāsvādīkṛtam | <lb>
yasya cittaṃ dravībhūtaṃ kṛpayā sarvajantuṣu |
tasya jñānaṃ ca mokṣaśca kiṃ jaṭābhasmacīvaraiḥ ||

322,11

etallakṣaṇalakṣitaṃ satāṃ caritamabhyupagantavyam | tatastenākṛtakṛtyayoḥ śatakratunānugrahaḥ kṛtaḥ | martyaloke <lb> nivasatorbhavatormadanasenākhyasya haradattatanayasyopayogo bhaviṣyati | tato 'sāvanujñāsyati saṃtuṣyaiva <lb> bhavantau | tadānīṃ punarnagaramasmadīyamavāpsyatha | ityabhidhāya niragātsakrandanaḥ | tatsamastamapi caritaṃ vi<lb>dyādhano 'vekṣamāṇa āsīt | tataḥ puṣpāṇāmapaharaṇāya samayo 'pyaticakrāma | tataḥ sumanasaḥ samānīya <lb> munisamīpamupayātaḥ | tato vyāhāri tapodhanena | vidyādhana | vayaṃ devānarcayituṃ puṣpāharaṇāya prahiṇuma <lb> tvām | tarhi samayātikramaṃ kasmādakārṣīstvam | asmadīyā devapūjā vighnitā | tato malīmasamānanaṃ <lb> vidhāyāsthāt | <lb>
jīvanto 'pi mṛtāḥ pañca vyāsena parikīrtitāḥ |
daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ pravāsī nityasevakaḥ |

322,20

atha tena vidyādhanena gandharvavṛttāntaṃ taponidhestasya purastādupavarṇitam | tadākarṇya munīndro 'sāvato <lb> 'diṣṭa | vidyādhana | viśvāvasumālāvatyau vāsavo 'bhiśaptavān | tatastau martyalokamāpatatāṃ tatastvaṃ martya<lb>lokamavāpsyasi | tatastenānugraho yācitaḥ | tadanu karuṇākrāntasvānto munīndro vyāhṛtavān | tvaṃ martyaloke <lb> nivasan jātismartā bhaviṣyasi | haradattena samaṃ maitramutpatsyate tasyopayogāya bhaviṣyasi | tataḥ punara<lb>pyāśramamasmadīyamāgamiṣyasi | tataḥ so 'haṃ vidyādhanastrivikramo bhūtvāvatatāra | ata eva śukaśāri<lb>kayoḥ prathamavṛttāntaṃ jānāno 'smi | tarhi te śukaśārike 'trāgacchataḥ | tathā karavāṇi | tataḥ śuciḥ <lb> snāto bhūtvā sauparṇaṃ mantraṃ japtavān śukaśārikayorāvāhanamuddiśya | tatastajjaptakṣaṇa eva tau pakṣiṇau <lb> pāṇiprāptāvajāyetām | tata ekasminpañjare prakṣipya madanasenasya mandire citraśālāyāḥ pañjare antarā<lb>sthāpayat | haradattatrivikramau niyatau bhūtvā yathābhilaṣitaṃ niragātām | itthaṃ bhūyāṃsyatikrāntāni <lb> dināni | tatastayā śārikayā babhāṣe śukaḥ | bho prāṇanātha | yasmai kāryāyāvāmānītau tarhi tvaṃ <lb> prayojanaviśeṣeṇāsmai madanasenāya na kimapyabhidadhāsi | tato 'smadāgamanasya ko nāmopayogaviśeṣaḥ | <lb> tadākarṇya kīro 'pi girāmudgāramāvirabhāvayat | priye tvaṃ yadabhidhatse mamāpi mānasaṃ tadvimṛ<lb>śatyaharniśaṃ paraṃ prastāvo na samāpatati | <lb>
prastāvasadṛśaṃ vākyaṃ svabhāvasadṛśaṃ priyam |
ātmaśaktisamaṃ krodhaṃ yo jānāti sa paṇḍitaḥ ||

322,35

itthaṃ kasmiṃścidavasare madanasenaḥ śukaṃ vyājahāra | bho rāmacandra | vārttāmekāṃ vyācaṣṭāṃ bhavān | tataḥ <lb> śukaḥ provāca | śṛṇuṣvāvahito madanasena | adyatane samaye tvāṃ vihāya nānyaḥ kaścana sarvato 'bhimānaṃ <pb> svamānasenānubadhnāti | dharmārthakāmalakṣaṇapuruṣārthatrayasādhanena tvayaivāsārasya saṃsārasya saṃsāratā vidhīyate <lb> tato te 'pyatiśayamokṣaḥ | prathamajaḥ puruṣārthastvayaiva nādhigataḥ | sarvasvamanvabhāvi puruṣārthadvayabādhanena | eta <lb> eva puruṣārthāḥ pūrvapuruṣaiḥ pūrvaparipāṭyā sādhayitavyāḥ | vyatikramo na kartumanveṣṭavyaḥ | <lb>
<pb n="323">
dharmamarthaṃ vyatikramya kevalaṃ kāmamāśritaḥ |
ayaśobhājanaṃ loke paratrāpi ca ninditaḥ ||

323,6

anyacca | viṣamaviśikhasya vyasanaparavaśaṃ tvāmabhivokṣya tava pitarau duḥkhākrāntasvāntau staḥ | tayorduḥkhavi<lb>taraṇe tava garīyānpratyavāyo 'bhīpsitaploṣamāpādayannaharniśaṃ jarījṛmbhīti | yastu mātāpitarāva<lb>vajānīte taṃ vihāya nānyaḥ kaścana patito 'stīti «|» <lb>
mātāpitrorapoṣṭāraṃ kriyāmuddiśya yācakam |
parārthe tilahotāraṃ dṛṣṭvā cakṣurnimīlayet ||

323,11

tasmādākarṇayatu bhavān | etadarthe mahābhāratīyamitihāsamekaṃ tvāṃ prati vakṣyāmi | ityabhidhāya madanasenaṃ <lb> prati śukaḥ paurāṇikīṃ kathāmekāṃ vyāhartuṃ pravavṛte | śṛṇu madanasena | mālavajanapadamadhye nāgapuraṃ nāmā<lb>grahāraḥ | tatra vijayaśarmāhvayo brāhmaṇo hyavātsīt | tasya tanayo devaśarmābhavat | tena samastā api <lb> vidyā abhyastāḥ paraṃ śāntirmanasyudayaṃ nāsādayati sma | tataḥ pitarāvabhāṣiṣṭa | ahamanyā api vidyā <lb> adhyetuṃ vrajiṣyāmi | tatastau niṣeddhuṃ pracakramāte | tatastayoruditamavamatya dvitīyameva deśāntaraṃ nira<lb>gāt | itthaṃ deśāntare 'ṭāvyaṃ kurvāṇo 'nekatīrthāni devāyatanāni pavitrakṣetrāṇi darśaṃ darśaṃ darśādiṣu <lb> viśeṣaparvasu parvasaparyāparāyaṇo bhūtvā tāpasaveṣānusaraṇarasikaḥ paraṃ vairāgyamavalambya viṣayavāsanā<lb>vitṛṣṇo niḥspṛhatayā pravartamānaḥ citrakūṭaparvatamāsasāda | tatra pavitramekaṃ tapovanamālokya mahāmeruprāsādaṃ <lb> śivasya dṛṣṭvā nirmalajalaparipūrṇaṃ saraścābhivīkṣya samāsādya cāplavanaṃ saṃdhyopāsanaṃ surapitṛtarpaṇaṃ ca <lb> vidhāya prāsādamāsādya śivamarcayitvā stotrādinā saṃtoṣya praṇipatya ca svacetasi paramaṃ samādhā<lb>namanubhūya tatraikasya tarostale niṣasāda | padmāsana upaviśya nāsikāgre dṛśau vinyasya śyāmalāṅgaṃ <lb> caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhacakragadāpadmodāyudhamāśrayaṃ śriyaḥ purodeśāvasthitasaṃbandhayojitakarayugalagaruḍamityādivi<lb>śeṣaṇaviśiṣṭaṃ śrīmantamādinārāyaṇaṃ dhyātvā sāṃsārikadehāhaṃkāratāpuraskṛtavyāpāro paramacetasoni<lb>vāraṇatayā sakalāvaraṇapariṇatāśayaḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitavān | <lb>
dehabhāvaṃ parityajya nirālambanamāśritaḥ |
ānandapadasaṃyogī sa yogī modate sukham ||
nidrādau jāgarasyānte yo bhāva upajāyate |
taṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayedyogī dvividhābhāvavarjitam ||

323,29

evamākāravikāranirākaraṇenāsau devaśarmā dhyānanimīlitacakṣuratiṣṭhat | tadanvādau tundilāntaḥkaraṇo <lb> bahirviṣayasaṃbandhābhibandhibodhavidhuro madhyaṃdinātikramamapi nājñāsīt | tato bhikṣānimittaṃ prati<lb>niragāt | tato 'mbarapadavīmavagāhamānā balākā tasyoparyadūṣayat | yāvatā upari paśyati tāvatā <lb> balākāmāluloke | tatastāṃ sāsūyamaśapat | śāpavitaraṇasamayasamanantarameva bhuvastalaṃ sā gatāsuḥ papāta | <lb> tadavekṣya devaśarmā manasi mahāntamanutāpamāsasāda | varākaḥ prāṇī vṛthaiva garīyāṃsaṃ nigrahaṃ grāhitaḥ | <lb> alpīyasyaparādhe daṇḍabāhulyamāsañjitaṃ kopaparādhīnatayā na kiṃcidajñāsiṣaṃ tapaso 'smadvihitasya <lb> pariploṣaḥ samavartiṣṭa | <lb>
krodho vaivasvato rājā tṛṣṇā vaitaraṇī nadī |
vidyā kāmadughā dhenuḥ saṃtoṣo nandanaṃ vanam ||
<pb n="324">
nāsti kāmasamo vyādhirnāsti mohasamo ripuḥ |
nāsti krodhasamo vahnirnāsti jñānasamaṃ sukham ||

324,3

ityabhidhāya devaśarmā tasya doṣasyāpākaraṇakāmyayā punarapi snānadevārcanādikarmāvaśeṣaṃ nirmāya <lb> samādhāvupaviśyaikāntacitto bhūtvā kāmapi mantrānuvṛttiṃ kṛtavāndvaitabhāvaparityāgena | <lb>
aṅgulyagreṇa yajjaptaṃ yajjaptaṃ merulaṅghane |
vyagracittena yajjaptaṃ tatsarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||

324,7

tadanu nimittaṃ nirmāya nagarāntargantuṃ prakrāntavān | tato nārāyaṇanāmadheyasya brāhmaṇasya gṛhaṃ bhikṣā<lb>haraṇāyāgacchat | tatastadīyapatnyā dvāri gataṃ bhikṣumavekṣya bhikṣāṃ dātuṃ ≤prā≥«pā»traṃ kare 'kāri | tāvatā <lb> tasyāḥ patirnārāyaṇo gṛhānagacchat | tatastayā bhikṣāpātraṃ sthāpayitvā kṣaṇamātraṃ sthātavyamiti devaśarmā <lb> vyāhāri | bhartre jalapātraṃ dattvā snāpanāya salilaṃ samānīya snānasurasaparyābhojanādisāmagrīsaṃpādanaṃ <lb> saṃsādhya devaśarmabhikṣunimittaṃ bhikṣāmāhṛtavatī | tato devaśarmā tāmavādīt | etāvantaṃ samayamahaṃ dvāryeva <lb> tiṣṭhāmi | tvaṃ vilambena bhikṣāṃ vitariṣyasi | tarhi garīyānpratyavāyastavāghaṭiṣṭa | tataḥ sā bhikṣumavocan | <lb> ekasmādvidheyaviśeṣādekasya balavattaratā | yasyāsti dharmo 'tra yasminnucitatvamukhyatā sa tenādau vi<lb>dhātavyaḥ | tato 'nyasmai prayojanāya pravartitavyam | <lb>
apūjyā yatra pūjyante na pūjyante guṇānvitāḥ |
trīṇi tatra bhaviṣyanti durbhikṣaṃ maraṇaṃ bhayam ||

324,17

asmābhiḥ pativarivasyānusaṃdhātavyā | <lb>
ayameva paro dharmo hyayameva paraṃ tapaḥ |
patiśuśrūṣaṇaṃ yatra tatstrīṇāṃ svargahetukam ||

324,20

etāvatāsmadīyaṃ samastamapi vyavasitaṃ caritārthaṃ bhavati | <lb>
kokilānāṃ svaro rūpaṃ pātivratyaṃ tu yoṣitām |
vidyā rūpaṃ kurūpāṇāṃ kṣamā rūpaṃ tapasvinām ||

324,23

bhavādṛśānāṃ yogīśvarāṇāṃ kṣamaiva bhāvyā | tadānīmevāvikalaṃ yogasya phalamāsādyate | itarathā vyarthaḥ <lb> pariśrama evodeti | tato 'sau saroṣabhrūbhaṅgadurdṛśyatārakaṃ nyaphālayat | tadanu tayā pativratayāvādi | <lb> bhavatāṃ kopena kiṃ nāma śakyate kartum | kathamahaṃ sā balākā yā kopena bhavato 'ntarikṣādapatat | <lb> etadākarṇya devaśarmā vismayavivaśaḥ saṃjātaḥ | anyapradeśajanitaṃ vṛttāntaṃ kathameṣā dṛgviṣayībhāvamāpāda<lb>yituṃ pragalbhate | na hyasau sāmānyasaṃbhāvanāsaṃbhāvyā bhavati | abhidhāyetthaṃ tāṃ daṇḍavatpraṇatavān | <lb> vyābhāṣīcca | tvayāhamupadeṣṭavyaḥ | tavedṛśamatīndriyaṃ jñānaṃ kutastyam | tataḥ sāśrāvayat | yasya prāṇino <lb> yo dharmo 'bhihito 'sti taṃ yathāvadanutiṣṭhati | tarhi svabhāvata eva jñānodayastasminnāspadaṃ saṃpādayati | <lb> mama patyurupācaraṇena jñānaṃ jarījṛmbhīti | bhavānvārāṇasīṃ gacchatu | tatra dharmavyādho nāma mṛgayuradhivasa<lb>ti | sa tubhyaṃ jñānopadeśaṃ dāsyati | tataḥ sādhvīvacasāsau devaśarmā vārāṇasīṃ prati prasthitavān | śanaiḥ <lb> śanairviśvanāthanagaraṃ muktikṣetramāsāditavān | nagaramadhyamāviśya tīrthe samāplāvya śrīviśveśvaramabhipūjya <lb> pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍavatpraṇipatya pavitramātmānaṃ vidhāya dharmavyādhaṃ didṛkṣustadupāntamagacchat | tatastena <lb> darśanasamanantaramevābhāṣi | kiṃ pativratayā prasthāpitā bhavantaḥ | tadākarṇya tamavadat | tathaiva prasthāpito <lb> yuṣmatsaṃnikṛṣṭamāgato 'smi | tato dvāvapi vyādhasya niketanaṃ gatau vyādhena devaśarmāṇamāsanāyāsanaṃ <pb> pracikṣipe | tadanu vyādhasya vṛddhau pitarau tiṣṭhataḥ | tayorupāntaṃ gatvā draviṇamārjitaṃ tatpurastādavasthāpya <lb> daṇḍavatpraṇipatya karau yojayitvā atithireko 'bhyāgato vartata ityavādīt | tacchrutvā pitarau jagadatuḥ | <lb> atithirāgataśceddaivamasmadīyam | tasya saparyā jyāyasī kāryā | <lb>
<pb n="325">
gururagnirdvijātīnāṃ varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥ |
patireko guruḥ strīṇāṃ sarvasyābhyāgato guruḥ ||
atithiścāpavādī ca dvāvetau mama bāndhavau |
apavādī haretpāpamatithiḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ ||

325,8

tato dharmavyādhastasminnatithau satkāramakārṣīt | tato devaśarmābhyabhāṣata | tvaṃ ca sarvajñastvayā dharmopadeśaḥ <lb> kartavyaḥ | taduditamākarṇya mṛgayurjagāda | tvaṃ patitastvamupadeśayogyo na bhavasi | atithiriti matvā <lb> mānanīyo 'smākam | <lb>
vipro vāpyathavā śūdraścaṇḍālo vā gṛhāgataḥ |
atithiḥ pūjya evātra sarvathā sādhuvadbhuvi ||

325,13

tvaṃ pitṛbhyāmuditaṃ na karoṣi | kimarthaṃ tīrtheṣu bhrāntyā śramaṃ vyarthamāpādayasyātmani | tavaitadvilasitaṃ sakalaṃ <lb> vyarthameva | tvaṃ punargṛhāngaccha pitroḥ śuśrūṣāṃ sādhīyasīṃ samācara | etāvatā svata eva jñānamutpadyate | <lb> ayameva tavopadeśaḥ kṛtaḥ | tato vyādhavacasā nijameva niketanaṃ nirjagāma devaśarmā | pitṛbhyāṃ samāgamat | <lb> tayormanasi tanayasamāgamajanitaṃ niratiśayaṃ saukhyaṃ pravartiṣṭa | etāvatāsau devaśarmā niṣpāpaḥ saṃjātaḥ | <lb> ata eva madanasena tvayā pitroḥ paricaryā kartavyā | etāvatā tvamapi vicitrapātraṃ bhaviṣyasi | kāle <lb> pitrorupāsanamapahāya nāparaṃ kimapi nṛṣu prārthitaphalapradaṃ jāgarti | paśyaitadviṣaye tavaikamudāharaṇamupa<lb>varṇayāmi | bhāgīrathītaraṃgiṇītīre pāṇḍarapurasaṃjñakaṃ pṛthu nagaram | tatra puṇḍarīkastu pitrorupāstiṃ <lb> mahanīyāmaharniśamācarati | tajjātatapo'tiśayasāmarthyena svayamevākuṇṭhadhāmā vaikuṇṭhaparivṛḍho vaikuṇṭha<lb>vasatiṃ śithilīkṛtya tamupaḍuḍhauke | so 'dyāpi tatrārtha evāvasthito 'bhūt | tatsthānaṃ dakṣiṇadvārakātvena <lb> sarvatra prakhyātamāvirbibharti | etāvatphalaṃ pitrorasti paricaryāyāḥ | tarhi tvamapi pitroḥ sevāmupāsva | <lb> kathāmenāṃ madanasenaṃ prati śuko 'bhāṣiṣṭa | tadākarṇya madanasenaḥ kīraṃ gīrbhirupācarat | kīra tvadīyapra<lb>sādena paramo bodho mama hyudiyāya | ityabhidhāya madanasenaḥ pitroḥ samīpaṃ pra≤ri≥«ti»vrajya daṇḍavatpraṇipatya <lb> karau saṃyojya vyajijñapat | etāvato divasānmuṣitasarvārthasārtho 'smi yo 'haṃ bhavatāmādeśaṃ na kṛtavān | <lb> tadetadvimānasugataṃ mamājāyata | adya prabhṛti preṣye yathādeśaḥ pradīyate tathaitāvatprayojanapreṣaṇaṃ mayi <lb> dātavyam | etadākarṇya haradattaḥ saṃtuṣya paraṃ pramodabharaṃ prāptavān | <lb>
yasya putraḥ piturbhakto bhāryā chandānuvartinī |
vibhavo dānabhogāya tasya svarga ihaiva tu ||

325,29

tataḥ saṃtuṣya haradattaḥ putraṃ pratyuvāca | tvayā kuṭumbasya paścādbhāge cintodvahanaṃ kartavyam | ahaṃ dhanārjana<lb>vyavasāyāya pravrajiṣyāmi | dhanahīnaḥ pumāṃstṛṇasyāpi na vinimayatāmarhati | <lb>
dhanī pūjyo dhanī ślāghyo dhanī sarvaguṇāgraṇīḥ |
dhanahīnā na śobhante nirgandhā iva kiṃśukāḥ ||
yasyārthastasya mitrāṇi yasyārthastasya bāndhavāḥ |
yasyārthaḥ sa pumāṁlloke yasyārthaḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ ||
<pb n="326">
yasyāsti vittaṃ sa naraḥ kulīnaḥ sa paṇḍitaḥ sa śrutavānguṇajñaḥ |
sa eva vaktā sa ca darśanīyaḥ sarve guṇāḥ kāñcanamāśrayante ||
akāraṇaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ tantrīśabdo 'pyakāraṇam |
akāraṇaṃ trayo vedāstaṇḍulāstatra kāraṇam ||

326,5

iti piturabhihitaṃ niśamya madanaseno janakaṃ jagāda | mayi putre vidyamāne yadi tatrabhavadbhiḥ prayāsaḥ <lb> kartavyastadānīṃ putrasya ka upayogaḥ | yastu tanayo janayitroḥ saparyāyāmananuyuktaḥ kiṃ tasya janmanā | <lb>
ko 'rthaḥ putreṇa jātena yo na vidvānna dhārmikaḥ |
tayā gavā kiṃ kriyate yā na dogdhrī na garbhiṇī ||

326,9

yastu pitroḥ saparyayā sukhaṃ janayati tasyaiva saphalaṃ janma netarasya | <lb>
vittānusāriṇo dharmaḥ śraddhānvitaśivārcanam |
piturmātuḥ sadā bhaktiḥ saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam ||
ekenāpi suputreṇa siṃhī svapiti nirbhayam |
sahaiva daśabhiḥ putrairbhāraṃ vahati gardabhī ||

326,14

ata eva bhavanto 'traiva tāvattiṣṭhantu | ahameva vāṇijyavidhānāya vrajiṣyāmi | ityanujñāmādāya nirga<lb>tavān | nijamandiramāsādya prāṇapriyāṃ prabhāvatīṃ prati prāvocat | priye prabhāvati | dhanamārjayituṃ <lb> vyavasāyoddeśena iyāsurasmi | tvayā na kaścinmadvirahajanyaśramaḥ samavalambanīyaḥ | mayāpi bhavatyāḥ kṣaṇa<lb>syāpi viyogaḥ soḍhumaśakyaḥ | paraṃ janakavacanamanatilaṅghanīyamiti matvā gamanasaṃjāyamānamanā asmi | <lb> tadviṣamaviśikhaviṣayavimukhaṃ viṣādaviṣaviśeṣapoṣakaṃ guruvacoviṣavedanāyanātiploṣaparaṃ patyuḥ krakacakarkaśaṃ <lb> vacanamatiduḥsahaṃ śrutvā nirastajīviteva vidhvastāpaghanā vigalitāṅgasaṃdhibandhā galitakalā pairāha<lb>taprabhā prabhāvatī mohānandasaṃdohabhūyasyā tāpoṣṇavyathayā galagṛhīteva prāṇeśvaraṃ prati provāca | śṛṇuṣva <lb> prāṇanātha | piturvacanamanatikramaṇīyaṃ paramo dharmaḥ | paramanyadapyasti | yaduktaṃ | <lb>
prāvṛṭkāle yātrā yauvanakāle pūruṣadāridryam |
prathamasnehe virahaḥ trīṇyapi duḥkhānyatigurūṇi ||

326,24

etattritayamapi puruṣasyātikaṣṭataram | <lb>
siddhe hyanne phale pakve nārīprathamayauvane |
kālakṣepo na kartavyaḥ kālasya tvaritā gatiḥ ||

326,27

etāvatsu prayojaneṣu puruṣeṇātyutsukatayā prayatanīyam | <lb>
utkocaṃ prītidānaṃ ca dyūtadravyaṃ subhāṣitam |
kāminīṃ prathamāvasthāṃ sadyo gṛhṇāti buddhimān ||

326,30

itthaṃ prabhāvatī prābravīt | paraṃ na tattasya cetasi paryeti | tadanu hiraṇyagarbhagṛhiṇīhṛdayaṃgamaiḥ priyavacobhiḥ <lb> samāśvāsya tāṃ niragāt | tatastayābhyadhāyi | madanasena tava mama cettādṛśaṃ paramaṃ premasāmagryaṃ tarhi <lb> māmīdṛśīṃ parityajya tvayā gamanaṃ kathaṃ kriyamāṇamasti | tato 'sāvajalpat | ahaṃ yatra kvāpi gatavān¿tarhi¿ <lb> tatrāpi tvaṃ mama hṛdaye vasantyevāsi | evaṃ nayamikadṛśā jānīhi | <pb>
<pb n="327">
girau kalāpī gagane ca meghā lakṣāntare bhānurathāpsu padmam |
dvilakṣasomaḥ kumudasya bandhuryo yasya maitrī na ca tasya dūram ||
dūrastho 'pi samīpastho yo vai manasi vartate |
yo hi citte na varteta samīpastho 'pi dūrataḥ ||

327,5

vyāhṛtyetthaṃ madanaseno niragacchat | tatastayā bahujalapariplute vilocane akāriṣātām | tadālokya mada<lb>nasenastasyāḥ samīpe samāgatya nibiḍaparirambhasamārambhasaurabhyamabhyasyātmīyapāṇināśruparimārjanaṃ vidhāya <lb> śukaśārike avocat | ākarṇayatāṃ guṇasāgaro mālāvatī ca | iyaṃ prabhāvatī sarvasminnapi viṣaye <lb> bhavatorupahāre tiṣṭhantī | bhavadbhyāmetasyāścetaso virahajanyapralayakālasaṃkāśaṃ kaṣṭaṃ śanaiḥ śanairuktiviśeṣaira<lb>pohitavyam | iyaṃ bhavaddhaste dattāsti | etasyā viraho vardhituṃ na dātavyaḥ | ityabhidhāya madanaseno <lb> vaṇikkaraṇanimittaṃ manīṣitaṃ kṛtvā deśapradeśamuddiśya nirayāsīt | tadupari prabhāvatī vivoḍhurvirahave<lb>danāvasthayā vihvalāvayavā rātriṃdivaṃ tadavasthāmavalambamānā sānnodakakriyāyāmapi na spṛhāṃ badhnāti | <lb> tatastasyā virahavyathābāhulyamabhivīkṣya śārikā śukamuvāca | rāmacandra | madanasenena prabhāvatī dattā<lb>sīdāvayoḥ | yadiyaṃ bhavadbhirvirahavyathākadarthanato nivāraṇīyā | tarhyetāṃ viyogavanajvalanajvālāja<lb>ṭālajājvalyamānāpaghanāṃ mārakārāgāravihāraviklavakleśaviśeṣavigalitāṅgasarvasvāṃ vikṣatekṣaṇe 'kṣaṇaśo<lb>kaśaṅkunikāraparikaramanākulamābadhnānāṃ tvameva kimiti kathācaritretihāsādibhiḥ kautukādhikaṃ jana<lb>yanduḥkhaviśeṣāpākaraṇena na śikṣayasi | tava maunālambanamanupadaṃ tavaiva vacanīyatāmāpādayiṣyati | <lb> tato niśamitakāntāvacanaḥ śakuntastadvacanānukūlakalitakalevarakāntasaṃkocakliṣṭāntaḥkaraṇagaṇastāmabhāṣīt | <lb> prāṇādhipe | strīṇāṃ cetāṃsi kṣaṇikāni durvārāṇi nirvāhaśūnyāni ca | paśyāmi tāvadetasyāścetaso <lb> 'vasthitāyatiḥ kimudarketi | tatastadavabodhāttadanurūpaṃ kamapyupāyaṃ racayāmi | <lb>
anṛtaṃ sāhasaṃ māyā mūrkhatvaṃ calacittatā |
aśaucaṃ nirdayatvaṃ ca strīṇāṃ doṣāḥ svabhāvajāḥ ||

327,22

ityuktvā pakṣī joṣamāsādyātiṣṭhat | tadanvekasmindivase prabhāvatī svasyopatyakāyāṃ sthitavatī | tato <lb> vinayakandarpeṇa pārthivakumāreṇa tatrasthā samanmathāvasthā kadarthitānāṃ svasthakaraṇapariṇatadivyamahauṣadhī <lb> sā dadṛśe | tadanvanekakalākovidā vīkṣaṇakṣaṇābhilakṣaṇābhilakṣitaharṣotkarṣotpādanavailakṣaṇyāstātkā<lb>likottaravinimayaniyamitamanovṛttisvecchāviharaṇaparihṛtavigrahāḥ śrutisamuditaparabrahmātyantikānubhava<lb>saṃbhāvitāḥ stokālokaśokaśaṅkūtkīlanakovidāḥ patyurmanasi saṃśrutya kṛtamapyātmīyamaparādhaṃ vismāraya<lb>ntīrvyavahāre paramārthe ca nānodāharaṇānugṛhītopapattisaṃpattisphuritādharā evaṃvidhā dūtīḥ prabhāvatīṃ <lb> prati jighāya | tāśca tasyāḥ saṃnidhānamāgatya śanaiḥ śanairbahuvidhāṃ vibudhahṛdayaṃgamāṃ goṣṭhīṃ kurvanti <lb> manovāsanānurūpaṃ nirūpayanti | anena prakāreṇa prabhāvatyā saha naikaṭyaṃ prāvartiṣṭa | tataśca vyāhartumādadre | <lb> prabhāvati tvaṃ bharturviyogaṃ kasmādbibharṣi | avidyamānamapi śramaṃ nije mānase kasmādāropayasi | adyatanaṃ <lb> dinaṃ dvitīyadine na nirvahati | gatāstu divasā na punarāgacchanti | adya tvaṃ nijāvayavavidyamānānurā<lb>gaṃ tāruṇyaṃ lāvaṇyaṃ ca kimiti kimiti vṛthaiva parikṣapayasi | tvaṃ yadviyogaṃ bibhrāṇāsi sa cedbhavatyāṃ <lb> premaparavaśaḥ syāttadātmanā samaṃ kimiti na nayati | sa tu puratogatābhirnitambinībhiḥ samaṃ divyaṃ <lb> viṣayasukhamupabhuñjannāste | tvaṃ bharturbhaktyā kiṃ na bhakṣayasi | anayā patiśuśrūṣayā kā nāma jāteti <lb> mahyamekāmapi pradarśaya | paralokopabhogyātpātakādbibheṣi cettadā sa paralokastatpātakaṃ ca kasya <lb> locanagocaropabhāvamāpannaṃ vijṛmbhitam | <pb>
<pb n="328">
yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ jīvedṛṇaṃ kṛtvā ghṛtaṃ pibet |
bhasmībhūtasya dehasya punarāgamanaṃ kutaḥ ||

328,3

tattvamupabhogavirahitamātmīyaṃ janma kimiti vṛthaivātivāhayasi | svecchayā sukhopabhogamācarantyā bhavatyā <lb> vayamapi sāhāyyabhāvaṃ yāsyāmaḥ | anena rājakumāreṇa vinayakandarpeṇa samaṃ bhavatyāḥ saṃgamaṃ kārayāmaḥ | <lb> etāvatāpi januḥ saphalaṃ bhaviṣyati | etādṛśairvacobhistasyā mānasaṃ bhramitam | <lb>
saṃtaptāyasi saṃsthitasya payaso nāmāpi na śrūyate muktākāratayā tadeva nalinīpattrasthitaṃ dṛśyate |
antaḥsāgaraśuktimadhyapatitaṃ tanmauktikaṃ jāyate prāyeṇādhamamadhyamottamajuṣāmevaṃvidhā vṛttayaḥ ||
svātantryaṃ pitṛmandireṣu vasatiryātrotsave saṃgatiḥ goṣṭhīpūruṣasaṃnidhāvaniyamo vāso videśe tathā |
saṃsargaḥ saha puṃścalībhirasakṛdvṛtternijāyāḥ kṣatiḥ patyurvārddhakamīrṣyitapravasanaṃ nāśasya hetuḥ striyāḥ ||

328,14

tataḥ sā prabhāvatī bhūyobhirbhūṣaṇairātmānaṃ bhūṣayitvā vyabhicaraṇāya nirgantuṃ prāvartata | tadānīṃ śārikā <lb> pakṣiṇaṃ vyābhāṣīt | madanasenena iyaṃ prabhāvatyāvayorupahāre niveśitāsīt | tasyaiṣā vyabhicāre pravarta<lb>mānā | tattvaṃ kasmādenāṃ na nivārayasi | tadanu kīra udīrayāmāsa | tvaṃ tūṣṇīmāsva | yadabhidhātavyaṃ <lb> tatsvayamevaināmahaṃ vyāhariṣye | yāvatā vihaga upāyaṃ viracayati tāvatā śārikā prālapat | prabhāvati <lb> yattvaṃ vidhātumabhilaṣasi tena tvaṃ vināśamavāpsyasi | ityākarṇya tayā dūtīmukhamudaikṣi | tato dūtī <lb> rarāṇa | iyaṃ pakṣiṇī pāpinī nihantavyā yā pareṣāmasukhāya pratyūhavyūhamācarati | tadā prabhāvatī <lb> samīpamāgamya pañjarārgalamapācakāra | pāṇinā dhṛtvā śārikā vipādanīyeti manasi pravartamānāsīt | <lb> tāvatā śārikā samuḍḍīyāpalāyiṣṭa | tataḥ sarvā api babhāṣire | niragamadiyaṃ tadaiva | sādhvajaniṣṭa | <lb> tataḥ prabhāvatyā sakalavṛttānta āveditaḥ | tacchrutvā śuko 'pyakathayat | tadetadruciraṃ vyaraci | sarvadaivāhaṃ <lb> bhavatīṃ manmathāvasthābhṛśārditāṅgīmāloke | kimapi bhavatīmetadviṣayaṃ vyāhartumanvicchāmi | paraṃ pareṣāṃ <lb> manobhāvaṃ ko nāma jñātumīṣṭe | saṃsāre sādhvabhisaraṇaṃ vihāya netaratsukhaṃ bhūyasā jarījṛmbhīti | <lb> tarhīdaṃ tvayā sādhvācaritam | paramatrānyadapi vidyate | guṇaśālinīva saṃkīrṇāvaprasaṅgaprāptā uttaraṃ <lb> kartuṃ prabhavasi cettadetadbahvāyāsavibhāvyaṃ vidheyamaṅgīkuru | ityuditā prabhāvatī babhāṣe | kā nāma <lb> guṇaśālinī | kīdṛśaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ nistīrṇam | tadupavarṇayatāṃ nāma bhavān | tataḥ śuko vyāvarṇayati | <lb> prabhāvatī vayasyā pativratā paripṛcchati | itīyaṃ prathamā kathā itarāsāṃ kathānāṃ mūlapīṭhikārūpā <lb> vyāvarṇitā | iti kathākośe kathāvatāraḥ || <lb>

328,30

atha candravatī nāma nagarī | tatra bhīmaseno nāma rājā | tatra mohananāmā vaṇik | tasya bhāryā <lb> nāmato guṇaśālinī | sā rūpeṇātiśayaṃ prakarṣaṃ prāptā | tato vasudattatanayastāmīkṣitavān | tadvīkṣaṇakṣaṇa <lb> evāyaṃ manmathamathitasarvārthasārthaḥ prāvartata | tato 'pārthīkṛtetaravyāpāro dūtībhistatprārthanāṃ niravartayat | <lb> paraṃ sā norīkṛtavatī | tataḥ yadyāciṣyase tadvitariṣyāmi | tadānīṃ tayā tathā karavāṇītyaṅgīcakre | tataḥ samyaṅmuhūrtamālokya guṇa<lb>śālinīgṛhamagacchat | tayā samaṃ pratyahaṃ gariṣṭhāṃ goṣṭhīmanutiṣṭhati pratidinaṃ śrīkṛṣṇavilāsamallāyodha<lb>kandukakelipramukhāni caritāni gāyati purātanabālatvasya goṣṭhīṃ nirmimīte | itthaṃ tayormaitrī samajāyata | <pb> tata ekasmindine pūrṇāyai kimapi dātumudadhunat | tataḥ sā | yadi madīyamabhihitaṃ kariṣyasi tadānīmidamarthe <lb> tvayā mahyaṃ tathyavāk dātavyā | tato guṇaśālinī satyaṃ pratiśrutavatī | tataḥ pūrṇā nijodīrṇaṃ tayā <lb> samaṃ nirṇīya vyāharat | tvayā tasmai <pb n="329">
asāraḥ sarvataḥ sāro vācā sārasamuccayaḥ |
vācā sā calitā yena sukṛtaṃ tena hāritam ||
vācā yadyatpratijñātaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham |
tatsaṃdeho na kartavya idameva hi sāṃpratam ||

329,16

iti vimṛśya guṇaśālinī pūrṇāṃ babhāṇa | tvayābhihitaṃ tavābhipretaṃ pumāṃsamānaya | tāvatāhaṃ parasminde<lb>vatālaye nivasāmi | tataḥ pradoṣasamaye pūrṇā tamānetuṃ gatavatī janasaṃmarde taṃ nopalakṣayantī tatsā<lb>dṛśyasthagitamānasā guṇaśālinyāḥ patiṃ kare gṛhītvā tasminsaṃketaniketane samāninye | tadā tena <lb> nijadayitā tayā ca nijapatiścopalakṣitaḥ | tarhyabhidhehi prabhāvati | tathāvidhe 'sminsaṃkocasamaye ki<lb>muttaramakāri tayā | etatpurastādastāśaṅkamācakṣva paścādyāhi | prabhāvatī vimarśavatī samajani paraṃ <lb> taduttaraṃ nājñāsīt | tāvatā rātrirapyatyavartata | tataḥ śukamaprākṣīt | śuko 'pi vyāhārṣīt | sā taṃ <lb> bhartāraṃ parijñāya kacairnigṛhya capeṭābhistāḍayāmāsa | tvaṃ matpurastādastāśaṅkaṃ sadaivaṃ vyāharasi yadahaṃ <lb> bhavatīṃ vihāya nānyāṃ kāṃcana kāminīṃ jānāmīti | tavaitādṛśaṃ visadṛśaṃ caritaṃ mayā dṛśāpi <lb> spraṣṭuṃ na śakyate | tato māṃ janakamandiraṃ prāpaya | no vā rājñe āvedayiṣye tvāṃ daṇḍayiṣye | tadānīmasau <lb> mohano guṇaśālinyāścaraṇayorapatat | mamāyaṃ mahānaparādha āyāditi bhavatyā kṣantavya ityabhidhāya <lb> tāṃ samatoṣayat | tarhi prabhāvatyevaṃvidhaṃ karma kartuṃ prabhavasi cettadānīṃ bāhulyavibhāvyamidamādartavyam «||» <lb> iti prathamā kathā || 1 || <lb>

329,28

punarapi prabhāvatī vinayakandarpaniketanamupagantuṃ pakṣiṇaṃ papraccha | śuko 'bhidadhe | tvamapi yaśodāvadupā<lb>yakalpanāṃ pariśīlayasi cettato yāhi | tadākarṇya prabhāvatī kīraṃ prati tava manasi <pb> yaduditamasti tanmatpurastādastatrapaṃ bhavānvadatviti mātrābhihite 'sau cittasthitaṃ sarvamabhiprāyaṃ tasyā <lb> agre ujjagāra | yadi śaśiprabhā madaṅgasaṃgamaṅgīkurute tadānīṃ majjīvitamasti netarathā | tarhi prabhāvati <lb> tvameva pūrvamupavarṇaya | tasyābhilāṣo yaśodayā kathamapūri | yaśodā śaśiprabhāṃ kathaṃ saṃyojitavatī | <lb> etadabhidhāya yathoddiṣṭaṃ vrajatu āyurvittaṃ gṛhacchidraṃ rahasyaṃ mantramaithune |
pāyudhvaniṃ cāvamānaṃ matimānna prakāśayet ||

330,22

ityabhidhāya rahasi vaktuṃ pravṛttā | śṛṇu śaśiprabhe | pūrvamahamiyaṃ tvaṃ ca śunī ceti tisraḥ sodaryaḥ <lb> svasāra ekasya vaṇijo niketane vartāmahe | iti satyahaṃ vyabhicāraparāyaṇā nijecchayā pravṛttā | yaṃ tu <lb> pumāṃsaṃ kāmārtaṃ paśyāmi tasmai suratopabhogaṃ prayacchāmi | tvamapi yasyopari mānasamullasati tasmai <lb> surataṃ dadāsi nānyasmai prayacchasi | etāvadeva tvayi vaiguṇyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam | ārteṣu dīyate dānamiti <lb> vākyaparipālanasāmarthyopabṛṃhitaṃ mama pūrvajātismaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ jñānamudiyāya tvaṃ tu nijāgrahavyagramānasā <lb> etāvadvaiguṇyādbhogaviśeṣaṃ prāptāsi paraṃ na bhāgyasaṃpado jñānaviśeṣasya | anyā caiṣā dvayorapyāvayorjyāyasī <lb> nijena pātivratyaviśeṣeṇa nigīrṇā na kasmai cārtāya ratiṃ prayacchati | tatpātakavrātenaiṣā śunītvamanīyata | <lb> tarhi śaśiprabhe tavāpāradustarasaṃsārottaraṇākāṅkṣā jāgarti yadi tadā tvayāpyārtāya puruṣāya upabhogaḥ <lb> prayoktavyaḥ | etāvatā svata eva jñānamutpatsyate | tadānīṃ śaśiprabhā vyābhāṣata | atidustaramasāraṃ saṃsāraṃ <lb> nistarāmi tatrabhavatyā eva prasādo 'bhyudayanīyaḥ | tvamasmadīyakuladevatā | tarhi tvayā yaḥ ko 'pi <lb> kandarpakaṅkapattrakarkaśaparāhatiparigalitanikhiladhairyagāmbhīryaḥ pumāṃścakṣuṣā viṣayīkriyate sa matsaṃnidhā<lb>namānetavya ityabhidhāya daṇḍavatpraṇipatitavatī | tata itarasmindine yaśodā ākrāntaprāntadaśābhyu<lb>dayopakramaṃ nijatanayamānīya atithirabhyupagato 'stīti śaśiprabhāṃ jñāpitavatī | sā tamāgatamatithiṃ <lb> pariṇatirasanibhṛtopacāraiḥ cārutayā paricitavatī | tarhi prabhāvatyetādṛśaprapañcitopāyacāturyaṃ pari <lb> kalpasi yadi tathā vidheyaviśeṣe 'muṣminsādhanabuddhirbhava || <lb> iti dvitīyā kathā || 2 ||

331,1

punaḥ prabhāvatī vivakṣuḥ pakṣiṇaṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ lakṣīcakāra | tato 'bravītpatatrī | devi narottamanṛpativadbhavatī <lb> yadyabhiyogaṃ nirṇetuṃ pārayati tadetadādriyatām | tataḥ prabhāvatī 331,28

etasmātkāraṇānmamātrabhavāñcharaṇamāvirāsīt | tato mahīpālastamalīkavimalamānetuṃ mānuṣānanūnudat | <lb> tadanvasya nṛpatiśāsanamāyātamabhivīkṣya rājñe darśanavidheyenārpyāṇi mauktikāni ratnāni vastrāṇi <lb> cāparicitapūrvāṇi samānītavān | <lb>

naimittikaṃ tathā mitraṃ phalena phalamādiśet ||

331,33

itthaṃ rājānaṃ dṛṣṭavān | athāsau rājñā nijagade | tvametadīyāṃ saṃpadaṃ kimiti vyayīkaroṣi | tacchrutvā<lb>vitathavimalo vācaṃ prāpañcayat | saṃpattiriyaṃ madīyā | dasyurasau | tathaiva samyagvimalo vācā jijṛmbhe | <lb> evaṃ sthite sati rājño 'pi sātiśayaḥ saṃdehasamudaya udiyāya | dvāvapi sādṛśyaṃ spṛśantau na cāna<lb>yorekasya mithyātvasaṃjñānaṃ saṃpādayituṃ prabhūyate kenāpi | tarhi prabhāvati bhavatyapi vicārayatu nāma | <pb> sa tayornirṇayakathakaghaṭakakoṭiṃ kathamaṭīkṛtavān | tadākarṇya prabhāvatyapi pratibhāvijṛmbhamānavicāracā<lb>turyapariṇatimavagāhamānā tamasvinīmanīniṣatpāram | paraṃ tato na tannirṇayo buddhidarpaṇe pratiphalati | <lb> tathā prātaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ pakṣī prabhāvatīṃ pratyāha | tadā tvavanīnāyako vimalasya dve striyau samānīyāprākṣīt | <lb> bhavatyorvivāhasamaye bhavadbhartrā bhavatyoḥ kṛte bhūṣaṇāni kāni kalpitāni | tayorvyāhṛtaṃ śrutvā dvāvapi <lb> vimalau pṛthagavasthāpya pūrvoditamevāpṛcchat | taduditaṃ satyavimalavacasā tādātmyamāpanīpannam | tacchrutvā <lb> nṛpatiḥ satyavimalaṃ mānayitvā svagṛhānprati prāhaiṣīt | dhūrtavimalāya cukopa satyavimalasya saṃpattiṃ <lb> tasyaivākarot | tarhi prabhāvati nirṇayādāvitthaṃ pratibhāprabhāvaprabhutāmālambase cettadānīmatyutkṛṣṭamava<lb>gāhyametadaṅgīkāryam || <lb> iti tṛtīyā kathā || 3 || <lb>
<pb n="332">

332,10

punaḥ prabhāvatī upapatyupāntamīyuṣī pataṃgapuṃgavaṃ jagāda | so 'pi bahusutamantrīvatsamāsannamāyāsaghanaṃ <lb> kāryaṃ nistarītumīśiṣe yadi tadānīmanutiṣṭheti prabhāvatīmavādīt | sāpi kathaṃ bahusutamantrī sāyāsaṃ <lb> kāryaṃ nistīrṇastadabhidhatsveti | tataḥ so 'pi tatpraśnaṃ vaktuṃ pracakrame | somapurākhye nagare somaśarmābhidho <lb> brāhmaṇo nyavātsīt | tasyaikā kanyā | na kaścidapi tāmudvahate alakṣaṇaparicitasarvāṅgatvāt | itthaṃ sāpi <lb> vivāhasamayamatinītavatī | tatastasyāḥ pitā tāṃ saha nītvā tadvaradarśanāya pradeśaviśeṣānākrāmadbhūyasaḥ | <lb> na kaścidapi tāṃ vṛṇīte | tadanu janakasthānaṃ nāma puṭabhedamāsasāda | tatra govindo nāma vidyārthī <lb> maṭhe vidyābhyāsaṃ praguṇayati | sa somaśarmā tasmai svāṃ duhitaraṃ dadau | sa govindo bahubhirnivāryamāṇo <lb> 'pi paraṃ tāṃ paryanaiṣīt | tataḥ pitā tāmudvāhya nijaṃ nagaramājagāma | sa govindo bhāryayā saha <lb> tatrāvasthātuṃ pravavṛte | tadanu divaseṣvatikrānteṣu tayā jāyayā sa govindo 'bhyadhāyi | yadāprabhṛtyahaṃ <lb> bhavatodvāhitā tadānīmārabhya bhaktabhojyaviśeṣo na kvacidāsādyate | ātmāndhasā hīnā bubhukṣayā mriyamā<lb>ṇāsmi | tarhyuttiṣṭhata | yāmo matpiturgṛhān | tatra gatānāmasmākaṃ pitṛdarśanaṃ bhaviṣyati | śvaśuro mā<lb>nayiṣyati bhavato vasanādinā | atra tu ko 'pyupāyaviśeṣastiṣṭhati | sa gṛhamasmākamāpādayati | <lb>
yasmindeśe na saṃmāno na vṛttirna ca bāndhavāḥ |
na ca vidyāgamo nāpi dhanaṃ tatra sthitiḥ katham ||
sthānatyāgaṃ prakurvanti siṃhāḥ satpuruṣā gajāḥ |
tatraiva nidhanaṃ yānti kākāḥ kāpuruṣā ajāḥ ||

332,26

itthaṃ tayā jāyayāpyaśabdi | govindastu na tanmanasi kurvanpunarabravīt | vacanametattathyamupapannaṃ na nīti<lb>padavīṃ davīyasīṃ prakalpayati | yatra pradeśe puṃso nodyamaviśeṣaḥ kaścinna tena tatrāvasthātavyam | paraṃ <lb> śvaśurāśrayaṃ śritavatāṃ śāstre loke 'pi nitarāmavamatyatā vidyotatetarām | <lb>
uttamāḥ svadhanaiḥ khyātāḥ pitṛdravyeṇa madhyamāḥ |
adhamā mātulaiḥ khyātāḥ śvāśuraiścādhamādhamāḥ ||

332,31

govindenetthamabhihite 'pi paraṃ tayā durāgrahī gṛhītaḥ | balādeva sā taṃ nītavatī nijajanakasamī<lb>poddeśam | tato govindaḥ śatāṅgaṃ sajjīkṛtya tamadhiruhya dvāvapi niragātām | tato gacchatormārge <lb> keśavaḥ sahaprasthāyī saṃgatavān | davīyasi vartmani tena samaṃ gariṣṭhāṃ goṣṭhīmanutiṣṭhan govindastamapi <lb> śakaṭamāropitavān | tadanu mārge mūtramutsraṣṭuṃ govindaḥ syandanādavārukṣat | tato 'sau keśavastvavatī<lb>rṇamālakṣyānaḍvāhau pratodena tūrṇagatyā prāṇudat | tadanu śakaṭopari parapuruṣeṇa samaṃ saṃjātamanīṣiṇī <pb> jātā | viviktatayā dvayorapi hṛdaruṃtudaḥ sātiśayaḥ kaścana premā prāvardhiṣṭa | tadanusārī govindo <lb> 'pi śakaṭamāṭīkate smākapaṭasnehaḥ śakaṭamāroḍhuṃ prāvartiṣṭa | tato govindaḥ keśavenolluṭhya parataḥ pari<lb>cikṣipe | anuyāsyasi yadi tadānīṃ sādhutayā śikṣayiṣyāmi | madīyā jāyā madīyaḥ śakaṭaḥ | na <lb> niścinomi tvāṃ kutastanaṃ pāripanthikam | kasmācchakaṭamārurukṣasi | itthaṃ karuṇayā śakaṭamāropitaḥ <lb> keśavaścaṇḍālacaṇḍatāmamaṇḍayat | itthaṃ tayorvivadamānayoḥ govindastu naradevamāvedayat | nṛpasamakṣaṃ <lb> vyavahāro 'jāyatobhayorapi | eko vakti madīyeyamiti | itaro 'pi tathaiva | tatratyāḥ sabhāsadaḥ striyaṃ <lb> tāmaprākṣuḥ | kasya tvaṃ jāyeti | tayā saṃjātanūtanamaitro dhūrta eva bhartṛtvena parigṛhītaḥ | tāṃ dṛṣṭvā go<lb>vindo jagāda | pāpametadabhilāṣamanīṣayā vyavaharamāṇā vartate | tadanu pṛthvīpraśāstā pradhāninaṃ babhāṣe | <lb> tvayā sa vivādo nirṇetavyaḥ | tarhi prabhāvati tvameva pratibhānavatī bhūtvaitaduttaraṃ vāvadīhi | kenopāyena <lb> vivādastayoratruṭyat | tataḥ prabhāvatī cintāvatī babhūva paraṃ na hṛdayasaṃdehamapanudatī | tataḥ pṛṣṭvā śukaṃ <lb> taduttaradānotsukaṃ cakāra | tadānīmamātyastāṃ striyamavocat | bhavantau saṃvasanānniragātām | tarhyasyāṃ <lb> triyāmāyāṃ kimabhyavahāri | tathā caitadeva govindakeśavau ca praśnīkṛtavān | strīvyāhṛtena govindagaditaṃ <lb> saṃgatamabadhnāt | tataḥ keśavamavamatya govindāya tāṃ striyaṃ vitatāra | prabhāvati prabhāvavaibhavametādṛśaṃ <lb> bhāvayasi cettadānīmetadādaraṇīyam || <lb> iti caturthī kathā || 4 || <lb>
<pb n="333">

333,16

punarapi yāminīmukhe vinayakandarpasamīpamiyāsuḥ prabhāvatī prālapaditi pakṣiṇam | so 'pi svopari <lb> paryāptaṃ tamaparādhamaparasyopari kṣeptuṃ bālasarasvatīvadbuddhivaibhavena prabhavasi cettadānīṃ saṃjīvatāmiti <lb> prājalpat | prabhāvatyapi bālasarasvatyāścaturacaritamavabubhutsuḥ kīraṃ gīrbhirudīrayat | so 'pi caritaṃ <lb> tatprabhāvatīmavajigamiṣurvācaṃ prāpañcayat | ākarṇayatu kumudanandinī samuddyotayantyadyatanā mīnāḥ | tatkimiti na bhavatībhirabhyavahṛ<lb>tiviṣayatāmāpadyante | tatastayāpyarāṇi | kimiti prabhubhirasamaṃjasamabhidhīyate | atitīvrasatīvrataparaprakarṣa<lb>prabhāvapradaṃ <lb> rājā ca tānmatsyahāsakāraṇamaprākṣīt | tatastadanimeṣahasitaṃ na ko 'pi vipaścidvivektuṃ śaknoti | tadanu <pb> te maunamevālalambire | bhūpo 'pi sarvebhyo vidvadbhyo 'krudhyat | etāvantaḥ sarve <pb n="334">
kāke śaucaṃ dyūtakāre ca satyaṃ sarpe kṣāntiḥ strīṣu kāmopaśāntiḥ |
klībe dhairyaṃ madyape tattvacintā rājño mitraṃ kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā ||

334,6

tatastaiḥ sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya rājā vijñaptaḥ | deva dinapañcakamasmabhyametadvicāraparicāraṇāya dātavyam | pakṣabhi<lb>rahobhirmatsyahāsasya hetuṃ vyāhariṣyāmahe | dharitrīśvaro 'pi tattadudīritamurarīkaroti sma | tataḥ saṃsarga<lb>visarge sarve 'pi svānsvāngṛhānagaman | mantrī ca nijāgāramāgatya ugracintāgrahagrasta upāvikṣat | tadanu <lb> tatkanyā bālasarasvatī tadantikamāgatya janakaṃ jagāda | tāta cintāsaṃtānanitāntasvāntānākalayāmi <lb> kimu tatrabhavataḥ | tarhi tatkāraṇaṃ mamāpi vyāharaṇīyam | tathokte tu tayā amātyo 'pi svāpatya <lb> pratyāha | tvaṃ bālikā | kimetayā cintayā te | tvayā dīvyantyā sukhenāvasthātavyam | tacchrutvā sāpi <lb> prāsūta sarasvatīm | kimiti bhavanta evamabhāṣiṣata | <lb>
yuktiyuktamupādeyaṃ vacanaṃ bālakādapi |
anyattṛṇamiva tyājyaṃ vyuktaṃ pañcamajanmanā ||

334,15

tatastena tatkāraṇamupavarṇitam | tanniśamya bālasarasvatī babhāṇa | tāta etāvataiva kimiti cintāsaṃtā<lb>naprakarṣamātanoti | imaṃ hetumahameva vyāhariṣye | tadānīṃ rājā vijñaptaḥ | deva matsyasya hāsahetuṃ matkanyakā <lb> vyāhariṣyati | tadākarṇya tadānīmeva nṛpatirapi tāmānaya iti rājāpyāgatya sabhāmabhāsayat | bā<lb>lasarasvatyā āsikāmupababandha | tāmaprākṣītkṣatriyeśvaraḥ | tayāpi tataḥ pratīyate sma | deva tvaṃ sarvajñaḥ <lb> sakalakalākalāpakuśalaḥ | tarhyetasyārthasya praṣṭavye nānyaḥ samucitaucityamatyantamābadhnāti | <lb>
aśvaplutaṃ vāsavagarjitaṃ ca avarṣaṇaṃ cāpyativarṣaṇaṃ ca |
strīṇāṃ ca cittaṃ puruṣasya bhāgyaṃ devo na jānāti kuto manuṣyaḥ ||

334,22

ityetādṛśaṃ strīṇāṃ caritaṃ devānāmapi vijñānasya na viṣayībhavati | māyāśatamapyasti yo na tāsāṃ <lb> cittaṃ kiṃcidapi kalayati | <lb>
gītārtho mānavo dharmaḥ tava śīlaṃ varānane |
strīśīlaṃ vaiṣṇavī māyā vismayāya muhurmuhuḥ ||

334,26

tvayaivedaṃ cāru vicāraṇīyam | nānyaḥ praśnārhaḥ | kaḥ samīhate | itthaṃ pāpamatyāgrahaparigrahaṃ gṛhṇīṣe | <lb> tarhi ślokamekamahaṃ gṛṇāmi | tasyārthavicāramācara | kṛte 'pi vicāre yadyabhiprāyaṃ na pariśīlayasi <lb> tadānīmahamāvedayiṣyāmi | <lb>
rājñī na ca spṛśatyasmānpakvānapi mahāsatī |
puruṣākhyāṃstato rājanhāsitā sma iti dhruvam ||

334,31

ślokamimaṃ pūrvaṃ caturacetasā vicāraya | ityabhidhāya bālasarasvatī nijāgāramāgamat | <lb> iti pañcamī kathā || 5 || <lb>

334,33

punarapi nṛpatirbālasarasvatīmāhūtavān | timipramodanidānamapṛcchat | taṃ praśnamāśritya sāpi viśvaṃbha<lb>reśvaramaśrāvayat | etatkāraṇādbhavato 'nutāpa udeṣyati | maṇḍakāgamanasyānuyogato vaṇijo jāyāyā <pb> ajāyata | tavāpi tādṛkprakāraḥ prāduṣkariṣyate | tadā rājāpi tathā pṛṣṭavānmaṇḍakāgamanacaritam | <lb> bālasarasvatyādadhvāna | jayantyāṃ nagaryāṃ sumatināmadheyo vipaṇirnyavātsīt | tasya sali<lb>laviharalaharīpoplavamānasamantakakubhaṃ prāvṛḍmāyāntamabhivīkṣya saṃnihitagaṇeśaprāsādamāsādya utthi<lb>tavān | tatra ca gaṇeśābhimukhaṃ nirahlādayat | kāṣṭhaghaṭitāṃ gaṇeśamūrtiṃ adrākṣīt | tiṣṭhāmaḥ | kutastānānayatīti na vidāṃkaravai | tadanu mandodarī giramu<lb>dīrayāmāsa | tarhi tvayā nijapatiriti praṣṭavyaḥ | kasmātpradeśādetānānayanti bhavanto maṇḍakāniti | <lb> vāṇīṃ praguṇīcakāra | <lb> kimanena vṛthāgrahaparigrahavilasanena cikīrṣitaṃ bhavatyā | etadarthāvagamātsamīhitasiddhirapi kā nāma | <lb> yadā parameśvaraḥ prasīdati tadā sarvamapyapekṣaṇīyamanāyāsasamarthitamarthāpayati | <lb>
<pb n="335">
arirmitraṃ viṣaṃ pathyaṃ adharmī dharmatāṃ vrajet |
anukūle jagannāthe viparīte viparyayaḥ ||

335,34

tarhi tvameva tajjijñāsitasya māgrahaṃ parigṛhāṇa | tūṣṇīmāpnuhi | tena nyakkṛtā sā maunāvalambanaparāyaṇā <lb> tasthau | tataḥ prātarutthitā sā punarapi mandodaryā samudairi | aho tvayā maṇḍakasamāgamakāraṇamavagacchāmi <lb> na vā kim | tadā tadākarṇya padminī yāminīsamatītaṃ caritaṃ vyāhṛtavatī | tanniśamya mandodarī <lb> nijodarodgāraṃ girāṃ vyāhāraṃ vyaracayat | yasya jñīpsetsthitaṃ yadmatireva na spṛśati tasya dayitātvaṃ <pb> vyarthaṃjīvitā bharturbhāryā vyavahāraparihāryā sā | jājvalītu jīvitaṃ bhavatyā iti | narākūtaprabhāmāsā<lb>dayāmyāpṛcchya bhavatyai vyāhariṣyāmītyavādīt | tato vibhāvaryāṃ sā bhartāramanvayuṅkta | tadākarṇanāttatpatiḥ <lb> pratyavadat | pāpiṣṭhe patīnāṃ sukhapoṣaṇaploṣaṇāya kimityuditatvarāsi | tvaṃ maunamavalambasva | tena tathā<lb>bhihite 'pi sāgrahaṃ parijagrāha | maṇḍakāgamanakāraṇamidamevākarṇayasi yadi tadānīṃ jīvāmi netarathā | <lb> iti tadāgrahagrahaparigṛhītagalo 'sau vṛttāntamāśrāvayāmāsa tām | tayā ca prativeśinyai prājalpi | <lb> sā ca tathā kārayiṣurmandodarī kuṭhāraskandhaṃ vidhāya gaṇeśamūrtigatadārubhedanāya gaṇeśaprāsādaṃ prati <lb> prāṇaiṣītprāṇanātham | etāvatā tubhyamapi vratamaṇḍakānvitariṣyati pratidinaṃ paśupatinandanaḥ | niśamyetthaṃ <lb> so 'pi sumatisamanvito vināyakanikāyyamāseditavān | tadanu lambodaro 'pi tayorvivatsubuddhi<lb>nibandhanamabhiprāyamavabudhyālambakabodhyaiḥ pāśairabadhnāt | alakṣitaprahārāstu śarīrasyoparyuparyāpatanti | evaṃ <lb> jīvitavyanirapekṣaspṛhau kṛtvā vighnanāśanaḥ sumatimavādīt | are duṣṭamate nivārito 'bhūrmayā pūrvaṃ <lb> na kasyāpi purastādvyāhartavyamiti tatkasmādbhavānabhyadhāt | niśamyeti gaṇeśamuvāca | kiṃ nāma tvāmahaṃ <lb> vyāvacam | pūrvajanmadurantaduritaparipākāt | tarhi bhūmahendra vicārayatastavāpītthaṃ bhavati || <lb> iti ṣaṣṭhī kathā || 6 || <lb>

336,14

punaḥ prabhāte rājavṛndasamabhyarcitaśāsano vikramādityo bālasarasvatīmānāyya visārihasitakāraṇa<lb>maprākṣīt | sāpyūce | deva keśavasya yogadaṇḍena yathābhūttathā te bhaviṣyati | keśavavṛttāntaṃ 337,12

nṛpaśca bālasarasvatīṃ nijaparicaravartinīṃ vidhāya visārahāsyapraśnamanuyuyukṣū raṇati sma | bālasarasvati <lb> pūrvapraśnasyārthaṃ vāggrathanenottarayatarām | ityavagatyāmātyasutā vyāyacchadvācam | tadagnijanitasaṃmardasamākrandanamadhye <lb> 'hamalakṣitaprakāraṃ tadupakaṇṭhamakuṇṭhitapracārā maṇḍayiṣyāmi nijāvasthāraṇaraṇakatā tatsaṃnidhisaṃgatā<lb>ṅgasāndrānandalaharī 337,31

tato dvitīye dine medinīnāthaḥ padyārthasyāvindako bālasarasvatīmābhāṣyāsmadīyaṃ hṛdayaṃ yathārthā<lb>vedanena viśadasaṃvidāpādayeti nivedite viditavedyā sāpi taṃ jagāda | rājannadasīye 'bhidheye <lb> raṇabāhubala ityātmanaḥ saṃjñāṃ purastātprācīkaśat | tatra rājā tasyālīke viśālaṃ karavālarājaprahā<lb>ramālakṣya sādhīyānprathanaprathitapragalbho 'yaṃ padātiḥ 338,23

tataśca bhūyo bālasarasvatīṃ svopāntakalitoddeśāṃ vidhāyānimiṣahasitanidānapraśnopakramāya pragalbhāṃ <lb> cakre | bālasarasvatī tacchrutvoditavatī | deva bahvāgrahānugrahasaraṇena kasmādetatpipṛcchiṣasi | niṣiddho 'pi <lb> nāgrahaṃ jihāsasi | yathā mātulaḥ paścātpariśramaṃ mahāntamavāptavānsa prakārastvayi bhaviṣyati | tatasta<lb>davabubhutsuḥ kiṃ taccaritamiti pratyāha pārthivaḥ pradhānaputrīm | sāpi tadākhyānena pṛthivīprabhuṃ cāca<lb>ritārthayat | yathā śṛṇu bhūpate | pratiṣṭhānanāmadheyaṃ nagaram | tatraikasya mālikasya vāṭikā | tatrātibahūni <lb> vālukaphalānyajāyanta | tatastamasvinyāmāgatya jambuka eko vāṭīmadhyagatāni phalāni pratyahamabhakṣayat | <lb> mālikastu pratiniśaṃ rakṣaṇāya prayatate paraṃ nāsāvāsādyate | ekadā tu phalāni pradarśya paraṃ sauhityamā<lb>tmānamātanvānaḥ tṛṣāparigato jalaṃ pātuṃ gaṅgāmadhyagacchat | jalamāpīya taraṃgiṇyāstīre kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā<lb>tīvadurbalaṃ rajakasya gardabhaṃ tṛṇāni carantaṃ lakṣīcakāra | tasyāsthiśeṣāṇyaṅgāni vīkṣya mṛgadhūrto 'vā<lb>dīt | mātula bhavantaḥ kimiti durbaladehāḥ | śrutvetthaṃ gardabho 'pi babhāṣe | kiṃ vacmi bhāgineya | madīyaḥ <lb> putro nirṇejako 'harniśaṃ karuṇāṃ niruṇaddhi | asādhāraṇaṃ sicayanicayaṃ parikṣipati mamopari | na <lb> rājāvāhāraṃ ca prayacchati | divase tvetāndūrvāṅkurānkavalīkaravai | etāvatā bubhukṣayā stimitamānasa <lb> eva tiṣṭhāmi | kāraṇādetasmādahaṃ durbalakale≤b≥«v»araḥ | nānyaḥ kaścana mamopadravasaṃmardī vartate | <lb>
kṣudhāsamaṃ nāsti śarīrapīḍanaṃ cintāsamaṃ nāsti śarīraśoṣaṇam |
vidyāsamaṃ nāsti śarīrabhūṣaṇaṃ kṣamāsamaṃ nāsti śarīrarakṣaṇam ||

339,3

tarhi bhāgineya kutrāpyasmākamāhārāvāptirbhaviṣyati tathā kriyatāṃ nāma | tataḥ kroṣṭā vyācaṣṭa | ahaṃ <lb> tubhyamāhāraṃ saṃpādayiṣyāmi | paraṃ tavodaramāpūrṇaṃ cedetāvatā tvaṃ na huṃkāradhvanimudgiriṣyasi | tāvatā <lb> dhvanyupādarśitasmṛtipatho 'sāvāgatya māmapi laguḍaistāḍayiṣyati tvamapi prahāraśatavidalitadehaḥ śramaṃ <lb> bhūyaḥ samupeṣyasi | tataḥ prasabhaṃ saṃbabhāṣe rāsabhaḥ | pūrṇe 'pi mamodare nāhaṃ huṃkṛtidhvanimādarīdarīmi | <lb> amuṣminviṣaye bhāṣeyaṃ madīyā | ityukte pracaṇḍacaṇḍimāpāṇḍityākāṇḍoddaṇḍatāṇḍavitāḍambaraḥ pheruṇḍī <lb> gardabhasaṃbhāvitapaścādbhāgaḥ vālukāvāṭīnikaṭabhuvamaṭīkaroti sma | tadanu pradoṣasamaye tamālamālinyamā<lb>tanvati jagati tatra vāṭikāyāmantaḥ praviśya vālukāphalānyabhyavajahratuḥ | gardabhastu vālukāṃ bhuktvā <lb> vālukālatāmunmūlayati sma | itthaṃ gardabhodaraṃ paryapūri | etāvatā huṃkāraṇadhvanirapi praroditi | tatra <lb> rakṣaṇamuddiśya māliko babhrāmyamāṇo 'bhūt | sa tvaritagatirdhvanyupalakṣitaṃ sthānamājagmivān | tāvatā <lb> palāyya mṛgavañcako manaḥsamīhitaṃ pradeśamājagmivān | sa tu gardabho nigṛhya laguḍaprahāraiḥ śataśo dalitā<lb>khilāṅgabandhāsthisaṃcayaḥ kṛtaḥ | nirjīva iti matvā parityaktaḥ | gale ca sthūlakāṣṭhapariluptakāyaṃ tu kākaraṇaṃ <lb> prayojitavān | mahatā duḥkhena vadankliśyanparamapīḍāmanubhavanbhagnacaraṇapāṇiḥ śanairnirayāsīt | kaṇṭhaca<lb>lanamadhikṣeptuṃ bhavati yatra tatra kāṣṭhabandhanena ca mṛtakalpo 'gacchat | pathi kroṣṭāraṃ dṛṣṭavān | tena cā<lb>bhyadhāyi | madīyamabhihitaṃ na kariṣyasi udare pūrṇe tvaṃ gānameva pragalbhase | tarhi gītasyaitādṛśaṃ phalaṃ <lb> hastaprāptaṃ tavājāyata yatnavataḥ | <lb>
māma gītaṃ na gātavyamityākṣipto mayā bahu |
apūrvo 'yaṃ maṇiḥ kaṇṭhe tava kiṃ gītikalpitam ||

339,20

bhavānpaścāttāpaṃ kartuṃ pravavṛte | ahaṃ tava niṣedhaṃ nāṅgīkṛtavān | tatastasyaitādṛśaṃ phalaṃ prāpto 'smi | <lb> tarhi rājendra tathātvamudeṣyati | tvametatpraśnātkalpitodyogaḥ sukhamāsādaya | ślokasyārthavicāramaticāturyeṇa <lb> paricintaya | ityabhidhāya bālasarasvatī nijamandiramāgatavatī || <lb> iti daśamī kathā || 10 || <lb>

339,24

punaḥ prabhāvatī vinayakandarpasya saṃketasadanamīpsantī kīramujjarīgariti sma | tataḥ so 'pi vacaḥ <lb> prayuyuje | ślokasyārthamabhidhehi devi | sā ca tamevāpṛcchat | tataḥ pakṣī vācā lakṣīcakāra | aharārambhe <lb> bālasarasvatīṃ mahīnātho matsyahāsasyāvirbhāvaprathamāṅkuraṃ jñīpsati sma | sā ca rājānaṃ pratyavadat | <lb> narendra enamatiśayaṃ kasmādādarīdarīṣi | avidyamānānnaiṣaṇāviśeṣānālakṣayanti vicakṣaṇāḥ | anyadīyo <lb> vyāpāro yadyanyena sisādhayiṣyate tadānīmaśrāntaṃ śramāśraya eva viśrāmyate | gardabhasyaikasyāvidheyavidhā<lb>nabuddheranutāpakhedaścāsādayāmiyāya | tathā tavāpi bhobhaviṣyati | tato medinīvinodastāṃ taṃ vṛttā<lb>ntamaprākṣītsāpyavādīt | śṛṇu śravaṇīyaguṇāgragaṇya | kalyāṇasaṃjñe nagare śvāparatyāhvo rajako dvitīyāṃ <lb> gṛhiṇīṃ svāṃ gṛhiṇītvena parigṛhītavān | tadāvartane niśīthinyāṃ pāripanthiko vivāhavihārapariśrā<lb>ntānakhilasadmasasāsannajanānnidrāvidrāvitamānasavilāsānālakṣya tadveśmamadhye praviveśa | tadā dvāri <lb> sthitibhājaṃ bhaṣakaṃ gardabho dadarśa | tena ca bhaṣako babhāṣe | are śvanko api corastu khātaṃ pradāya <lb> veśmāntaḥ pravivikṣurjāgarti | ayaṃ ca sarvamapi gṛhāntaḥsthitavastujātaṃ gṛhītvā gamiṣyati | tarhi tvaṃ nijaṃ <lb> vyāpāraṃ kimiti parijihīrṣasi | tacchrutvā śvā vacaḥ saṃcaskāra | na kadācanāyaṃ madīyāṃ sukhaduḥkhā<lb>dicintāṃ vicārayati | tadāhaṃ bubhukṣita eva tiṣṭhāmi | na kadāpyannaṃ mahyaṃ prayacchati | sarvasvanāśaścedasya <pb> bhaviṣyati tadānīṃ mama kācana kṣatirna jāghaṭīti | yasya prabhoḥ parisare dānamānamatīva nopapadyate <lb> tasya kāryaviṣaye sevako yadi svakāyakleśavāsanākadarthita upekṣālakṣitavailakṣaṇyapakṣakṣuṇṇatayā pari<lb>śīlayati tadānīṃ tasya pātakapratīpapātārdhī 'nusaṃpadyate | tathā cānucaro yadyātmanaḥ sādhīyasīṃ prasā<lb>dhanāmanusaṃdadhāti āviṣkāramāpādayanmaraṇamapyaṅgīkariṣṇuḥ svaśarīraṃ praharajharjharitaṃ vidhāya sevāṃ <lb> vidhatte | tathāvidhaṃ bhṛtyaṃ svāmī yadi dānamānādinā mānayati tadānīṃ tasminnadhamavarṇāvarṇavarṇanā<lb>vṛttimābadhnāti | tarhyetasya prabhormama ka upayogaḥ | nagnīkṛtaścettadānīṃ na kimapi hīyate | <lb>
<pb n="340">
tyajetsvāminamatyugraṃ atyugraṃ kṛpaṇaṃ tyajet |
tyajecca kṛpaṇaṃ bhūpamamitraṃ māyinaṃ tyajen ||

340,9

bhaṣakeṇetthaṃ bhāṣitaṃ niśamya gardabho 'bhyadhāt | yadi na bhāṣasi tvaṃ tadānīmahaṃ huṃkaromi | tenāyamapi <lb> sāvadhāno bhaviṣyati | ityāśrāvya śvā vācamaśiśriyat | śvānaḥ vyaktaṃ dhvananti tato janāḥ sāvadhānāḥ <lb> saṃbhavanti | udyamo 'yamasmadīyaḥ | na bhavādṛśāṃ vilasitamatastvaṃ maunamavalambasva | iti vārito 'pi <lb> śunā gardabhastadīyaṃ mataṃ nānumanute sma | tadā gardabho 'tiparuṣaṃ jagarda | tacchabdakārkaśyākarṇanasamayasa<lb>manantaramevākarṇayatāṃ karṇāni bādhiryaṃ śirāṃsi ca paramāmārtimāpedire | paraṃ gardabho nirṇejakasya <lb> mūrdhna upari gardanamaśeṣayati | tadā rajako vyājahāra | pāpajātiścaṇḍālo 'yaṃ nidropadravaṃ vidadhāti <lb> dine tu vyāpārabhāraparicaraṇasāmagryā pariśrāmyāmi | saṃprati asmānnidrāvayati gardanena gardabhaḥ | <lb> tarhyayaṃ svāmighātakaḥ | etasya pracaṇḍalaguḍena doṣa utpatsyate 'smākamityabhidhāya rajaka udasthāt | <lb> dvāridattāmargalāṃ gṛhītvā hastābhyāmubhābhyāṃ dhṛtvā yathābalaṃ trikasyopari tridhā samabhihāreṇa tama<lb>tāḍayat | pramīta iti matvā prahāraprayogaṃ paryahārṣīt | tadānīṃ sa rāsabhaḥ subhāṣitamekamabhāṣata | <lb>
parādhikārajāṃ carcāṃ yaḥ karoti narādhamaḥ |
sa nūnaṃ sīdati kṣipraṃ rajakādgardabho yathā ||

340,21

tarhi bhūpāla tvametaṃ praśnaṃ mā kṛthāḥ | āgrahaṃ jahīhi | tadākarṇanāttava śramo bhaviṣyati | ityudīrya <lb> bālasarasvatī svakīyaṃ veśma samāsadat || <lb> ityekādaśī kathā || 11 || <lb>

340,24

punarapyavanīnātho visārahāsarasapīyūṣasārajñīpsārasānusāro bālasarasvatīṃ samāhūya vācaṃ pracikṣepa | <lb> tanniśamya sāpyavādīt | mahīmahendra tvametadāviṣkaraṇātiśayaṃ jahīhi | etadācaraṇena eko bhujago <lb> 'vasanna āsīt | tathā tvamapi bhaviṣyasi | tadanu tadvṛttāntaprāduṣkāraṃ kuruṣvetyabhiyuktā bālasarasvatī <lb> nṛpatimajñāpayattadvṛttāntam | ākarṇaya narendra | kautukamekaṃ vāvacmi | vismayasmitaṃ rasaviyuktaṃ vā bhavatu <lb> paraṃ tatrāvadhānaṃ kartavyam | etāvatā vacanaprayoktṝṇāṃ manaḥ samādhānamudrāmudritaṃ bhavati | tathā sati <lb> tatra rasābhivyaktirvikasvaravihāravatī parilasati | anyacca | prabhūṇāṃ lakṣaṇametat | yatsarvāsvapi kalāsu <lb> kalāvilāsavivecakaṃ tattatkalāparikalitāṅgaparīkṣābhivīkṣaṇamanubhūyate | yadi tasminkalāsu śikṣitatvaṃ <lb> jāgarti tasminnādaraṃ vidhāya kalā paricitavyā no cetkimapi tasmai vitīrya yathāgatagamanāyānujñā <lb> dātavyā | tadānīmeva kīrtiḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ paramāṃ sphūrtiṃ dīpayati | pūrvaṃ virāṭopavartane kasmiṃścitsamaye <lb> prāvṛḍākālikī prādurāsīt | tatsaṃgāttāḥ sarvā api taraṃgiṇyo bahulajalaparamapūraṇe kūlaṃkaṣākhyā<lb>viśeṣamātmanaḥ kṛtārthīkurvanti sma | tatpūramadhye pravahannahireko gamanamurarīkṛtavān | tasyātitarāṃ pariśrā<lb>ntasya śiraḥpradeśa eva kevalo jalabahirbhūtaḥ prakāśate | itaratsarvaṃ śarīraṃ jale magnam | tatraiko maṇḍūka <lb> āgatya phaṇāyā uparyāsedivān | sarpastūṣṇīmāsta | na tāvatī śaktistasmiṃstadānīmavasthānaṃ paricinoti <pb> sma | tato 'sau tenaiva chandena gantuṃ prāvartata | itthaṃ kūlaṃkaṣākūle nivasanbharadvājaḥ pakṣī bhekākrāntaśirodeśaṃ <lb> sarpamālokyāhāsīt | pakṣihāsamabhivīkṣya darvīkaro giraṃ kirati sma | bharadvāja kasmādahasi tvayā | <lb> tataḥ so 'pyavadat | viparītanirīkṣaṇena mama hāsyāvirbhāvaḥ samajāyata | tatkiṃnāma vaiparītyamityukte <lb> pakṣī vicikṣepa vācam | bhavatāṃ kuṇḍalināmāhārabhūtā bhekāḥ | sa cedbhavanmūrdhānamāruhyopaviśati tadā <lb> hāsyasamunmiṣadāsyaṃ bobhavīti | tataḥ sarpa uvāca | <lb>
<pb n="341">
kiṃ hasasi bharadvāja sarpī darduravāhanaḥ |
kālacchandena varteta ghṛtāndho brāhmaṇo yathā ||

341,8

tato bharadvājo bibharāṃbabhūva bhāratīm | ghṛtāndhāgrajanurudantamudīrayatāṃ bhavāniti niśamya patagoktāṃ <lb> vācaṃ vyañjayat | brahmapuranāmnyagrahāre kṣemaṃkaro brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya bhāryā aticalācalā | sa tu parilasadasa<lb>makusumaśarāsāraprahāravyathāpariniṣṭhitadhairyaḥ sarvasvasaṃsārasārabhūtapañcabāṇopāsanasāmastyopadeśikakaṭā<lb>kṣalakṣyābhivyaktānandasamudayaparimṛditāśeṣakleśasthirīkṛtahṛdayācidudayollāso 'ṅkhitabahirabahiravastu<lb>vastuvinyastāntarakalanākalapañcamaprapañcavipañcitavipañcīparivādinīdhyānanimīlitanayano 'vaninīṣati sma <lb> dināni | sa tu tasyāḥ patiḥ na tasyai surataṃ vitarati | adyāmāvāsyā vyatīpāto vaidhṛtāḥ paurṇamāsī <lb> daśamyekādaśyaṣṭamī yugādirmanvādiḥ saṃkrāntiścaturdaśī ityādiparvaviśeṣasañjanena māsasya madhye saṃbhoge <lb> viśeṣataḥ prasaṅgo na jāghaṭīti | itthaṃ tasyā manmathopabhogavāsanā na kadāpyāpūryate | iti sati kadācana <lb> tayā svacetasā vyavacintitam | saṃsāre viṣayopabhogasāre samutpannayā mayā na kadācidapi viṣayā<lb>nuśīlanasukhamāsvāditam | madīyaṃ yauvanamanupabhuktāmandaviṣayarasāsvādaṃ vṛthaiva pratidinaṃ gacchati | tadanu <lb> vegitagatyā vārddhakyamudeṣyati | <lb>
adhvā jarā manuṣyāṇāmanadhvā vājināṃ jarā |
asaṃgamo jarā strīṇāmaśvānāṃ maithunaṃ jarā ||

341,21

ityabhidhāya sā vyabhicārācaraṇāya pravavṛte | tataḥ kiyatānehasā sa tatpatirbrāhmaṇo 'pyajñāsīt | paraṃ <lb> maunamavalambanena tiṣṭhati | nāṅgīkartuṃ prabhavati puṃsā yatkimapi kāryaṃ nijāvalokanā<lb>taṅkāvalokanāparyāptāvaśeṣanīyaḥ | netre eva tasya rūpagrahanigrahe vidhātavye | tataḥ sa devatādambho babhāṇa | <lb> ahaṃ māyeriṇī devatā tathā kariṣyāmi yathā tasya nayane madīyanetre tu gate | ahamandhaḥ saṃjātaḥ | tvamanadhigatāvadhikriyāmājanmano madīyopāsanaṃ <lb> cikīrṣasi pariśrāmyasi | tarhi mama haste musalamekamarpaya | tathāhaṃ tatparikalpitavartmā tiṣṭhati | tau dvāvapi sukhena <lb> nivasataḥ | etāvatā tenopapatinā pratidinamantarāgamyate | upaveśite sati eteṣāṃ caraṇau niścitya <lb> gṛhāntarākārayatāt | itīdṛśamādaraviśeṣaṃ vyadhāt | tato 'sau gadāparvākhyānamākhyātumupacakrame | tato <lb> ghṛtāndho 'bhyadhāt | gadāparvākhyānamuhūrtamākārayiṣye | pratyahamiha bhavadbhiḥ sadāyātavyam | bhavatāmahaṃ <lb> gadāparvākhyākharvagarvaparvabadhira itthaṃ durvahamudrānirvāhavibhedakaṃ sarvasuraparvapratiparvacarvitanirvitathanirvā<lb>sanoditvarasukṛtasarvasvaṃ varivasitaśarvakṛpākaṭākṣacchaṭākṣiprasādābhivyañjakaṃ bhavaccittalayaviśeṣasaṃpoṣaka<lb>sarvodyogenāṅgeṣu samāpayiṣye | ityavagantavyam | anena prakāreṇa sa upapatiḥ pratidinaṃ dvijottamāttasmā<lb>dgadāparvapurāṇaṃ śṛṇoti | ghṛtāndhaśca taṃ prati vyabhicāriṇyā api kapālamekaghātena śakalīkṛtavān | itthamasau ghṛtāndho 'grajanmā svavairamasādhayat | <lb> tadbhujagastu kālakavalitakalevaraḥ | tarhi mahīnātha tvamāgrahaṃ jahīhi | padyasyaivārthamāmṛśa | ityupadiśya <lb> pradhānanandinyapi yathāgatamagāt || <lb> iti dvādaśī kathā || 12 || <lb>

343,6

tadanu dinanāthasyodaye avaniramaṇo 'mātyatanūjāmānāyya jalacarahasitanidānajñīpsayā aprākṣīt | <lb> tadāśrutya śāpādbiḍaujasa apsarā rājanandinī samajāyata | tadanveko janastadabhyagramāgatavānsa tu sthāsyati | <lb> tava mṛtaśarīrasyārātparicaryāpare dve striyau sthāsyataḥ | āgatāya pūrvapuruṣāya tava nirjīvakalevaravṛttā<lb>ntāvedanaṃ vidhāsyato vanite te | tatastvaṃ tu tasya puruṣasya kaścidāsīt | sa taccaritaṃ bubhutsuḥ sakalaṃ bhūmaṇḍalaṃ babhrāma | <lb> tataḥ kollāpuraṃ kṣetramāsādya śrīmahālakṣmīsthāne 'nvatiṣṭhat | devatā prasādya varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti vyājahāra | <lb> tato 'sau | viśālapurī kā | sā kasminbhūmibhāge 'vasthitimādadhāti | tannagaraṃ mayā cakṣurviṣayīkartavyam | <lb> tathā prasīdatu bhavatī | ityākarṇya śrīmahālakṣmīstasmai viśālapurīdarśanāya prādātpāduke | ete 344,19

punarapi rājñā bālasarasvatī samāhūtā | matsyahāsyakāraṇamaprākṣīt | tacchrutvā sāpi sasarja giram | <lb> etadākarṇanāddharādhīśa tavāpi tathā bhaviṣyati yathaikasyāḥ puṃścalyā jāro 'pi nājāyata tathā <lb> sukhenaiva nivasāmaḥ | tvaṃ nijagṛhādhiṣṭhātrī sukhaviśeṣopabhogarasikā parilasasi | ahamapyātmano mandire <lb> sukhaparavaśaḥ paramasaṃtoṣasamāsāditapoṣastiṣṭhāmi | yadāvayormanmathenāvasthopanīpadyate tadānīṃ tadapi <lb> vidheyamanubobhavāmaḥ | iti vartamānaṃ sukharasābhivyañjakasamayamapahāya kimanyatra gantavyamiti abhihitā <lb> tena sāpyagadat | yadi māṃ na <lb> gṛhītvānyatra nirbādhabhogaviśeṣānubhavo 'bhyasyate | paramahametattvāṃ vaktuṃ bibhemi | tarhi tvaṃ madīyacittā<lb>ntargatamabhiprāyamavagatya vyāhārṣīḥ | adya tvaṃ sāyaṃtanasamaye mama yāminīprathamapraharasamaye nirgamiṣyāmi | adyatano gamanavidhau muhūrtayogo 'pi sādhakatamo <lb> 'sti | iti saṃketaṃ tasyai dattavān | tadanu rātrau dvāvapi niragātām | tataḥ kasmiṃścitpradeśe tāṃ gṛhītvā <lb> tāṃ tatra parityajya tadīyaṃ sakalamapi dhanamapāhārṣīt | tataḥ sā paramanutāpamāpatat | mayābhīkṣṇamasā<lb>dhvakāri | siddho 'pi nijaḥ kaumāraḥ parityaktaḥ | anyacca sa pāpiṣṭhatama 345,8

athānyasmindine bālasarasvatīmānāyyānimiṣahāsyahetumapṛcchannṛpaticakraśiraḥparigṛhītaśāsanaḥ | tataḥ <lb> sāpyavādīdbhūbhujam | asudrumajambukasya gotradūrīkaraṇādyadajaniṣṭa tathātvāpattirbhavato 346,1

punarapi nṛpatistāmānāyya timihasitahetumacīkaṇat | sāpi prāsoṣṭa vācam | bhūpate kimityāgrahaṃ carīka<lb>rīṣi | atiśayaṃ jahīhi mahīpate | atyāgrahaṃ kurvāṇayościntāmaṇyaśmantayoḥ yathā dvayorapyapāyaḥ sama<lb>jāyata tādṛkprakāraḥ tavāpi bobhaviṣyati | tato bhūpālastayoścaritamāvedayatu bhavatīti tāmudayojayat | <lb> sā covāca | śṛṇu śravaṇabhūṣaṇabhūtakīrte | śrīmallikārjunasya vartmani aśmantako vṛkṣo 'bhūt | sa tvekena <lb> kenacitpathikena sādhubhāvamāpāditaḥ | tatskandhe 'dhastādekāṃ vitardikāṃ viracayya upari vartulaṃ sarvataḥsamaṃ <lb> sthāpitavān | ekaṃ bhūrisindūraparipūritapratīkaṃ prasūnapūjitatanuṃ ca kṛtvā cintāmaṇināmadheyaṃ tasya <lb> cakāra | itthaṃ bahubhirahobhirgatānugatikatayā tasya devasya sādhīyasī prasiddhirajāyata | pratyahaṃ tasya <lb> sindūrādipūjānaivedyaṃ vardhate tathā caturthīdine modakapāyasādiracanā | itthaṃ mahimā tasya bahurabhavat | <lb> anyacca pūrvaṃ mārgitāḥ aśmantakasya parṇamekaikaṃ gṛhṇanti sarve pathikāḥ | tena vikārāṅgīkāramāviṣkaroṣi | iti niśamyāśmantako 'pi cintāmaṇiṃ vyāharati <lb> sma | tvayi kiṃ nāma cintāmaṇiḥ | macchāyāsamāśrayaṃ kṛtavānmadāśrayabalena tava garīyānmahimā prā<lb>durāsīt | naivedyādyabhyavahārato bhavato 'ṅgāni samūlāni jātāni | ahaṃ tvadanubhūtāndvādaśāpi māsā<lb>nkaravāṇi | tvaṃ sarvasminkṣetre tiṣṭhasi | sarvaḥ ko 'pi karṣako hārāsañjanāya lāṅgalasyopari sthāpayati 'śmantakaḥ cintāmaṇimabhāṇīt | tvayā <lb> vinā mama kiṃ nāma hīyate | tvaṃ kimiti na yāsyasi | tadānīṃ sa cintāmaṇirvedikāṃ tāṃ vihāya <lb> parato gatavān | cintāmaṇirahitaḥ sa tarurbādhāmanvabhavat | anyasmindine jana eka āgatyāśmantakasya <lb> tvaco bandhavidhānāya samākṛṣṭavān | apara āgatya medinīkhananāya skandhata evānuciccheda | iti <lb> prakārastasya prāvartata | cintāmaṇistu kaṇṭakaghaṭitapratitalakṛtāvasthitiruṣṇāṃśūṣmaṇā pāṇḍuradhūsaravarṇatā<lb>mādade | tadupari pakṣiṇa ajahuḥ | sa tvekena janena paravalgugulphāntaḥparikṣepāya prāpta iti dūrataḥ <lb> paryastaḥ | iti 346,30

tadanu dināntare dharāturāṣāḍbālasarasvatīmānāyya timihasitakāraṇamanvayuṅkta | tadākarṇya bālasarasvatī <lb> sasarja vācam | ākarṇaya vikramāditya | etatkāraṇamāvedayāmi | paramekā vijñaptirasti | bhavatpradhānamukhyaḥ <lb> puṣpahāso 'yaṃ bhavatā kasmānnigṛhītaḥ | tacchrutvā rājā vyāhārṣīt | yadā hasati tadānīṃ pariṣada <lb> upari bahulapuṣpāsārābhisāro bhavati | evaṃvidha etadīyo guṇaḥ | itthaṃ paramajanapadaparivṛḍhasya śiṣṭāḥ <lb> samīpamāgatā abhūvan | tebhyaḥ kautukaṃ darśanīyamiti dhiyā ahamenamajahasam | kiṃ tadānīmabhihito <lb> 'pi nāsāvahāsīt | tadroṣaparavaśo 'hamenaṃ nigṛhītavān | iti niśamya bālasarasvatī dharādhināthaṃ <lb> girā jagrāha | sa tu kusumahāso devena nigalādunmocanīyaḥ | sādhutayā mānayitvā tadānīṃ kiṃ <lb> dinadvaye hāsaṃ nākārṣīstvamiti devena praṣṭavyaḥ | tadanu matsyahāsyahetujijñāsārthamapi sa evānuyoktavyaḥ | <pb> tatastadvacanāvagamānnarapatiḥ puṣpahāsamunmocya pradhānamudrādhikāraṃ ca vidhāya kimiti tadānīṃ na <lb> tvamahāsīriti tamanvayuṅkta | tadānīṃ rājādeśamāsādyāmātyo 'pyavādīt | deva ityasti | <lb>
<pb n="347">
siddhamantrauṣadhaṃ dharmaṃ grahacchidraṃ ca maithunam |
bandhanaṃ cāvakāśaṃ ca matimānna prakāśayet ||

347,5

deva enamaprākṣīt | tadānīṃ rahasyamapi vaktavyameva | manaḥsaṃmohinīnāmadheyā madīyā gṛhiṇī | sā jīvā<lb>dapyatyantatayā praṇayapātram | tāṃ vihāya kāmapi kāminīṃ na pariśīlayāmi | kiṃ tu | sāpi vyabhicarantī <lb> mama dṛgayanamāsasāda | ata eva tadānīṃtanadine mama manasi na kaścana sukhalavāśrayaḥ | kiṃ tu svairojjā<lb>garaduḥkhasāgarāntargatagurugarodgārakalitagāmbhīryaṃ mama mānasaṃ prāṇapriyāyāḥ prāṇasthānasamāno yaḥ kṣaṇaḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pravartamāno 'sti mūrcchollā<lb>sitaitādṛśī kaṣṭā daśā prāvarīvarti taddharṣotkareṇa hāsyaṃ bhavataḥ prāsaṃjayat | tataḥ puṣpahāso jagāda <lb> rājānam | deva yadyabhayadānaṃ dātumīśiṣe tadā vakṣyāmi | vāvadīhīti dattaṃ mayābhayaṃ taveti nṛpa<lb>tinābhihitaḥ puṣpahāso babhāṣe | deva tvadīyeyaṃ prāṇeśvarī kāmakalikā | asyā girā matsyā api <lb> 347,30

punaḥ prabhāvato pradoṣakāle vinayakandarpopāntaprāptaye pakṣiṇaṃ papraccha | so 'pyavādīt | devi śṛṅgāravatīva <lb> vyasananirasane prasṛmarasaṃvidrasā≤nṛ≥«nu»sāriṇī bhavasi cettadā yāhītyabhyadhāt | 348,16

anyasmindine kumudakośanandinī vinayakandarpasya saṃketaniketanagamanāya śukaṃ vakti sma | so 'pyavādīt | <lb> madanavatīvottaravitaraṇe prabhutāmālambase cettadānīṃ vraja | tatastaccaritāvagamāya prabhāvatībhāvitapraśnaḥ <lb> pakṣīndro 'pyādade vācam | ākarṇaya | kaumudīdaṃhinī nāma grāmaḥ | tatra trilocanasaṃjño rāvuttaḥ | tasya <lb> sahacarī madanavatī | sā cātīva saundaryabhāvavatī vyabhicāracāturyaviracanāprapañcānvitaparicayāpi paraṃ <lb> prasaṅgaṃ na prāpnoti sma parito rakṣakamanuṣyaniṣiddhabahirgamanā | itthamatikrāmati kāle parvaviśeṣeka<lb>smingaṅgāvagāhāya bhartrānujñātagamanā gṛhītopacāraparikarā ceṭīdvitīyā prakaṭitabhavabhaktidhūrjaṭidṛ<lb>ṣṭinikaṭīkaraṇāya samāṭīkate sma śivālayam | sā ca vilāsābhivyaktipaṭīyasī taraṃgitāpāṅgataṭīkā<lb>bhinayapravartitruṭī sthagitadvipaṭī prapañcitārabhaṭī sphuṭībhavati samakuṭīcaroccāṭīkaraṇamūrtistadanu mada<lb>nādhidevateva mūrtimatī tasmātkaraṭicarmakuṭanikaṭādvyāghuṭya paryaṭantī khaṇḍaparaśubhayaparityaktakārmukaṃ <lb> kāmamivāparaṃ vāḍavaṃ madhyepathamadrākṣīt | sā taṃ dṛṣṭidūtībodhitasaṃketaṃ kalākalāpakovidānāmagragaṇyaṃ <lb> taddṛkpallavitamadanadāvapāvakaṃ tadabhiprāyāvabodhadattāvadhānaṃ nijaparisaramānināya māninī | <lb>
udīrito 'rthaḥ paśunāpi gṛhyate vahanti nāgāśca hayāśca coditāḥ |
anuktamapyūhati paṇḍito janaḥ pareṅgitajñānaphalā hi buddhayaḥ ||
āhāranidrābhayamaithunaṃ ca sāmānyametatpaśubhirnarāṇām |
jñānaṃ narāṇāmadhiko viśeṣo jñānena hīnaḥ paśubhiḥ samānaḥ ||

348,31

tatastadupakaṇṭhamāgatya prayuṅkte svavācam | tvaṃ kasmānmāṃ samānaiṣīḥ | tadabhidhehi prayojanam | tatastayā <lb> vyāhāri | mama tvadīyābhilāṣaḥ samupanīpannaḥ | tarhi tvayā madīyamagāramāgantavyam | etajja<lb>nanī nimimīla | tatastajjanitaduḥkhaharātkāndiśīyahṛdayasaṃnidhāna janmā jagāma | ityabhidhāya tamavekṣya <lb> vepamānāṃ rudantīṃ tāṃ saṃsāraniḥsārāviṣkaraṇagirā samāśvāsayat | 349,31

punarapi prabhāvatī praśnaprasaṅginī pakṣīndraṃ pratyarpayadgiraḥ | so 'pi kāntimatīva āyāsavistaraṃ titīrṣasi <lb> cettadānīmidamādartavyam | iti tāmujjagāra giram | tatastadvṛttāntāvagamaṃ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ pakṣīndraḥ prāha | <lb> prabhāpurābhidhānaṃ nagaram | tatra mandabuddhyabhihitaḥ kumbhakāraḥ | tasya patnī kāntimatī | sā vyabhicāra<lb>niratā | kadāciduparamaṇena samaṃ mandiramadhyamadhyāste | tatastasyāḥ patirāpatitaḥ | tarhi vāvadohi prabhāvati <lb> tasminsamaye sā kamupāyamacīcarat | prabhāvatī vicāraparā prāvartata | taduttaraṃ nājñāsīt | tataḥ śukaḥ <lb> pravaktuṃ pracakrame | bhartāramāgatamabhivīkṣya sā devadattamavadat | tvamenaṃ burburadrumamadhyāroha | mā kimapi <lb> vācaṃ prayuṅkṣva | ahamuttaraṃ karavāṇi | tato 'sau bhayavidruto vasanavirahito burburadrumamadhyārūḍhavān | <pb> kumbhakāraḥ samāgacchattāvatā taṃ burburadrumamadhirūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭavān | tadanu taṃ vyāharati sma | tvaṃ ko bhavasi re | <lb> tato 'sau na vakti ca | tataḥ kāntimatī giraḥ prākāmyamākāṅkṣati sma | etatpṛṣṭhe vairiṇaḥ parigṛhītavanto <lb> vyāpādanāya | kāraṇena tenāyaṃ bibhyatpalāyamāno drumamenamadhyārukṣat | kālakalitavaikalyo bhrāmyanma<lb>tijīvaścarandṛḍhasthānāvalambano janitavacanavismaraṇa ādityodayādatraivāvatiṣṭhate | ityākarṇya kumbhakā<lb>rastamārūḍhadrumaṃ vyājahāra | re piśācanagnakāya taroravaroha | tadanu taroravarohati | tamālakṣya tasmai vasanaṃ <lb> dattvā kṣemādikaṃ nirmāya nirmatsarastaṃ prāhiṇot | tādṛśī prajñā tava posphurīti cettadānīṃ vraja || <lb> iti viṃśo kathā || 20 || <lb>

350,8

352,30

maraṇe kṣaṇikaṃ duḥkhaṃ mānabhaṅge dine dine ||

353,14

tasmādidānīṃ pramīyate | ityaṃ bhartari śṛṇvati sati sā niścityāhāryaniścayeva gṛhanikaṭasthitajalagarte <lb> patiṣyāmītyuktvā gatvā ca jalagartasamīpaṃ kūpasyopari vartinīṃ śilāṃ gṛhītvā kūpasyāntaḥ prākṣipat | <lb> svayaṃ cāgatya dvāraśākhāntike nyalīyata | śilā tu jalamadhyamāpātayantī ṭhaṭhātkāreṇa mahatānādyata | <lb> taddhanerbibhyadasau pravepamāno vegena vihāya śayanīyaṃ kavāṭaṃ vighāṭayanbahirāgatya kūpopakaṇṭhaṃ gatvā <lb> tatsaṃnidhāyinyau śrutī vidhāyāntaḥ patitavadhūdhvaniviśeṣākarṇanāya praguṇobhavati sma | tasminnavasare sā <lb> gṛhāntaraṃ praviśya kavāṭaṃ kṛpīṭayonimānasā samajīghaṭatkapaṭopāyaprakaṭitamatiḥ kulaṭākuladevatā | <lb> so 'pi kūpamadhye kamapi dhvanimanākarṇayanpunarāgatya yāvatā pravivikṣati tāvatā pihitakavāṭadvāraṃ <lb> lakṣitavān | tadanu manasi dhvanati sma | tadvidheyavaiśiṣṭyaṃ mugdhikayā evetyabhidhāya dvāri sthitaḥ mugdhikā<lb>mabhyadhāt | vayaṃ bhavatyāścāturyeṇa samunmiṣitapratibhāḥ svamanasi parāṃ saṃtuṣṭimābibhrāṇā vartāmahe | tadānīṃ <lb> niśamya kavāṭamudajīghaṭat | dvayorapi premaprakarṣaḥ prādurabhūt | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapītthamupāyaviśeṣaṃ <lb> praguṇayasi cettadānīmādartavyaṃ svasamīhitamiti || <lb> iti pañcaviṃśatī kathā || 25 || <lb>

353,26

punaḥ prabhāvatī papraccha pakṣiṇam | guṇāḍhyabrāhmaṇavadyadi saṃkīrṇasamayaṃ netuṃ pārayasi tadādartavyamiti <lb> so 'pyavādīttām | tadvṛttāntaṃ vyāharatāditi prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ pakṣī pratyāha | viśālapurābhidhāne nagare <lb> guṇāḍhyanāmāgrajanmā | sa dhanārjanamuddiśya deśāntaramaśiśriyat | tadanu pathi gacchannagaramekamāsasāda | <lb> tatra sthitvā samānaloke kiṃ karavāṇyatreti na kamapyudyamamāpnute sma | tadanu goṣṭhe gatvā nirudyama<lb>ścintayati sma | tadā bṛhattanuṃ pralambagalakambalaṃ jarāśithilitastrāyuṃ vṛṣamekaṃ goṣṭhe lakṣīcakāra | tataḥ <lb> sa guṇāḍhyo 'nudinaṃ tadabhyagramāgatya karoṣaśakalena vṛṣabhasyāṅgāni kaṇḍūyati tṛṇakaṇādi grāsāya <lb> prayacchati | iti pratyahaṃ pariśīlanena sa taṃ vṛṣabhaṃ svavaśīcakāra | itthaṃ sa pratyahamāgatya rajjvā nibadhya <lb> yatra kvāpi gacchati tatra niṣadho 'sau gacchati śṛṅgacālanena raudratāṃ darśayati | tata ekasmindivase <lb> vṛṣabhe paryāṇaṃ nikṣipya pradoṣasamaye kasyāścana paṇyagaṇikāyā gṛhānagacchadvṛṣabhamāruhya | tasyāḥ kuṭṭinīṃ <lb> prati giraṃ nayati sma | vayaṃ vyavahāriṇaḥ | asmadīyā vastupūrṇā anaḍvāhaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samāyānti | prātastvā<lb>gamiṣyanti | ahaṃ tvatra gatvārthanirṇayāyāgrata eva samāgamamidānīm | paścānniveśitasaṃnidhānaṃ yā<pb>maścattadānīṃ divaso 'pi samānaṃ nāvasānabhāvaṃ bhajate | adyatanaṃ divasamatraivāsminnivāsāya saukaryaṃ <lb> kurvantu | yadyāciṣyante tadahaṃ vitariṣyāmi | tatastanniśamya kuṭṭinī prakaṭīcakāra vācam | īdṛśaṃ sāmā<lb>nyajanasvabhāvāsannaṃ ca kimiti vyavaharanti bhavādṛśāḥ | bhavantaḥ kimanyalokasāmānyāḥ | gṛhamidaṃ yauṣmā<lb>kīṇameva | atra sukhenāgantavyamuṣitavyaṃ ca | bhavatsadṛśāḥ samāyānti yasmindine tadeva sudinam | itarāṇi <lb> durdinānīti | tathaivamasmadīyā tanayā rathyāpaṇyāṅganā | bhāsvatkapardakaṃ gṛhītvā pānīyaṃ pāyaya tā<lb>dṛkklamabhāvodbhāvinī na bhavati | tataḥ kapaṭavipaṇī vāṇīṃ prāṇaiṣīt | dhanaṃ madīyo 'yaṃ balīvardo <lb> dūrataraṃ gacchati | dvāri sthāpayituṃ na yujyate | ayamantaḥśālāyāṃ prabaddhavya ityabhidhāya tatra sthitavān | <lb> aṅgamardanaplavanādyajāyanta | rātrau tayā saha nyavātsīt | pratyāsanne prātastanasamaye samutyāya veśyāyāḥ <lb> sakalamalaṃkāraṃ gṛhītvā gatavān | vṛṣabhaṃ ca tatraivāvasthāpayat | tadanu dinodaye dāsī bahirniragāt | <lb> vṛṣabhaṃ nibaddhamadrākṣīt | tāvatā jarantaṃ viśvaṃbharāspṛśatsāsnaṃ rorūyamāṇamabhivīkṣya kakudmantaṃ dāsī <lb> śambhalīṃ babhāṇa | kasyāyaṃ bahirnibaddho vṛṣabha iti | tataḥ śambhalī tasyāstadabhihitamākarṇya tvaritaga<lb>tirudatiṣṭhat | vṛṣabhaṃ cāpaśyat | paścātkuṭṭinī jagāda | paśya re śarvarīsamāgato madīyasamastavastuluṇṭhako 'yamityabhidhāya vidhṛtastayā | sā taṃ rājabhavanaṃ netumudyunakti sma | tarhi prabhā<lb>vati tvamapi bhāṣasva | etāvati saṃkucitasamayātipāte 'pi kamupāyamajīghaṭat | tadā madīyastvaritaga<lb>tiranaḍvānbhavatāṃ samīpe tiṣṭhati | sa dātavyaḥ | no cedayāhamāvedya rājakule bhavatīṃ daṇḍayiṣyāmi | <lb> mātaṅgasyopabhogamakārṣīdiyamityabhidhāya yāsyāmi | tadanu kuṭṭinī 354,28

tataḥ prabhāvatyuparamaṇanivāsamiyāsuḥ pataṃgapuṃgavaṃ girā saṃgatottaragiraṃ cakāra | devi sarṣapastenavadātmano <lb> vaiṣamyāpanayanaṃ nirmātuṃ prabhavasi cettadā vraja | tatastatpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prabhāvatīṃ tadvṛttāntamaśrāvayat | śṛṇu <lb> śravaṇānanda pradāyimatpadacarite | pratiṣṭhānapure ko 'pi dasyurnyavātsīt | sa tu dyūte sarvamapi dhanaṃ parā<lb>jīyata | tadanu yāminyāṃ kasyacidvaṇijo gṛhe bhittiṃ vibhidyāntaḥ prāviśat | tadgṛhamadhye na kimapi <lb> nayanaviṣayīkṛtavān | tata ekasminbhāṇḍe sarṣapānapaśyat | tāngṛhītvā vastreṇa baddhā bahirniragacchat | <lb> tāvatā rājabhaṭā ājñāsiṣuḥ | sa tairvidhṛtaḥ tadvaddhasarṣapavastraṃ tadgale baddhā rājñaḥ samīpaṃ prāptaḥ | rājāpi <lb> tānbhaṭānevamavādīt | gacchatainaṃ gṛhītvā mārayatetyukte prabhāvati tvamapi vicārya mahyamāvedaya | itthaṃ <lb> kenopāyabalena racitavānasāvātmānamiti | prabhāvatī vicāracāturyaṃ nāṭayantī na vetti tatpraśnam | <lb> tadanu prabhātaṃ saṃjātamavagatya pataṃgaśreṣṭhamanuyuyoja | so 'pyavādīt | ākarṇaya prabhāvati | rājā taṃ vyā<lb>pādanāyānāyayat | tato malīmaso malimluco mahīpālaṃ jagāda | ahaṃ bhavaducitaprayatnaśatairna hiṃsyo <pb> bhaveya | bhavanto manmāraṇanimittaṃ yathākathaṃcana kurvantu paraṃ nāhaṃ mriye | tadānīṃ vismayo rājña udiyāya | <lb> rājā tamaprākṣīt | bhavadamaraṇe kiṃ kāraṇam | tadanvavadatso 'pi | jñānaśīlinaḥ pumāṃso bālakagale <lb> rakṣāmabhilakṣya mantrasaṃskṛtānsarṣapāndīyantāṃ samastāpi ḍākinībhūtapretapiśācajanitabādhā bādhitā <lb> bhavati na kaścidapyupadravaḥ prabhavati pīḍayitum | mama gale sarṣapabhāra etāvānsaṃsthito 'sti | tataḥ <lb> kena viśeṣeṇa mayi maraṇodbhāvanaṃ vikacayanti hanta | ityākarṇya mahīndro vyāhārṣīt | taṃ mocayadhvam | <lb> tarhi kumudanandini etāvadupāyapariśīlanaṃ bhavatī vetti cettathā vidhehi vidheyaviśeṣaṇam || <lb> iti saptaviṃśatī kathā || 27 || <lb>

355,8

tataḥ prabhāvatī bhujaṃgasaṃgataṃ cikīrṣantī vayasi vācāṃ vilāsaṃ prakāśayati sma | tatastayā pṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ <lb> śāntikādevī hyātmano bhartāraṃ viṣamāvasthāpannaṃ matisamunmeṣābhivyañcanenodamocayat | kenopāyavidhānena <lb> svapatiṃ niramocayatsā | tataḥ prabhāvatī bahudhā vicāranirmāṇaparā nāvindattadupāyam | tataḥ prābhā<lb>tike samaye śukamajalpatkṛśodarī | śukaḥ prācīkaṭat kalpitaprabahūnnapākā samastopacāraprapañcanaparā yakṣiṇīprāsā<lb>damāsasāda | tadā rakṣaṇanimittaṃ dvāri sthitānbhaṭānadrākṣīt | te na kasyāpyantaḥpraveśaṃ dadati | tadanu <lb> sā tadabhimukhamāgatavatī dvārapālānavadat | parameśvaryāḥ pūjāyupacāraparicaraṇaṃ vihāya mama pāraṇā<lb>vidhirna phalati | adya bhavadbhirasmadīye mandire 'bhyavahṛtirabhyasanīyā | tāvatā tāmbūlaṃ nayantvityabhi<lb>dhāya karasthitaṃ kaṅkaṇaṃ yāmikānāṃ kare vyasṛjat | ahamekākyevāntargatvā devatāṃ copacāraviśeṣairabhyarcya <lb> niyamaṃ nirmāyedānīmeva vyāvṛtyāgamiṣyāmītyabhidhāya prāsādāntaḥ 356,1

tataḥ prabhāvatī patatriṇamaprākṣīt | śuko 'pi vyāhārṣīt | devi kelikeva saṃkucitāvasaramapasārayituṃ <lb> pārayasi cettadānīmabhitiṣṭhābhisaraṇamiti vihagenābhihite tadvṛttāntavividiṣayā prabhāvatyā vegagatirjalapūrṇaṃ kumbhaṃ gṛhe samānīya tatprātiveśinīpurastātsaṃketaṃ parikalpya tadanu nijakuladevatāyāḥ <lb> snānādikaṃ vidhāya pūjāpramukhopacāraṣoḍaśakaṃ samāpya prārthanāṃ kartuṃ pravartate | 356,21

punaḥ prabhāvatī vinayakandarpāntikagamanāya vihaṃgaṃ jagāda so 'pyavadat | devi maṇḍodarīvottaravi<lb>nimayanirmāṇe nijāṃ matiṃ viśadayasi yadi tadāṅgīkuru | tatastadvṛttāntamavajigamiṣuḥ prabhāvatī 357,19

357,27

ityabhidhāya taṃ mārayitumanayat | tarhyācakṣva prabhāvati | maticakora etāvatsamayasamāsaktau tadā pratārakaṃ <lb> kamakarot | tataḥ prabhāvatī vicāracāturyamanubhūyāpi tadaviṣayantī vihaṃgamaṃ vyājahāra | tayā pṛṣṭaḥ <lb> śuko 'pi tasyāḥ saṃdehāpanudaṃ jagāda | prabhāvati śṛṇu | tadā taskaro rājānaṃ vyajijñapat | deva <lb> vijñaptirekāsti | ahaṃ kimapi cūḍāmaṇisamahitaṃ jñānaṃ karatalakalitamavikalamākalayāmi | tarhi <lb> bhaviṣyataḥ samayasya kamapi jñānaprakāramabhidhāsyāmi | tadanu bhūpālo 'pyavadat | vyāharasveti | tato <lb> 'sau jagāda | deva etattvaṃ bādhārāhityena nirṇayakaṭākṣitameva jānīhi | ekasmātpraharādupari samasto <lb> 'pi sargo 'nyathaiva bhaviṣyati | andhakāraḥ pravartiṣyate mahābhayānakaḥ | tarhyevaṃvidhasyātigarīyaso jagadu<lb>padravasya śāntikaraṇāya tvayyākāṅkṣā varīvarti yadi tadānīṃ kuru tat | itarathaitatsarvamapi parisamā<lb>ptamevetyahaṃ paśyāmi | tadanu medinīnātho giramasṛjat | tarhyetasyopadravasya kathaṃ śāntirbhavatītyāca<lb>ṣṭām | tadā rājājñāmāsādya so 'pyuvāca | tvameva tadupadravasya śāntiṃ kariṣyasītvetadarthe mahyamātmanaḥ <pb> satyavacanaṃ prayaccha paścādabhidhāsyāmi | tadā rājā tasmai satyavacanaṃ prāyacchat | tato 'sau tacchāntikaṃ <lb> rājānamāśrāvayat | madrakṣaṇaṃ kartavyametāvatā tacchāntirbhaviṣyatītyavagaccha | rājāpyavocat | anyādṛśī <lb> sṛṣṭirbhaviṣyatīti tatkim | so 'bravīt | avadhatsva mahīmahendra | ātmani praśamite sarvāpi sṛṣṭiḥ samā<lb>ptarūpaiva | yadāhaṃ mṛtastadā samasto 'pi sargo 'nyathā jāta eva | mametareṣāmapekṣayā kiṃ nāma prayojanam | <lb> tadā rājā tadvacanamapahāsya taṃ niramocayat | tataḥ prabhāvati ityādyabhyāsaṃ cikīrṣasi yadi tadā <lb> prayāhi || <lb> iti ekatriṃśatkathā || 31 || <lb>

358,8

359,24

punaḥ prabhāvatī girā jagrāha vihaṃgamam | so 'pi prāsoṣṭa vācam | devi dhūrtamāyākuṭṭinīva svasyopari <lb> samāpatatparidyūnatvaṃ punastapaḥsaraṇe prasarati yadi prabhāsamutsekastadānīṃ 360,10

tataḥ kuṭṭinī vācamanīyata rasanāgram | āyuṣo vināśaṃ vinā śaknoti na maraṇamabhibhavitum | anyacca | <lb> sahānusaṃdhānamāsādya vividhabuddhividhānanibandhanakaramapi na cinvanti santaḥ | <lb>
