360,14

itthamukte tatkuṭṭinīvacananiyamitamānasā tasmingrāme paśyatyevātmānaṃ jalagarte cikṣepa | tadanu dhāvamāno <lb> rāmastatkūpasamīpaṃ gatvā tāṃ samīkṣayāmāsa | tadā svamanasi camatkṛtavān | ityamabhyadhāñca | naitasyāḥ <lb> cetaḥ prapañcopacayaparicitipārīṇam | iyaṃ kevalaṃ māmevānusṛtavatī | tadanu yatkimapi tasya dhanamabhūtta<lb>tkarasātkṛtavān | tadanu kaiścana dinairnirdhanamājātaṃ tamālokya dūrīcakāra kalāvatī | tato dhanavirahito <lb> rāmo nijanagaramājagāma janakasya purastāduditamavarṇayat | sa tu dhūrtamāyākuṭṭinīṃ samāhūya sahasradvayaṃ <lb> suvarṇānāmayācata | tadā sā kamalākaramabhyadhāt | tasminneva nagare punardhanārjanoddeśena vyāpārapuraskṛtaṃ <lb> rāmaṃ prasthāpayatu bhavān | ahamapyanena samaṃ prayāyām | tadnu sa tāmapi sthānaviśeṣaṃ prātiṣṭhipat | <lb> tato rāmastatsthānamāsedivān | tatastadabhimukhī kalāvatyāgacchat | tadāgamanoddeśopayācitadīpikā <lb> vibhinnabādhā rūpabahulasaṃbhramavibhramavatī rāmaparisaramāgatya nīrājayāmāsa rāmam | tadanu nṛttagītavā<lb>dyādyanekopacāraprapañcaparicitaṃ nijaniketanamanṣait | dvāvapi sukhena viṣayāmbubhujāte | tarhi prabhāvati <lb> tvamapi cāru vicintyācakṣva | tadā sā tadīyaṃ dhanaṃ kathamānītavatī | tataḥ prabhāvatī tañcintāyāṃ <lb> dattacittāpi dhanānayanopāyaṃ na kalayati sma | tadā tayā pṛṣṭaḥ pataṃgo vyācaṣṭa | tadānīṃ dhūrtamāyā <lb> kuṭṭinī rāmāya saṃketaṃ prādarśayat | tvayā gatvātmoparitanabhūmikāyāṃ kalāvatyā mandirasya śāri<lb>bhirdevanīyaṃ tayaiva saha | ahaṃ ca tenaiva vartmanā gamiṣyāmi tadgṛhaṃ purato gatvā tvaṃ tu māmabhivīkṣamāṇo <lb> madbhīticintitaḥ | parato dṛṣṭvā tvāmapasarantaṃ kalāvatī prakṣyati | tvaṃ kimityātmānaṃ gopāyasīti | <lb> tadā sā bhavataivamabhidhātavyā | iyaṃ purato mārge samāgacchantī vāśreyakāriṇī jaratī madīyā jananī <lb> sā | etadīyaṃ draviṇaṃ nītvā bhavatyāḥ saṃnidhānaṃ pūrvamāgatavān | taddhanaṃ bhavatyai dattam | idānīmiyamā<lb>gatāsti | ko jānīte kiṃ karomīti | iti vacanaṃ bhavatā śrāvayitavyā kalāvatī | kuṭṭinīkṛtasaṃketo <lb> rāmaḥ kalāvatīmandiramāgacchat | tatra gatvā tathā sahopatyakāyāṃ śāribhiradīvyat | tadā dhūrtamāyā <lb> kuṭṭinī skandhopari vipañcīṃ vimucya tadagramārgamanusasāra | rāmo 'pi tadabhimukhamevālokamānastiṣṭhati | <lb> sa ca tāmabhivīkṣya krīḍāṃ tatyāja ca tadgagocare gatavān | tataḥ kalāvatī tamapṛcchat | tvaṃ kasmā<lb>dutthito 'sīti | tadāsau pūrvatanaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ tasyā agre jagāda | tataḥ kuṭṭinī dvārapradeśamāpatat | tā<lb>gṛhasthitānvāvadīti | madīyaṃ putraṃ rāmaṃ prasthāpayantu | mama sarvasvamapahṛtya bhavatīnāṃ haste vitīrṇamasti | <pb> tatastābhiraprākṣi sā | kā kiṃnāmadheyeti | kutratyeti | sāvocat | padmāvatyāṃ nagaryāṃ sudarśanasya medinīpa<lb>rivṛḍhasya prātaḥkālagāyakāham | ahaṃ mātaṃgagāyakā | ayaṃ ca mama putraḥ | bhavatyāścaitadīyena saṃsargeṇa <lb> vartamānaḥ samastamapi sādhulokamaśucīkaroti sma | paraṃ bhavatyo yathāruci kurvantu | mama tena kiṃ <lb> prayojanam | iti vacobhistā abibhayuḥ | tāṃ gṛhāntaramānayāmāsuḥ samastaṃ dhanaṃ tasyai prāyacchan | <lb> taccaraṇayorapataṃśca | vārtteyaṃ na kasyāpi puro 'bhidhātavyā | ityabhidhāya sadhanāṃ tāṃ prātiṣṭhipan | tarhi <lb> prabhāvatīti viśeṣamāyānaṭane prāgalbhyaṃ bibharṣi yadi tadā sādhyatāmiti || <lb> iti catustriṃśatkathā || 34 || <lb>

361,8

prabhāvatī punaraprākṣīcchukam | tenāpi vyāhāri | devi ratanādevīvottaraṃ kartuṃ jānīye yadi tadā sā<lb>dhvabhisara | ityabhihite śukena prabhāvatyāvādīt | ratanādevīvṛttāntamāvedayetyabhihitaḥ śuko vyājahāra | <lb> indrapure nagare vikramasiṃhanāmā rājaputrastasya sahacarī ratanādevī | sa tāṃ tāḍayati gālīrvitarati <lb> vinaiva prayojanamīrṣyālutāṃ prakaṭīkaroti | ko 'tra samāgato 'bhūtko vā gatavān | he upapatisamudbhave <lb> dvārīpradeśe kasmādūrdhvā sthitāsi nirnimittaṃ sicayaṃ kasmātsaṃvītaṃ bhavatyā | ityābhāṣya vācāṭatāṃ <lb> pratyahabhupanyasyati tāṃ prati | tataḥ sā svamanogataṃ nigadati sma | ayamevaṃvidhaḥ pāpiṣṭhatamaḥ | tarhyetasya <lb> vañcanāprapañcane 'pi na kaścana doṣakalaṅkaśaṅkuśaṅkākulitotpātaḥ | tadanu sā vyabhicāracaraṇāya pravartate <lb> sma | vyabhicāravidyāyāmatīvāśeṣakovidā caṇḍacaritā prāvartata | tadā tannagarādhipatinā samaṃ tathā <lb> tasya sutena ca saha gacchati | parasparaṃ jñātuṃ na dadāti | ekasmindivase grāmādhipasutena saha suratopabhogaṃ <lb> kurvāṇāsti | tāvatāsau grāmādhipa eva samāgataḥ | tataḥ sā tamālokya tatputraṃ gopāyati sma taṃ ca <lb> mandirābhyantaramājuhāva | tamapi pūrṇamanorathamakārṣīt | tāvatā vikramasiṃharājaputraḥ kopakaluṣitaḥ samā<lb>gatavān | tarhi prabhāvati vyācaṣṭhāṃ nāma bhavatī | etasminnavasare tayā kimuttaramakāri | sā ca vicā<lb>raviśadamānasāpi na taduttaraṃ kalitavatī | tataḥ śuko 'bhāṣata | ākarṇaya prabhāvati | bhatīramāyā<lb>ntamavagatya grāmādhipasya haste kaśāṃ prāyacchat | tvaṃ śapathaṃ dadhāno bahirnirgaccha | madīyaḥ putraścaṇḍālo <lb> yadā mama hastaprāpto 'bhaviṣyattadānīṃ tasya śira eva hariṣyāmītyamidadhāno tiṣṭhanneva bahirgatya yā<lb>hīti | tadāsau grāmaprabhustādṛgabhinayastathaiva vyāharamāṇo bahirniragāt | vikramasiṃharāvutto mandira<lb>madhyamāgatya ratanādevīmaprākṣīt | yamagṛhīto 'yaṃ grāmanāyakaḥ kasya gālīrvitarannirgacchati | tataḥ sā <lb> rāvuttamavādīt | idānīṃ bhavantaḥ śrāntāḥ santi | pūrvaṃ suparvaparicaryāntaṃ pratyavasānaṃ ca kurvantu | paścā<lb>dbhavataḥ puro vṛttāntamidamabhidhāsyāmi | tadanu rāvuttastu suparvārcanamabhyavaharaṇādikaṃ ca kṛtvā tāmbalapū<lb>ritānano bhūtvā sukhāsīnaḥ śramaṃ tatyāja | tadā ratanādevī bhuktvā rāvṛttasaṃnidhimāgatya tadvṛttāntavyā<lb>haraṇāya prāvartata | rāvutta kimapyadya nūtanamajāyata | grāmaparivṛḍhaḥ sakṛtputrasyopari cukopa | kṛpāṇaṃ <lb> nirastakośaṃ kṛtvā tatpṛṣṭhamagrahīt | tadānīmasau varākastasya putro rirakṣayiṣuḥ palāyamāno 'smā<lb>kīyadvārapurodeśe vartinīṃ dṛṣṭvā māmevamavādīt | māṃ rakṣata rakṣata | śaraṇamāgato 'haṃ bhavatām | tadā<lb>nīmahaṃ <pb n="362">

362,4

tataḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha | so 'bravīt | tvamapi devi suratasundarīva yadyāyāsanistaraṇe 'vadātamati<lb>tvaṃ prathayasi tadānīmaṅgīkurutāt | tadā prabhāvatyā tadvṛttāntāvabhāvāya pṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ provāca | śaṅkhapurā<lb>bhidhāne nagare mahādhanābhidho grānthikaḥ | tasya sahacarī suratasundarī | sā ca parapuruṣānavaratarataniratā | <lb> tasyāḥ patiryadi kimapi vāvadīti tadā taṃ na sahate | vṛthaiva patyurupari yathākathaṃcana vyājarīharīti | <lb> tato 'sau tadbhītyāvalambitamauna evāvatiṣṭhate | ekasmindine sā nijamupapatiṃ gṛhamānināya | tato <lb> yāminījemanaṃ vidhāya sarve 'pi gṛhanivāsinaḥ śayanāya śayanīyamaśiśriyuḥ | dīpo 'pi nirvā<lb>ṇabhāvaṃ prāpitaḥ | tadā bhartāraṃ nidrāṇamājñāya sā bhujaṃgena saṃgatā bhujaṃgī pratibhāvirāmasamunmiṣadudayā <lb> nibhṛtarasānandāmandasaṃbandhā nitarāmaraṃsīt | tatastadratijanitadhvaniṃ mahādhano 'pyaśṛṇoṣīt | tatastaṃ grahītuṃ <lb> karaṃ prāyuṅkta mahādhanaḥ | tadā sa karastasyopapatermehanamagrahīt | tadāsau suratasundarīmabhāṣiṣṭa | mayā <lb> coro 'sti vidhṛtaḥ | tvaṃ vegena gatvā dīpaṃ samānaya | tataḥ sāpi vyājahāra | ahaṃ dopāharaṇāya <lb> dvāri gacchantī bibhemi | ahameva coraṃ gṛhīṣyāmi bhavanto gatvā dīpamānayantvityabhidhāya tataḥ sā <lb> coramagrahīt | mahādhanastu dīpamānetuṃ bahirniragāt | tato bahirgate mahādhane sāpyupapatiṃ mumoca | tadā <lb> sā mahiṣasiṃhasya jahujihvāmākṛṣya jagrāha | mahādhanastu dīpamujjvālya samānayat | yāvatpaśyati tāvatā <lb> kāsāraśābasya rasanā pāṇinā niyantritāsti | tadālokya mahādhanaṃ vyāhārṣītsuratasundarī | sādhu <lb> sādhu | vīrācaritaṃ caritamakārṣīḥ | tvayā netaraiḥ śūrairīdṛkkartuṃ śakyate | tayetyabhihite mahādhano 'patrapi<lb>ṣṇurivāvatiṣṭhat | tarhi prabhāvatīdṛgvidhamuttaraṃ kartuṃ bhavatī pārayati yadi tadānīṃ sukhena gacchatu || <lb> iti ṣaṭtriṃśatkathā || 36 || <lb>

362,21

punaḥ prabhāvatī vinayakandarpanāmadheyanarendraṃ jigamiṣuḥ pakṣīndraṃ prati prāyuṅkta vācam | tāṃ niśamya so <lb> 'pyabhyadhāt | devi buddhimatīva saṃkīrṇāsaktinistaraṃ kartuṃ jānāsi yadi tadā svamanobhilaṣitamasaṃku<lb>citadhiyā sādhaya | tataḥ prabhāvatyavādīt | he pakṣīndra buddhimatīvṛttāntamāvedayāditaḥ | tacchrutvā śuko <lb> 'pyavocat | ucopuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra sāṃpuratanāmadheyaḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ | tasya sahacarī buddhimatī | sā <lb> parapuruṣaratasamuditamānasā | bhartuḥ kṛte kṣetrabhojanaṃ gṛhītvā gacchantyā mārge kasyacidekasya tarostale <lb> jāreṇa saha pratyahaṃ rahasyasukhamanubhūyate | tasyāstadvilasitaṃ sarve jānate | te taccaritaṃ sāṃpuratakarṣakasya <lb> purastādācacakṣire | tadanvasau tasyāścaritrasyāvajigamiṣayā tamevānokahamāruhya pracchannatanuḥ sthitavān | <lb> tato gṛhītabhojanā gṛhādāgatā tamājagāma buddhimatī | tatrāgatya tadannaṃ jagatyāṃ niveśya bhujaṃgena saṃgatā <lb> samupabhogabhaṅgivigalitavigrahāgrahaparigrahaṃ tadekatānakalitapūrvāparakalākalāpakabahulaṃ niratiśayaṃ vi<lb>ṣayasukhamanvabhūt | tatastayostathāvidhanibaddharasavilasadasamamanaḥsamudayānandaghanatāṃ nirīkṣya vanaspatera<lb>vatatāra | buddhimatī ca taroravatarantaṃ taṃ lakṣīcakāra | tarhi vāvadītu prabhāvati bhavatī | tasminsamaye <lb> sā kimuttaramakarot | tataḥ prabhāvatī cintayantyapi nābudhyata | tatastayānuyukto dvijo 'pi nijagāda | <lb> sā ca bhartāraṃ vīkṣya upapatiṃ prātiṣṭhipat | tadā tatpatiśca samāgatya buddhimatīṃ paryaprākṣīt | bhavatyāḥ <lb> saṃnidhāne dvitīyaḥ pumānka āsīt | tataḥ sā patimavādīt | tvaṃ kiṃ na jānīṣe | drumasyāsyāyameva <lb> svabhāvaḥ | etadārūḍho jano hi sthalasthitamekamapi dvitvena paśyatīti pūrvavṛddhā ācakṣate | tadā svayaṃ <pb> ca taṃ mahīruhamāruroha buddhimatī | tadānīmāruhya taṃ pratyevamavādīt | tvamapyaparasīmantinyā samaṃ sura<lb>tasukhamupabhuñjāno 'si | evaṃvidhastvaṃ pāpatamaḥ | tarhi rājakulānetya bhavaccaritraṃ nivedayiṣyāmi bhavantaṃ <lb> nagnīkariṣyāmi | tadāsau vyāharat | tādṛśaṃ bahvāyāsopapāditaśramasāmastyasamayamityādibuddhivaibhavaga<lb>hanaprayogakalpanātāratamyena yadyativartituṃ prabhavasi yadi tadā sādhayepsitam || <lb> iti saptatriṃśatkathā || 37 || <lb>
<pb n="363">

363,6

tataḥ punaḥ prabhāvatī bhujaṃgasaṃnidhānaṃ jigamiṣuḥ pataṃgaṃ parismayati sma girā | taduditaṃ niśamya so <lb> 'pi jagāda | devi madanāvatīvottaraviracanāyāṃ cāturyaṃ tanoṣi yadi tadā sādhayatu bhavatī | sā <lb> tadvṛttāntaṃ papraccha śukaṃ śuko 'pyavocat | nākapure nagare rathakāro hi karālanāmā | sa tu dvitīyāṃ <lb> striyaṃ paryaṇaiṣīt | tasyā madanāvatīti nāmadheyam | sā ca parapuruṣasurataniratā | tadā janebhyastasyā <lb> vyabhicāracaritaṃ niśamya rathakāraḥ pratyayāvagamāya gṛhe grāmagamanamabhidhāya niragāt | tataḥ pradoṣasamaye <lb> guptadvāramārgeṇa kairapyalakṣito gṛhamadhyamājagāma | sa tvāgatya mañcakasya tale nililye | madanāvatī ca <lb> rathakāracaritaṃ nājñāsīt | tadā sā rathakāraṃ grāmāntaragatamavagatya nitarāmānandalaharīparītāṅgā <lb> samajāyata | <lb>
durdivase ghanatimire gatasaṃcārāsu nagaravīthīṣu |
patyurvideśagamane paramaṃ sukhaṃ jaghanacapalāyāḥ ||

363,16

rathakāro gṛhe nāstīti matvā tathā nijopapatirgṛhaṃ samāninye | tena samaṃ vinodagoṣṭhīmanubhūyamānā<lb>sīt | tadā svacaraṇena bhartāramasprākṣīt | sā caraṇasparśādevetyavāgacchat | madīyo bhartā pracchannatanurmāṃ <lb> śikṣayitumatrāgatya nilīno nivasati | iti manasyabhidhāyotthātumupacakrame | tadānīmupapatirutthāya tāṃ <lb> kacabandhe jagrāha | tarhi prabhāvati tvamācakṣva | tadā tathāvidhe tasminsamaye tayā kimuttaramakāri | tataḥ <lb> prabhāvatī vicāre prayatnaṃ kurvāṇāpi saṃśayanāśaṃ na paricinoti sma | tadānīṃ tadavagamanāya pṛṣṭaḥ <lb> śukastāṃ prati provāca | śṛṇu prabhāvati | kacagṛhītayā tayā vyāhāri | mayā tava purastātpuraiva vyava<lb>hāri | rathakārastu sāṃprataṃ grāmāntaraṃ gato 'sti | tvamautsukyaṃ māmabhidhehi | yadyahaṃ tvadīyasādhanasaṃba<lb>ndhinī | tava dhanena saṃbandho rathakārasyāntikamājagāma | tarhi rathakāro grāmādāgacchatu | tadanu tvaṃ <lb> tameva jahīhi tava manasi yadrocate tvaṃ rathakārasya tatkuru | māmapi tava manaḥsamīhitaṃ vidhehi | <lb> itthaṃ tasyā vacanāni rathakāro 'śrauṣīt | tatastvasāvabibhet | manasyabhihitavāṃśca | lokānāṃ dhanasaṃbandhamā<lb>gadheyaṃ gṛhītaṃ tadatiśayenānaucityamakāri | ityabhidhāya viditabhāṣayā parityāgaṃ vidhāya niragāt | <lb> tarhi prabhāvati yadyetādṛśamuttaraṃ kartuṃ pārayasi tadānīmācara vocitam || <lb> ityaṣṭatriṃśatkathā || 38 || <lb>

363,29

punaḥ prabhāvatī pakṣiṇaṃ papraccha | tataḥ śuko 'bhidadhe | devi śvetāmbaravadātmana upari samāpatitaṃ pracchannā<lb>bhiyogamanyasyopari āropayituṃ prabhavasi yadi tadānutiṣṭha | tataḥ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ śukastadvṛttāntaṃ <lb> prababhāṣe | śṛṇu | śrīpure nagare narendranāmā śvetāmbaraḥ | sakalamapi lokaṃ vaśīcakāra | sarvo 'pi tasya <lb> varivasyāṃ sādhutayā niyamaparamatayā kurute | tadanu divyānnāhārasaṃbandhāttasya viṣayavāsanāpyudiyāya | <lb> tadāsau viṣayavivaśo veśyayā sahitastiṣṭhati | taccaritameko digambarastvajñāsīt | tacchvetāmbaracaritaṃ <lb> śvetāmbarabhaktāya digambara āvedayat | bhavadīyaḥ śvetāmbaro rātrau veśyāgṛhaṃ pravasati | adya pradoṣasamaye <lb> bhavadbhiravekṣaṇāya samāgantavyam | sa ca veśyāsahitaḥ śvetāmbaro draṣṭavyo bhavatāṃ bhaviṣyati | tataste śrā<pb>vakāḥ śvetāmbararakṣaṇāya parita upaviviśuḥ | kṛtasaṃketaḥ śvetāmbaro nijamandire nyavātsīt | tato <lb> veśyāpi tasya veśma prāviśat | tadā śvetāmbara ityavagatavān | madrakṣaṇakṛte ete 'tra paritaḥ prasarīsaranti | <lb> tarhi prabhāvati bhavatyapyāvedayatu | tadā śvetāmbara ātmanaḥ saṃjāyamānāṃ mānakhaṇḍanāṃ kathamapākṛtavān | <lb> tataḥ prabhāvatī vicārapratibhāniratā samajāyata | yadā nāvagacchati tadā śukamaprākṣīt | tataḥ śuko <lb> 'pyavocat | śṛṇu prabhāvati | śvetāmbarastathetthaṃ niraṇaiṣīt | yadidaṃ kaitavakṣapaṇako maduparyāropayannasti <lb> asya kṣapaṇakasya sphigunnato 'phalaṃ darśayiṣyāmītyabhidhāya svayaṃ kṣapaṇakaveṣaṃ vidhāya pāṇinā veśyāṃ <lb> vidhṛtya bahirniragāt | tadrakṣakāḥ śrāvakāḥ taṃ kṣapaṇakamadrākṣuḥ | tadanvabhimukhaṃ gatvā viśeṣatayā na vi<lb>vikṣāṃcakruḥ | kṣapaṇakaṃ cāvajñāsiṣuḥ śvetāmbaraṃ ca sarve 'pi mānayāmāsuḥ | tarhi prabhāvati tvamevaṃrūpamu<lb>pāyaṃ parikalayasi yadi tadānīṃ svasamīhitasādhanaparā bhava || <lb> ityekonacatvāriṃśatkathā || 39 || <lb>
<pb n="364">

364,11

punarapi prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha śuko api nānadīti sma | devi śaśakavadātmano maraṇamapācarīkarīṣi <lb> tenaiva vairiṇaḥ parāhatāḥ tathā buddhiviśeṣaṃ prayunakṣi yadi tadānīṃ yāyāḥ | tadānīṃ tadvṛttāntabubhutsayā <lb> prabhāvatī prababhāṣe | śaśakavṛttāntaṃ brūhīti | tataḥ śuko babhāṣe | śṛṇu śravaṇālaṃkaraṇavāṇi | tārakarā<lb>lābhighāṭavī | tatra kuṭilanāmā pañcānanaḥ | sa tu sarvānapi 'pi bhavadīyāḥ prajāḥ | tvatpurastādāpatitaṃ sarvamapi mārayasi <lb> trayaḥ santu catvāro vā | tarhi bhavataivaṃ vidhātavyamatyantamanucitam | tvayā ca sarvadā svaguhāyāmā<lb>sīnena sthātavyam | samāyātaḥ | sa tu śaśako <lb> vegādeva bhojanāvasare na tatparisaraṃ sarati sma | tadanu bhojanasamayamatikramya gatavān | tadā siṃhasta<lb>mavekṣya kopaparavaśaḥ prahartumudatiṣṭhat | tarhi tvaṃ paścātpatatriṇamaprākṣīt | śuko 'pyabhyadhāt | śṛṇu prabhāvati | siṃhasya peṭākapolālikopari <lb> yāvatā patati tāvatā śaśakaḥ śaśaṃsa | deva devaprabho mahārāja madīyamekamuttaramākarṇaya | tava manasi <lb> jātaḥ kulasamanvitaḥ kaścidabhimānaviśeṣo 'sti na vā | asti cettadānīṃ madīyamabhimataṃ sādaraṃ <lb> samākarṇaya | ahaṃ tu madhyaṃdina evāgato 'bhavam | tvadanyaḥ pañcānano madhyemārgaṃ nindāmākarṇayitumaśaknuvānastvadupāntamāsedivān | deva eva pramāṇamityabhyadhāt | <lb> tataḥ pūrvaṃ kadācidapyakuṇṭhitakhaṇḍitavikramo jaṭharānalakavalitakalevaraḥ kaṇṭhīravastadupakaṇṭhaṃ jigamiṣuḥ <lb> śaśakamavādīt | apratihatapratāpe mayi mahāraṇyaparivṛḍhe jāgarūke ko vātmanīnakarmā paripanthiko <lb> matsamānakarmā jāgarti | pradarśaya taṃ durātmano mārgamidānīmeva | kopāveśātiśayena pañcānano vāpyāmapatat | vāpyāṃ patitvā nakharāyudho maraṇamāsedivāt | tatratyāni <lb> sarvaṇyapi sattvāni sukhena sthātuṃ pravartante || <lb>
<pb n="365">
buddhiryasya balaṃ tasya durbuddhestu kuto balam |
paśya siṃhaṃ madonmattaṃ śaśakena nipātitam ||

365,6

tarhi prabhāvati yadīdṛśaṃ buddhiviśeṣamīśiṣe tadā yāhi || <lb> iti catvāriṃśatkathā || 40 || <lb>

365,8

punaḥ prabhāvatī praśnaparā prāvartata | śuko 'pyabhyadhāt | devi trailokyasundarīvāyāsanistaraṇapratibhāmudbhā<lb>vayasi yadi tadā yātu bhavatī | tadā prabhāvatī tadvṛttāntamaprākṣītpakṣiṇaṃ so 'pi apāṃsulāṃ puṣpaṇīṃ ca balādbhuṅge naro hi yaḥ |

365,32

tataste madekadevatāyā ramaṇasya cāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhirbhūyādato yathāgataṃ gaccha gaccha | yadi māmīdṛśīṃ <lb> punaḥ punaḥ spṛśasi cettadā gāḍhamudghoṣayāmīti | tato bahubuddhimānnāma vaiśyaḥ svakāntājalpitamākarṇya <lb> mañcādhastādutthito bhāryāṃ sānandamudvīcya yato madāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhyarthamīdṛśamapi karmāpāṃsulayā bhavatyā<lb>caritamato 'smatkuladevatāyāḥ paraṃ rūpaṃ tvamiti tāṃ praśaṃsayaṃstasyāścaraṇayoḥ śirasābhivandanaṃ vidhāya <pb> punaḥ punarānandodrekeṇa nanarta | tataḥ svācaritāsādhukarmagūhanacaturā suratasundarī svairaṃ vicacāra | tarhi <lb> prabhāvati tvamapīdṛśamupāyaṃ jānīṣe yadi tadā yātu bhavatī || <lb> iti ekacatvāriṃśatkathā || 41 || <lb>

366,4

tataḥ punaḥ prabhāvatī vinayakandarpasamīpaṃ jigamiṣuḥ śukaṃ giramudbhāvayituṃ pravavṛte | tadanu tāṃ śuko <lb> 'vadat | he kaumudi mūladevavatsaṃkīrṇopaplave samāpatite tanniḥsaraṇāya prasarati 366,26

tataḥ prabhāvatī paṭīrapārihāryādibhirātmānamalaṃkṛtya vinayakandarpaniketanaṃ gantumājagāma | tatastāṃ śuko <lb> 'bravīt | devi ratilīlāvatsaṃkoce samāpatite yadi kartumuttaraṃ pārayasi tadā tasmingoṣṭhīkaraṇasamaye tāvatā grāmādhipaḥ karṣakaḥ samāgacchati sma | taṃ tvāyāntamavekṣya veṇukaviracite <lb> kusūlamadhye vipaṇinandanaṃ pracikṣepa sā | tadupari pidhānakamakārṣīt | tatastaṃ kuṭumbinaṃ gṛhāntaḥ praveśayā<lb>māsa | tenāpi samaṃ sukhagoṣṭhī vidhātavyā | tāvatā kṣapāpālaḥ samāyātaḥ | tadā sa kṛṣīvalo 'pyabibhet | <pb> tataḥ sā ratilīlā taṃ kṛṣīvalaṃ kusūlasya pidhānopari tadanu niśīthinīpālakaṃ gṛhāntaraṃ nināya | yāvatāsāvupaviśati <lb> tāvatā senānāyako 'pyāyayau | tadā rātricaritaṃ racitapatatrikukṣau cikṣepa | tadanu senādhipaṃ tamantara<lb>naiṣīt | yāvatāsāvantaḥ mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ tu yatkṛtam |

367,23

tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyetādṛśamuttaraṃ kartuṃ pragalbhase yadi tadāśraya || <lb> iti tricatvāriṃśatkathā || 43 || <lb>

368,14

iti vicārapadavīmavagāhamānā tanmānasaṃ caritārthayati sma | tathā ca vyavasite nijapaṭīpaṭīyasīṃ <lb> cintāṃ cikīrṣuḥ kiṃcitkālamasthāt | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyabhidhehi | kenopāyaprakalpanena sa govindo <lb> nijāṃ prāvaraṇapaṭīyasīṃ paṭīmapāhārṣīt | iti patatrisamabhihitaṃ tadavagatya prabhāvatyapi vicāradṛśā <lb> cāru cintayantī na tadupāyacāturyaṃ svacetanāyāmāsādayati sma | tadanu kṣaṇadāpyakṣīyata prabhāte ca <lb> nabhogaṃ prabhāvatyabhāṣiṣṭa | mayā tu nāvabudhyate | khaga tvametadupāyanirmāṇamācakṣva | tadā śuko 'pi <lb> cakkāṇa | tadā prabhāvati sa govindo digambaro 'mbaramaṇitāpātiśayasphuṭamastakakaroṭīpradeśa eva <lb> drāgājagāma grāmam | tatra ca grāmadvāri grāmamukhyāḥ pañcaṣāḥ pañcajanahitānusaraṇasariṇipārīṇāḥ <lb> sakalayācakayāñcāpratyarpaṇakalāpārīṇā nyavātsuḥ | kaupīnamātradhanaḥ sa tu tānālokyāñjalimabadhnāt | <lb> avahitakarṇā bhavantu bhavantaḥ | dūrādāgacchannuttareṇa mārgeṇa kṣetraṃ samīkṣya bahudhā bādhamānāṃ bubhukṣāṃ <lb> ca nirīkṣya kṣīṇakaraṇagaṇo vālukaphalayugalamahamagrahīṣam | tāvatā padavīmetāṃ avidam | tadanu mañca<lb>madhyāruhya kṣetraṃ rakṣantī mahilā mañcādavaruhya madīyaṃ vastramagrahīt | ahaṃ śrīdvārakāṃ gatvā śrīkṛṣṇa<lb>darśanaṃ vidhāya punarnijagrāmaṃ vrajannasmi | vastrābhāvādanāvṛtāṅgo 'smyaham | tarhi madīyaṃ sicayaṃ dāpaya<lb>tetyabhidhāya samaṃ teṣāṃ purastādupāvikṣadasau | tataste tasya haste vastramadāpayan | te grāmādhīśāstasyai <lb> akrudhyan | sa ca brāhmaṇastaiḥ prasthāpito nijanagaramārgamanvasarat | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapīdṛśopāyā<lb>nusaṃdhānaṃ bobudhoṣi yadi tadā sukhena sādhaya || <lb> iti catuścatvāriṃśatkathā || 44 || <lb>

369,21

punaḥ prabhāvatī iyāsuruparamaṇasamīpaṃ pakṣiṇaṃ paryacinot | tadā so 'pyavadat | re buddhimatīvottaraṃ <lb> vyatyayituṃ yadi nāṭayasi tadā sādhyatāṃ nāma | tadā prabhāvatī babhāṣe | buddhimatī 370,16

punaḥ prabhāvatī nijapreṣyopakaṇṭhaṃ jigamiṣuḥ khagaṃ vīkṣate sma | tadiṅgitajñaḥ śuko vyācaṣṭe | devi halapā<lb>lavadāpatite parābhiyoge yadi vijñānaviśeṣāṅgīkāreṇa pareṣāmanyathātvasphuraṇaṃ 371,4

tataḥ punaḥ prabhāvatī vinayakandarpasamīpamiyāsuḥ pataṃgapuṃgavamavocat | so 'pyavadat | devi priyaṃvadavadupā<lb>yāntaraṃ prapañcayasi yadi tato 'bhiyuṅkṣva | sā kīdṛk caritamiti śukamanvayuṅkta | kurvantu paścā<lb>tsvagṛhamaṅgīkurvantu | tadānīmasau tatraiva sarvaṃ prītyavasādanāyāvasānaṃ cakāra | tadanu gṛhāgamanasamaye <lb> dhanikasya pumapatyaṃ dvāri dīpyatkavyāmadhiropya sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ nijagṛhānuddiśya niragāt | tadanvādāya <lb> tadapatyaṃ bhūmigṛhe sthāpitavān | iti tadapatyasya mātṛpitṛsakhibandhuvarga anvīkṣaṇāya prayatate | tadapatyaṃ <lb> na dṛśyata ityudghoṣaḥ sarvatrāpi prasarīsarīti sma | tadā tatprativeśinī mahilā vyāharat | bhavatāṃ yaḥ <lb> prāhuṇikaḥ samāgataḥ sa bhavadīyamapatyaṃ gṛhītvā gatavān | tataste dhāvamānāḥ tadgṛhānagacchan | tatra <lb> gatvā tamaprākṣuḥ | tato 'bhyadhādasau | mayā bhavadīyamapatyaṃ nāgrāhīti | tayorvivadatornabhaḥspṛśaḥ śabdaḥ <lb> prādurabhūt | tau dvāvapi vargau vivadamānau rājakulamagātām | sa tu kimuttaramakārṣīt | tataḥ prabhāvatī vicāradattacittāpi <lb> taduttaraṃ nākalayat | tadānīṃ śukamukhena taduttaramāviracīkaratprabhāvatī | tadānīmasau rājānaṃ vyaji<lb>jñapat | ahametadīyaṃ taduttaraṃ <lb> niśamya sarve 'pi te bhūsuparvasahitā nirvarṇanaparāstadurvīpatisacivāstadapūrvamapūrvamiti vyākurvāṇā<lb>ścamankurvate | tvaṃ kimetaduktamasamañjasaṃ bhāṣase | viṣkilaḥ tulāṃ lohasahasrasya yatra khādanti mūṣikāḥ |
gajaṃ tatra harecchyenaḥ kā kathā vada dārake ||

tataste punarevamavādiṣurvidvāṃsaḥ | tvaṃ kimetadabhidadhāno 'si | ¿śrṛ¿juvacobhirāvedaya | tadanu tulāvṛttā<lb>ntamāditaḥprabhṛti tebhyo nyavīvidat | tadanu medinīnāyakastadvṛttāntāvagamāduttamarṇāyākrudhyat | tadīyāṃ <lb> laurhī tulāṃ tasmai dāpayāmāsa | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyetādṛśopāyaracanaṃ prapañcayasi yadi tadānīṃ <lb> svakāryasādhane dhṛtāvadhānā bhava || <lb> ityaṣṭacatvāriṃśatkathā || 48 || <lb>

371,35

punaḥ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ pratyāha | devi mantrasārabrāhmaṇavatsaṃkocāpāte nistarituṃ yadi pārayasi <lb> tadānīṃ sādhaya samīhitam | tataḥ prabhāvatī pratyuvāca | mantrasāraḥ kathaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ 372,32

punaḥ prabhāvatī jāravasatiṃ sisīrṣuḥ śakuniṃ praśnātithīcakāra | śuko 'bhyadhāt | devi bālakṛṣṇavaduttara<lb>vinimayaṃ kartumīśiṣe yadi tadānīmādaro vidhīyatām | prabhāvatī jagāda śukam | tadbhavānbālakṛṣṇottara<lb>vinimayacaritaṃ brūhīti | tadānīṃ śukaḥ provāca | govardhananagare lakṣmīnārāyaṇasya mahānprāsādo 'sti | <lb> tasya paricaryākaro devadharanāmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya pañcavarṣīyaḥ putraḥ | tasya bālakṛṣṇa iti nāmadheyam | <lb> tasya jananī saṃtasthau | paścāddevadharaḥ pramotabhāryaḥ punarapyātmānamudvāhitavān | sā ca bālakṛṣṇasya sapatnī <lb> jananī bālakṛṣṇaṃ sarvadaivāvajānīte | tasyānnaudanādisaukaryamapi na karoti | tadānīṃ bālakṛṣṇastatkṛtā<pb>vajñānaṃ pituragre proktavān | tadāsau tasyāḥ prītyā putrāvajñāparihāraviṣayaṃ na kimapi vyāharati <lb> sma | iti sati sa bālakṛṣṇo 'pyacintayat | ataḥ paraṃ kaḥ prakāraḥ kartavyaḥ | pitāpi tāvadasmadīyaṃ <lb> pāramatyaṃ niravadati etasyāḥ prītiprakarṣollāsena | tasyai hi snehasyāsya bhaṅgopāyamāracayāmi | etāvatā <lb> prayojanamidamasmadīyaṃ svata eva setsyati | tadanvekasmindine bālakṛṣṇo nijajanakamabhivīkṣya tatsaṃ<lb>nidhānaṃ gatvā babhāṣe | tāta tava purastātkiṃ vyāharāmi | pitrābhidhatsveti bhaṇite jagāda bālakṛṣṇaḥ | <lb> asmākaṃ dvitīyo janako 'sti | yathā tvaṃ karoṣi tathaivāsau karoti pratyaham | tadā vyājahāra janakaḥ | <lb> tamapi mahyamekadā darśayiṣyasi | bālakṛṣṇo lalāpa | kasmiṃściddivase tubhyamapi darśayiṣyāmītyabhidhāya <lb> maunamevāste | tadanu devadharasya hṛdaye vicikitsodiyāya | manogatamuvāca | strīṇāṃ caritraṃ ko nāma <lb> jñātumīṣṭe | na kasyāpi striyo 'vaśyaṃ vaśyā bhaveyuḥ | <lb>

śāstraṃ suniścitadhiyāmapi cintanīyamārādhito 'pi nṛpatiḥ pariśaṅkanīyaḥ |

373,14

apatyaṃ yatkimapi vadati so 'pi śabdo na nirmalo bhavitumarhati | tasya kathaṃcidabhiprāyo vidyate | <lb> iti manasi niścitya tasyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ purātanīṃ prītiṃ parihṛtya gālīvitaraṇatāḍanādinātiroṣabhāvaṃ <lb> prāduṣkṛtya pravartamāno 'sti | tadā tasya bhāryā vicāradattacittā prāvartata | mamoparyetādṛśo 'nanya<lb>sādhāraṇapremāsya patyurāsīt | sa tvetasya bālakṛṣṇavyasanena parāhataḥ | tasmādamumevābhyakṣayāmi | tato <lb> yathā hyayaṃ sādhurbhavati tathā kaṃcana prakāraṃ kariṣyāmi | tataḥ sā taṃ bālakṛṣṇaṃ saṃnidhāvājuhāva | <lb> tadanvavādīcca | tvaṃ madīyastātaḥ | yadā mama śreyaḥ kariṣyasi tadānīṃ tava samohitaṃ kariṣyāmi | tato <lb> 'bhyadhādvālakṛṣṇaḥ | tava kutratyaṃ śreyaḥ | itthameva bhavatyā bhavati | etāvantaṃ kālaṃ mama na kāṃcana cintāṃ <lb> kṛtavatyasi | tadā sāpyabhāṇīt | ataḥ prabhṛtyārya tvadīyāṃ paricaryāṃ samyakkariṣyāmi | yatkimapi ramyaṃ <lb> tadbhavate vitarāmi | etasminviṣaye madīyamasti sukṛtaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ ca prayacchāmi | tadā sa bālakṛṣṇaḥ <lb> tasyāḥ śreyonirmāṇaṃ svīkṛtavān | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapi vicāraya | sa bālakṛṣṇaḥ pūrvoditaṃ vacanaṃ <lb> kathaṃ vinimayati sma | tadā prabhāvatī vicāraṇāya prāvartata paraṃ nāvajagāma | tadānīṃ pakṣiṇamaprā<lb>kṣīt | so 'pyāha | prabhāvati tadānīṃ sa bālakṛṣṇaḥ pitaramāsīnamabhivīkṣya svayamapi tadupakaṇṭhamā<lb>gādityabhāṣiṣṭa | tātāsmadīyaṃ dvitīyaṃ janakaṃ bhavato darśayiṣyāmi | tadānīmabhyadhādasau | darśayeti | <lb> ityabhidhāya darpaṇamānīya pāṇināgrahītpiturabhimukhaṃ sthāpitavān | tatratyaṃ pratibimbamadarśayat | jagāda <lb> cedam | ekastvaṃ janako dvitīyo 'yaṃ janakaḥ | pāṇimacālayat | tadānīṃ pratibimbasyāpi vepate sma <lb> pāṇiḥ | tataścāvocat | idaṃ tatsa bhavati | yathaiva bhavānkurvāṇo 'sti tathaivāyamapi karoti | tadānīṃ <lb> tadudīraṇāttasya manaḥsthito vikalpaḥ paryakṣīyata | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapītthamuttaraṃ vyatyayasi yadi <lb> tadānīṃ sādhayātmānaṃ svamanorathasādhanāya || <lb> iti pañcāśatkathā || 50 || <lb>

373,33

punaḥ prabhāvatī pakṣiṇaṃ praśnayati sma | tato 'vadadasāvapi | devi prabhāvati bahubuddhiḥ prakṛtiḥ pā<lb>rthivasyāyāsamapacakāra | tādṛśaṃ yuktiviśeṣaṃ prayuṇakti bhavatī yadi tadānīṃ pārthakyena kimāpattiṣṭhatītyabhidhāya mahīpaterākāṅkṣāmapoṣayat | tadā rājā pradhānaṃ vyādideśa | <lb> pradoṣasamaye tvayaināṃ gṛhītvā samāgantavyamamuṣminpradeśaviśeṣe | tadā rājādeśaṃ śirasyādhāya niragā<lb>tsacivaḥ | tarhyācakṣva prabhāvati tamupāyam | kena prakāreṇa paryahārṣīdamātyaḥ | tataḥ śukoktyā prabhāvatī <lb> vicārasamarpitahṛdayābhavat | punarnāvāgacchat | tataḥ śukamaprākṣītso 'pi nyavādīt | prabhāvati tadānīṃ <lb> sacivaḥ pārthivena pūrvaṃ parihṛtāyā rājñyāḥ samīpaṃ saṃprāpya tāmavocat | adya bhavatīnāṃ viṣaye naranātho <lb> smābhirvijñaptaḥ saṃbhūya sarvairapi rājño 'pi mānase yathā bhavatīṣu sneha utpadyate tathaiva samāpādayā<lb>mahi | bhavatībhyaścitraśālaikā dāpitā vidyate | bhavatībhiradya kṛtaprasādhanābhiḥ pradoṣasamaye tatra gantavyam | <lb> ityabhidhāya citraśālāyāmetasyāṃ saṃdhyāsamaye tāmanaiṣīdamātyavṛddhaḥ | tasyai rājñyai mātaṅgyā iva vastrāṇi <lb> tādṛśamevālaṃkāraṃ pradāyābhidadhau | tatra rājā bhavatībhyo vasanāni bhūṣaṇāni ca dattvā prātiṣṭhipat | <lb> iti tatratyamaśeṣaṃ vidheyaviśeṣaṃ sajjīkṛtya niragādagādhabuddhiḥ | tadanu gatvā rājānaṃ vyajijñapat | deva <lb> śrīmatā yadādiṣṭamabhūttatsarvamapi nirvartitam | tasyāṃ citraśālāyāṃ samānītāsti | sa tadanu rājā <lb> tatra gatavān | manmathapramathitamanā manorathaistāmajahāt | tadanu madanamārgaṇamohamahormivegabhaṅge vicā<lb>rapuraskṛto 'vanīśvarastadānīmeva citraśālāyā bahirniragamat | tadā sacivaṃ vyājahāra | māṃ mā <lb> sprākṣīḥ parato yāhīti | tataḥ saciva uvāca | kimetatsvāmin | tadābhāṇīddharaṇīnāthaḥ | mamaitā<lb>vānanarthaḥ samajīghaṭat | ataḥ paraṃ dehāvasānameva prāyaścittaṃ gṛhṇomahi | iti śrutvā tadocivānsacivaḥ | <lb> mayi saṃnidhānānusāriṇi yadi mahīnāthapramāda āpatiṣyati tadānīṃ so 'mātyaḥ kīdṛkprakāraḥ | <lb> samasto 'pyupāyo nirapāyatayā parihṛtasarpaḥ | tadā jagāda rājā sacivam | *** | tadānīṃ dīpamā<lb>nīya tāṃ rājñīṃ rājño locanagocarīṃ cakāra | tadālokya naranātho 'pi saṃtoṣaparavaśaḥ sthitavān | <lb> avocacca | bahubuddhināmadheyaṃ bhavata eva yujyate netarasya | tarhi prabhāvati buddhiviśeṣamevaṃ pariśīlayasi <lb> yadi tadānīṃ sādhaya || <lb> ityekapañcāśatkathā || 51 || <lb>
<pb n="374">

374,30

punaḥ prabhāvatī pṛṣṭavatī patatriṇam | tadanvasāvapyavocat | devi vyāghramāriṇīva saṃkīrṇanistaraṇe pragalbhase <lb> yadi tadānīmanusaṃdhatsva | tataḥ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ śuko vyāghrahantrīvṛttāntaṃ prabhāvatīmaśrāvayat | ākarṇaya <lb> prabhāvati | viśālapurābhidhānaṃ nagaram | tatra vicāravīro rājā | tasya karmakāro jagandhanāmadheyaḥ | <lb> tasya gṛhiṇī kalahapriyā vyāghrahantrī | sāharniśaṃ bhartrā samaṃ kalahaṃ karoti | bhartā yadā gṛhamāgacchati <lb> bhoktumupaviśati tāvatā tasminsamaye kiṃcidavidyamānameva kalahabījamupāsyati kṣaṇamātramapi sā <lb> sukhenāvasthātuṃ notsahate | <lb>
yasya bhāryā virūpākṣī kaśmalā kalahapriyā |
uttarottaravaktrī ca sā jarā na jarā jarā ||
<pb n="375">

375,1

ityabhidhāya sa tāṃ nirakāsayat | sa tāmapatyadvayasahitāṃ paryatyajat | parityāgavisaṃvidho na kaścana <lb> saṃbandho 'styataḥ paramityabhidhāya pradattavān | itthaṃ tadvisṛṣṭā sāpatyamekaṃ kaṭyāmabhiropyaikaṃ karāṅguli<lb>bhirādhṛtyāpatyadvayasahitā sānyasmingrāme mātṛmandiraṃ prati nirayāsīt | tato araṇyamadhye madhyāhne <lb> pathi gacchantī pariśrāntā kasyacidviṭapinastale niṣasāda | tatastāmabhivokṣya dūrādeva vyāghrastāṃ bhakṣa<lb>yituṃ samāgatavān | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapi cāru vicāraya | etādṛśe samaye kamupāyamakarotsā | tadā <lb> prabhāvatī vicāraṇāya prāvartata | na tadupāyaṃ kalayāmāsa | tāvatā tamasvinyapi prākṣīyata | tadā <lb> prabhāte prabhāvatī tadupāyāviṣkaraṇāya śukamanuyuktavatī | so 'pi tadvyāharaṇāya kṛtaprayatno 'bhavat | <lb> prabhāvatyākarṇaya | tadā citrakāyamāyāntaṃ lakṣīcakāra | tadā tadapatyadvayamapi peḍayā tāḍayāmāsa | <lb> tattāḍanapīḍitaṃ dvayamapyarudat | tatastadrodanaśamanāya svayaṃ putrāvavocat | ahaṃ tāvadvyāghrahantrī yena <lb> kenāpi prakāreṇa citrakāyadvayaṃ nihatya bhavatorāhārāya paryāptaṃ pūrayiṣyāmi | yāvatā dvitīyo <lb> dvīpī samāgacchati tāvatainamevāgacchantaṃ mayā nihataṃ vibhajya bhakṣayatamityabhidhāya tasya puṇḍarīkasya <lb> khaṇḍanāyākhaṇḍanavikramāpatyadvayaṃ tatra bhuvi vyavasthāpyodatiṣṭhata | tadvacanākarṇanasamanantarameva mṛgārirjīvaṃ <lb> gṛhītvā palāyamāno niragāt | tvamapītthaṃ jānāsi cedyadi tadānīmanusara || <lb> iti dvipañcāśatkathā || 52 || <lb>

375,15

punaḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ praṣṭuṃ prāvartata | śuko babhāṣe | devi tasyā vyāghramāryā ivopāyāntaraprayoge cā<lb>turyamudeti bhavatyā yadi tadā gantavyaṃ bhavatyā | tataḥ prabhāvatī tadvṛttāntaṃ jijñāsuḥ papraccha śukam | so <lb> 'pyavocat | śṛṇu prabhāvati | śārdūlaḥ palāyamāno gacchannasti | tadā mārge kroṣṭā dṛṣṭavān | sa ca tarakṣuṃ <lb> babhāṣe | vyāghra devāḥ kimiti palāyamānā vartante | tadā vyāghro na vadati | tadā kroṣṭā vacanayukti<lb>bhistadbhayamapākṛtya sthirīkṛtavān citrakāyam | tava ca pṛṣṭhato na kiṃcidāgacchati | tvaṃ paśya | tvayi <lb> kimeṣa ākasmiko bhayaḥ samudāyamānastiṣṭhati | bhayaṃ jahīhi | matpurastādācakṣva | yatkiṃcidvaiṣamyamāti<lb>ṣṭhitamasti tadahaṃ yuktiviśeṣeṇāpakariṣyāmi | ityākarṇya dhairyamālambya kṣaṇaṃ tasthivānpuṇḍarīkaḥ | tasya <lb> purataścaritaṃ vyāghrahantryāḥ prākṛtaṃ kṛtavān | tatastacchrutvā mṛgadhūrto narīnarti sma giram | yāhi purataḥ | <lb> kena tvaṃ vyāghraḥ kṛto 'si | tattvāmahaṃ mūrkhamukhyamupalakṣaye | sā tvāṃ bhīṣayāmāsa | kutra mānuṣāścitrakāyaṃ <lb> mārayanti | tvaṃ vṛthaiva bhītavānasi | āgaccha gacchāvastasyāḥ punarantikam | tadānīmabhyadhāddvīpī | tasmādeva <lb> palāyase tayāhameva dhṛtvā nihantavyaḥ | tadā kroṣṭābhāṣiṣṭa | tvaṃ yadi māṃ palāyamānaṃ bruvāṇo 'si <lb> tarhyātmano gale māmānahya tāvatā tavāpi matpalāyanaśaṅkā nivartiṣyate | tadanantaramātmano gale <lb> sṛgālaṃ pinaddhavāñchārdūlaḥ | tato mṛgārihantrī tāvapyāgacchantau vīkṣate | prabhāvati tvamapi vicārya <lb> vyāhara | tadānīṃ vyāghraturā kamupāyaṃ prākalpayat | tataḥ prabhāvatī prabhātaṃ pratibhāsāprabhavapratibhāvitaṃ <lb> vidhāya yadā taduttararahasyaṃ na kalayāmāsa tadā śukaṃ papraccha sotkaṇṭhā | avadacchukaḥ | ākarṇaya <lb> prabhāvati | sā dvīpijagdhinī mṛgadhūrtaṃ mṛgārimāgacchantamālokya kroṣṭāramabhāṣiṣṭa | are kroṣṭo pūrva<lb>smindine tvaṃ matpurastādātmanaḥ satyasukṛtaṃ dattvā garīyasīmājñāmapi vidhāya gato 'bhūḥ | tarhīdānīṃ <lb> kimityekameva dvīpinaṃ tvamānaiṣīḥ | ekena vyāghreṇaikasyāpatyasyodaramāpūryate | tadā dvitīyamapatyaṃ kiṃ <lb> tvāṃ bhakṣayiṣyati | iti vacanaṃ vyāghro 'śrauṣīt | tadanantaraṃ palāyanamevākarot | tarhi prabhāvati tvama<lb>pyupāyaviśeṣaṃ pariśīlayasi yadi tadānīmanuyāhi || <lb> iti tripañcāśatkathā || 53 ||
<pb n="376">

376,1

punarvyājahāra patatriṇaṃ prabhāvatī | śuko 'bravīt | tasya kroṣṭoriva yadyātmana uparyāāpatitasya maraṇopadravasya <lb> parihāropāyaṃ pariśīlayasi yadi tadānīmanumanyasva svakṛtyasamarthanam | tadākarṇya jagāda prabhāvatī | koṣṭā <lb> kīdṛgvidhaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ nistīrṇavān | tadvṛttāntaṃ vāvadotu bhavān | iti prabhāvatyābhihito vihago giramujja<lb>gāra | ākarṇaya devi | dvīpī tu vegenātmano maraṇabhayātpalāyamāno 'bhavat | kroṣṭā tu tatkaṇṭhe nibaddhaḥ <lb> kaṇṭakavisaṃkaṭāyāmākṛṣyamāṇo gātrasya samagrāmapi tvacamutkṛttya caraṇābaddhabādho bhūmerupari samā<lb>kṛṣyate | tadā tādṛśāvasthāmupabhuñjānaḥ kṣaṇamātrādasavo nijā nirgamiṣyantotyetādṛśīmavasthāṃ prāptavān | <lb> jīvaśeṣāvasthāmavalambamāno vidyate | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyabhidhehi | tadānīṃtane tādṛśe samaye sa jambuko <lb> dvīpigalabaddhamātmānaṃ prakāreṇa kenodamocayat | tataḥ prabhāvatī taccintayantī na viveda jambukamocanopā<lb>yam | tadā dinodaye papraccha patatriṇaṃ vyājahāra kīro 'pi | tadā kaṇṭakāṭavīmadhye samutkṛṣyamāṇaḥ <lb> kroṣṭā vihasyāvocat | tadā vyāghro babhāṣe | sṛgāla kasmādasminsamaye hāsyāspadaṃ māṃ kṛtavānasi | <lb> jambuko jagāda | tvadīyaṃ maurkhyamabhivīkṣya mama hāsyamajāyata | tato vyāhārṣīccitratanuḥ | kathaṃ mayi tvaṃ <lb> maurkhyamāsañjasi | sṛgālo 'vadat | yatra yatra tvaṃ gamiṣyasi tatra tatra vyāghrahantrī samāgacchati | tvāmavaśyaṃ <lb> bhakṣayiṣyati | tadā vyāghro vyājahāra | tvamityaṃ kena jānīṣe | tadā jagāda jambukaḥ | madīyāsṛgaktaṃ mārgaṃ <lb> dṛṣṭvā viditavidvadgatiravaśyamāgamiṣyati vyāghraghātinī | sā samāgatyāvaśyaṃ tvāṃ mārayiṣyati | itthaṃ jā<lb>nīhi | yadi bhavato jijīviṣā ca varīvartti tadānīmātmano galabaddhaṃ muñca mām | itthaṃ jambukavacanaṃ <lb> viśvasya puṇḍarīkastatkṣaṇaṃ galasthitaṃ mṛgadhūrtamavamucyāpāsaradanyena vartmanā | tarhi prabhāvati upāyamevaṃ<lb>vidhaṃ yadi bhavatī vetti tadāna gamanamaṅgokuru || <lb> iti catuḥpañcāśatkathā || 54 || <lb>

376,19

punaḥ prabhāvatī iyāsuruparamaṇasamīpaṃ nagaukasaṃ jagāda so 'pyavadat | devi viṣṇuvardhanavadātmanaḥ prati<lb>pakṣabhūtaṃ yadi parābhavituṃ jānāsi tadā yāhi | tataḥ prabhāvatī vyāhārṣīt | tadvṛttāntamācaṣṭāmiti <lb> pakṣiṇam | tadanu śuko 'bravīt | kanyākubjānāmni nagare kaścidviṣṇuvardhano brāhmaṇaḥ | sa ca surato<lb>pabhoge 'tilampaṭaścaṇḍaśca | tasminkanyākubje na kācana kāminī kamanīyaguṇā tadīyaṃ grāmyadharmaṃ sahate | <lb> tasminnetādṛśasāmarthye prathāmurīkaroti sma | etādṛśavāravilāsinīparivādapṛthuprathākāraṇajāgarūkā <lb> ratipradhānā kācana gaṇikā gaṇarātrāntaraṃ kasyāṃcinniśīthinyāṃ tamājuhāva | tadāhvānasamaye viṣṇu<lb>vardhano 'bravīt | ratipriye tvayāsmadīyaṃ surataṃ soḍhuṃ na śakyate | yadi tvaṃ na sahase tadā rātrinivā<lb>saparimitaṃ paṇaṃ dviguṇaṃ bhavatyāḥ sakāśādahaṃ grahīṣyāmi | tadā tatkuṭṭinī tadīyamiti vacanīyaṃ <lb> svīkṛtya rātrinivāsaparimitaṃ paṇaṃ tasmādagrahīt | sa tu tasyāṃ tamasvinyāṃ ratipriyopabhogāya nyavā<lb>tsīt | tadanu rātrau garīyaḥ kaṣṭaṃ pravartamānamabhūdratipriyāyāḥ | tadanu mūtrotsarjanamiṣeṇa tacchayyāyā <lb> utthāya kuṭṭinīsaṃnidhānaṃ gatvā ratipriyā tāmevamavādīt | etadīyaṃ dhanametasmai pratyarpaya | mama prā<lb>ṇāvasānapiśunaṃ nidhuvanametadīyaṃ nidarśanamujjṛmbhate | tadāvadatkuṭṭinī | mriyasva janakajāye | haste prāptaṃ <lb> paṇaṃ kathaṃ vā pratyarpyate | tarhi paṇyāṅganānāṃ madhye tava ko nāma nāma grahīṣyati | tvaṃ punastadantikaṃ <lb> yāhi | tatkṣaṇamātramupacāracāturyeṇa taṃ ramaya | paścādahaṃ tarumimamāruhya kukkuṭaninadaṃ bahudhā kariṣyā<lb>mi | tatastvaṃ prabhātaṃ saṃjātamityabhidhāyātmanaḥ samīpāttaṃ gamaya | tata iti kṛtaniścayā ratipriyā <lb> viṣṇuvardhanopakaṇṭhamāgatya punaḥ suratopacāraistaṃ siṣeve | tataḥ kuṭṭinī dvāri vidyamānaṃ bilvamadhiruhya <lb> tāmracūḍaninādānbahudhā cakāra | tadā tanninādaśravaṇādratipriyā vyājahāra priyam | idānīṃ prabhā<lb>tasamayaḥ prāvartiṣṭa | bhavantastu gacchadhvamityabhidhāya ratipriyā nirajīgamat | tarhi prabhāvati bhavatyapi <lb> vicāryabhidadhātu | viṣṇuvardhanastu tataḥ paraṃ kiṃ vyaracayat | sā tadvicāraṃ kurvāṇāpi nājñāsīt | tadā <pb> śukaṃ papraccha | śuko 'pi nijagāda | śṛṇu prabhāvati | viṣṇuvardhanastu dvārādbahiraṅgaṇabhāge sthitvā yā<lb>vatā paśyati tāvatā rātrimapi garīyasīṃ nyaphālayat | tadānīṃ dvitīyavāraṃ kuṭṭino kukkuṭaninādaṃ <lb> karoti sma | tadā so 'pi taccaritamadrākṣīt | tato viṣṇuvardhanaḥ karāśmabhiḥ tarusthitāṃ kuṭṭinīṃ <lb> nihatya bhūtale nipātitavān | tadākrandamānā papāta | tadā ratipriyāpi taddeśamāgatavatī | sā rati<lb>priyā taṃ viṣṇuvardhanaṃ kṣamasveti pādayorapatat | tvamātmīyaṃ draviṇaṃ punargṛhāṇa paramasmāsu kṛpāmutpā<lb>daya | ityabhidhāya tadīyaṃ draviṇaṃ punarasmai pratyarpayāmāsa | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyupāyaviśeṣaṃ pariśī<lb>layasi yadi tadānīṃ dhvaṃsatām || <lb> iti pañcapañcāśatkathā || 55 || <lb>
<pb n="377">

377,9

punaḥ prabhāvatī pṛcchati sma nabhaścaram | tataḥ so 'pi babhāṣe | devi priyajalpakavadāyāsanistaraṇaṃ jā<lb>nīṣe yadi tadānīṃ samīhasva vidheyaviśeṣam | tadā prabhāvatī prājalpata | kiṃrūpamāyāsaṃ nistīrṇavā<lb>npriyajalpakaḥ | tadāvedayatutarāṃ bhavāniti tayā pṛṣṭaḥ śuko babhāṣe | avadhehi prabhāvati | āśāpūrā <lb> nāma devatā | tatratyaḥ paricaryākaraḥ priyajalpakaḥ | tasya bhāryā karkaśānāmadheyā | sāharniśaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ <lb> nūtanaṃ kalahamudbhāvayati muhūrtamapi kalahavihīnā nāvatiṣṭhati | tasya dvāri pippalatarureko nivasati | <lb> tasmiṃstarau graha eko nivasati | sa grahastasyāḥ karkaśāyā aśrāntakalahavigrahaparigṛhītavigraho durgrahagrasta <lb> iva parityaktanijagṛho dhāvanamakārṣīt | tato grāmādbahiḥsthitaṃ śalmalīviṭapinamekamadhiruhya tasthivān | <lb> itthaṃ bahubhirahobhiḥ priyajalpakasya manasi karkaśākalahadūṣite vairāgyamudayati sma | gṛhiṇīṃ parityajya <lb> deśatyāgaṃ cikīrṣitavānpriyajalpakaḥ | tato 'sau nirgacchandṛṣṭavānpuradvāri tamātmano 'ṅgaṇatarusthitaṃ <lb> graham | sa ca grahastasya priyajalpakasya pratyakṣo babhūva priyajalpakamaprākṣīt | tvaṃ jigamiṣurasi | tadā <lb> priyajalpako jajalpa | ahaṃ mama brāhmaṇyā palāyamāno 'smi | tadā priyajalpakaśca tamavādīt | tvaṃ <lb> ko nāma | tato graheṇābhyadhāyi | bhavadgṛhadvāristhite pippalatarau nyavatsamaham | tatratyo 'nādisiddho <lb> 'grajanmagrahaḥ sādhumantravādibhirapi nivāryamāṇo nāhaṃ nirgatavān | so 'haṃ bhavadbrāhmaṇībhayena palā<lb>yanaparāyaṇaḥ sannatraiva nivasāmi | tarhīdaṃ bhayamajāyata | idānīṃ dvāvapi samaduḥkhinau nivasāvaḥ | <lb> ahamapi tavopakāraṃ kaṃcana kariṣyāmi | evaṃvidhastayoḥ satyavacananirṇayo 'jāyata | tadanu graho 'sā<lb>vekasyā rājakumāryāḥ samāviveśa śarīram | tadānīṃ taccikitsārthamaneke narendrā amilan | na kaścidapi <lb> grahamapākartuṃ prabhavati | iti sati sa priyajalpako brāhmaṇastatrāgacchat | rājānaṃ sametyāvocat | ahaṃ <lb> kumārīmullāghāṃ karomi | tadānīṃ jagāda rājā | yadi tvamasmadīyāṃ kumārīṃ nirupadravāṃ vidhāsyasi <lb> tadānīmapi tvāṃ draviṇapūrṇamardharājyabhājaṃ vidhāsyāmi | tadāsāvabhimukhaṃ kumāryā brāhmaṇo nirī<lb>kṣitavān | tasyāṃ ca yāminyāṃ catuṣkoṇāntarvartī catuḥṣaṣṭiyoginīmaṇḍalākāraṃ prakalpya ṣoḍaśabhiru<lb>pacārairdīpaśreṇībhiḥ parito bhrājamānaṃ naivedyaviśeṣaiḥ samyagabhipūjya ḍamaruninādāḍambarairambaraṃ pratidhva<lb>nibhirullekhya maṇimantrauṣadhavividhasāmagrīṃ vidhātuṃ prāvartata | tadā graho 'pi tasya nirmāṇāḍambaraṃ <lb> nirīkṣya krodhaparavaśastasthau svamanasyabhyadhācca | ayaṃ svacāturoparītamevaṃvidhaṃ saṃbhramaṃ nirmimāṇo 'sti | <lb> paśyāmi tāvadidametadīyaṃ sāmarthyamityabhidhāyāsau grahaḥ kenāpi prakāraviśeṣeṇa na tyajati kumā<lb>rīm | tarhyācakṣva prabhāvati | sa brāhmaṇastadānīṃ kataramupāyamakalpayat | prabhāvatī tadvicāraṇāya bahudhā <lb> ityevaṃvidhaṃ <lb> mantra japannasau tiṣṭhati yāvattadā brahmagrahasyodiyāya karuṇā | tadā graho 'pyavādīt | ahamenāṃ kumārīṃ <lb> vihāya yāsyāmi | tannimittaṃ bhavate yatkimapi vitariṣyati rājā 378,6

punarapi niśāsamaye prabhāvatī vinayakandarpaniveśanamiyāsuḥ vihaṃgamaṃ vākprasaṃgatamacīkarat | niśamya <lb> tadā tāṃ prati vihaṃgo 'pyagāhata girāṃ paricayam | devi tasyaiva priyajalpakasya brāhmaṇasya puro <lb> patitaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ nistarituṃ pārayasi yadi tadā gantavyam | tataḥ prabhāvatī babhāṣe | sa kathaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ <lb> nistīrṇavān | iti tadvṛttāntamāvedayatu nāma bhavān | so 'yavocat | prabhāvati sa tvasau priyajalpako <lb> jagatīpativitīrṇavibhavasamudbhavaparipūrṇatayā sukhena sthātuṃ prāvartata | rājā ca rājyasyārdhaṃ prādāt | <lb> iti satyasau brāhmagraho 'nyasya rājakumārasya kalevaraṃ prāvikṣat | tadānīṃ tasya mahībhṛto manuṣyāḥ <lb> samāgatāstaṃ mantravādinamāhvātum | tadā sa rājā prāsthāpayattam | sa tatra gatavān | tatra tasya grahasya <lb> darśanamaghaṭiṣṭa | tato 'sau jagāda grahaḥ | are priyajalpaka mayā tvaṃ vārito 'pi tarhi kasmādatrāgato <lb> 'si | idānīṃ tvāmevāhaṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmi prathamam | tarhi prabhāvati vāvadītu bhavatī | tadā kimuttaraṃ <lb> vidhāya grahavigrahānmocitavānātmānam | tadā vicāraṇāya pravartate sma paraṃ tu na taduttaramajñāsīt | <lb> tadā śukamanuyuktavatī | tadā jagāda vihagaḥ | devi tadāsau priyajalpako grahaparigṛhītavigrahaṃ grahameva <lb> gatvāñjaliṃ baddhā vijñāpitumādṛtavān | prabho svāminkimiti bhavānamarṣito bhavati | ahamatraikena <lb> prayojanena samāgato 'smi | matpatnī karkaśā nāma māmatra sthitamākarṇya nijamandiraṃ parityajyātra <lb> matsaṃnidhānamāgatavatī | tarhi madīyaṃ mitrabhūtaṃ tvāmavagatya kāṃ buddhiṃ vidadhāmīti praṣṭumāgatavān | <lb> tarhi tvayā madvidhātavyā buddhirmahyamāvedanīyā | tadākarṇya babhāṣe grahaḥ | tvaṃ bhavaccittasamucitaṃ vidhehi | <lb> paramahaṃ tu sthānādetasmātpalāvya gamiṣyāmi pradeśāntaramityabhidhāya rājakumāraṃ samutthāpitavān | tadā <lb> so 'pi narapatistaṃ mantravādinaṃ yathārhamabhyarcayāmāsa | tarhi prabhāvati bhavatyapyetādṛśamāyāsamupāya<lb>viśeṣeṇa nistarasi yadi tadā yātu bhavatī || <lb> iti saptapañcāśatkathā || 57 || <lb>

378,25

punaḥ prabhāvatī śukamaprākṣīt | śuko 'pi vyāhārṣīt | devi śakalāṭamantrivanmaticāturyaṃ caritārthayasi <lb> yadi tataste jigamiṣā bhavatu | tadābravītprabhāvatī | śakalāṭaḥ kiṃrūpo matimatāṃ dhuri kathaṃ ślāghanīyaḥ | <lb> tadvṛttāntamanalpamākalpakalitakalevaro jalpatu pratibhāvitīrṇamānasaḥ | tadā śuko 'bravīt | ākarṇaya <lb> karṇaviśrāntalocane | śakalāṭo 'sau mantrī nandamahīpālasya | sa tu buddhimatāṃ dhuri dhaureyaḥ | itthaṃ tasya <lb> tathāvidhāṃ prasiddhiṃ niśamya samya¿ktvā¿samya¿ktva¿parīkṣānirīkṣaṇāya vaḍabādvayaṃ na kutrāpyavayavaviśeṣe 'pi <lb> sādṛśyādavidyamānaṃ rūpato varṇataḥ svabhāvata ākārataśca prasthāpayāmāsa darśanapātanaṃ vidhāyānyaja<lb>napadasya parivṛḍha ityabhidhāyaitayordvayormadhye kā nāma jananī tanayā ca kā | iti vivecanaṃ vidhā<lb>yāsmabhyaṃ jñāpayitavyamiti | tataste āgate abhivīkṣya sarve 'pyahamahamityātmani parīkṣāvaicakṣaṇyaṃ bibhrāṇāḥ <lb> parivārya vokṣituṃ prāvartiṣanta paraṃ na kaścana nirṇetumīṣṭe | rājā tadā śakalāṭanāmānamamātyaṃ vyā<lb>hṛtavān | nirdhāro 'yaṃ bhavataiva vidhātavyaḥ | itarathāsmāskhetasmādetadajñānajanitaṃ mahāmandākṣamudeṣyati | <lb> tarhi prabhāvati tvamapi vicārya vyāhara | sa śakalāṭastadā nandanarendrasyājñāṃ śirasyādhāya kamupā<pb>yamakalpayat | tadā śukoditā prabhāvatī tadvicāraṇāya cāru cāturyaṃ dadhānāpi paraṃ na vivektuṃ <lb> prabhavati sma | tadā śukameva punaraprākṣīt | tadā śukastadvyāharaṇāya prārambhate sma | prabhāvati maduktau <lb> sāvadhānā bhava | tadā sa śakalāṭastadvaḍavādvayamapi saparyāṇīkṛtavān | vyāyāmaṃ garīyāṃsaṃ ca kā<lb>rayāmāsa turaṃgamādibhiḥ | tadanu paryāṇe pṛthagvidhāya dāmādibandhanamapākṛtya navatṛṇameva cakitāyāṃ <lb> medinyāṃ caraṇāya vyasrākṣīt | tadānīṃ jananī tanayāṃ rasanayā leḍhuṃ prāvartiṣṭa tanayā ca jananyāḥ <lb> stanyaṃ pātumudayata | iti nirdhāritavānsacivacūḍāmaṇiḥ | tarhi prabhāvati tvamapyevaṃvidhaṃ kartuṃ nirṇayaṃ <lb> pārayasi yadi tadā gamanāya yatnaṃ tanuhi || <lb> ityaṣṭapañcāśatkathā || 58 || <lb>

379,9

punaḥ prabhāvatī papraccha śukaṃ śuko 'bhyadhāt | dharmabuddhivadupāyavivecanaṃ kartumīśiṣe yadi tadānīṃ sā<lb>dhayepsitam | tataḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ dharmabuddhivṛttāntamaprākṣīt | vihago jagāda giram 380,1

anyedyurdināntodaye kumudakośanandinī vinayakandarpaniketanaṃ jigamiṣurdvijaṃ praśnayati | tadanvavādītpa<lb>tatrī | devi jayaśrīriva buddhivaibhavaṃ pariśīlayasi yadi tadā yāhi | sā jayaśriyo vivadamānāścatvāro deśāntarādāgatāḥ <lb> puruṣāḥ | tadānīṃ tānapṛcchannareśvaraḥ | bhavatāṃ kiṃnibandhano vyavahāraḥ | vayaṃ deśāntaraṃ gatāḥ | ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ <lb> ca tatrāsmābhiralambhi | tānyekatra sthāpitāni | tato rājāvevaitasyāṃ na jānīmaḥ kimajāyata | caturṇā<lb>masmākaṃ madhye ko nāma tāni gṛhītavān | iti niśamya vyājahāra | amātya eteṣāṃ caturṇaṃ madhye <lb> katamo ratnānyagrahīt | tvaṃ samyagvicārya vyāharatāt | itthaṃ rājñābhihite sacivastāṃścaturo nijama<lb>ndiramānayāmāsa | teṣāṃ bhojanaṃ ca viśrāmasthānaṃ ca prāyacchat | tataste pradhānasahitāścatvāro 'pyupa<lb>viviśuḥ | tataḥ sacivatanayā jayaśrīsteṣāṃ vivādaṃ pṛcchati sma | ka ete kasmātpradeśātkena prayojana<lb>viśeṣeṇātrāgamanamakārṣuḥ | sacivasteṣāmāgamanakāraṇaṃ sarvamavādīt | tanniśamya jagāda jayaśrīḥ | ahame<lb>vāmuṣya ratnacatuṣṭayasya gṛhītāraṃ vicārayiṣyāmi | tarhi prabhāvati kenopāyena viśeṣanirṇayaṃ vidadhāti <lb> sma ratnānām | sā vicāraṃ kurvāṇāpi nāvāgacchat | tadā śukaṃ vakti sma | śuko babhāṣe | tatasteṣāṃ <lb> caturṇāṃ rātrāvabhyavahāro 'jāyata | tato nidrākaraṇāya pṛthakpṛthaksthāne caturo 'pi prāsthāpayat | <lb> tadanu tamasvinyāmātmānamalaṃkṛtyaikasyopakaṇṭhamājagāma jayaśrīḥ | tāvattamavocat | mama mānasaṃ bhavaddarśa<lb>naprabhṛti smaraśarāhativikīrṇadhairyaṃ bhavati | bhavantaṃ vihāya na kaṃcidapyabhilaṣati sma | yadi pañcaśataṃ <lb> suvarṇānāṃ mahyaṃ dāsyasi tadānīmahaṃ bhavataḥ kulapālikātvamaṅgīkaromi | so 'pyavocat | paramidānīṃ <lb> pāṇigataṃ na kimapi dravyamasti | ahamārjayitvā bhavatyai vitariṣyāmi | tatastanniśamanātsāpi taṃ vihāya <lb> dvitīyamanusasāra | tamapi tathaivāvocat | tataḥ so 'pi na kimapītyavocat | tathaiva tṛtīyopakaṇṭhamā<lb>seduṣī taṃ tathaivāvādīt | tataḥ saṃprati mama haste na kimapyastīti tasya vyavahāramāśrutya caturthaṃ paśyati <lb> sma dṛśā dhairyasarvasvahāriṇyā | taṃ ca tathaiva prājalpat | tatastvasau ahaṃ pañcāśatsuvarṇaparyāptaṃ vastuviśeṣaṃ <lb> dāsyāmi bhavatyā haste | ityabhidhāya pāṇau prādādratnacatuṣṭayaṃ tasyāḥ | sā ca tadratnacatuṣṭayaṃ gṛhītvā <lb> adya tvasādhumuhūrtaṃ dinaṃ vartate prātastvāvayorekatropaveśanāya samyaṅmuhūrtamasti | iti tamabhidhāya <lb> svagṛhamāgatya ratnāni janakasya haste prāyacchat | sa ṣaṣṭikathā || 60 || <lb>

380,28

punaḥ prabhāvatī papraccha śukam | tadanu śuko babhāṣe | bhūdharabrāhmaṇavadāyāsanistaraṇe pragalbhase yadi <lb> tadā yātu bhavatī | sā bhūdharavṛttāntaṃ vyāhareti vyāhārṣīt | śuko 'pi vakti sma | devi camatkārapuryāṃ <lb> bhūdharanāmā brāhmaṇo nivasati | sa tu paṅguḥ | tata ekasminnavasare samastairbrāhmaṇaiḥ saha devatādarśanāya <lb> śakaṭārūḍho niragamat | tadanu gacchatāṃ mārge dasyava udatiṣṭhan | te sarve 'pi bāndhavā dasyandṛṣṭvāpalā<lb>yiṣata | sa tu caraṇavihīnatvātpalāyanasāmarthyamabibhrāṇastathaivāsthāt | tarhyācakṣva prabhāvati | sa tu bhūdharaḥ <lb> kamupāyaṃ parikalpya dasyubhya ātmānamudamocayat | tadā prabhāvatī vicārayantyapi na viveda | tataḥ <lb> pañjaragataṃ kīraṃ pṛcchati sma prabhāvatī | tato 'vadacchuko 'pi | ākarṇaya prabhāvati | sarvānsvayūdhyā<lb>npalāyanaparāyaṇānmalimbucaśca dhāvato dṛṣṭvā tadanvekākyeva bhūdharo vaktumupākramata dhāvamānānpunarā<lb>kārayan | aho bhavantaḥ kimiti palāyanaṃ kurvanti | tatra ca na santi pañcādaśītiśataparyāptāḥ paripa<lb>nthikāḥ | eteṣāṃ catuḥpañcaṣāṇāṃ bhītyā kimiti dhāvantaḥ santi | iyatāmeteṣāmahamevālam | śatahanteti <pb> madīyaṃ virudaṃ jagati prasiddham | tadīyaṃ vacanamākarṇya corāḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā taṃ vihāyaiva yathāgataṃ <lb> niraguḥ | tarhi prabhāvatyevaṃvidhaṃ buddhivaibhavaṃ jānāsi yadi tadā sādhaya || <lb> ityekaṣaṣṭikathā || 61 || <lb>
<pb n="381">

381,4

punaḥ prabhāvatī praṣṭuṃ prāvartata śukam | śuko 'bhyadhātprabhāvatīm | bhukkuṇḍavadātmano maraṇamanyathā kartuṃ <lb> jānīṣe yadi tadāṅgīkarotu bhavatī | tadā prabhāvatī papraccha | bhukkuṇḍa iti ko nāmāsau | kathaṃ mara<lb>ṇamanyathayat | tadvṛttāntaṃ vyāharatāṃ bhavān | prabhāvatīṃ pratyavadacchukaḥ | śṛṇu prabhāvati | sarvatobhadraṃ nāma <lb> nagaram | tatra bhukkuṇḍanāmā kitavo nivasati sa ca sarvadā dyūtena dvīpyati | ekasmindine dīvyanpra<lb>tikitavaiḥ parājitaḥ | teṣāmaṅgīkṛtapaṇārpaṇāya na kimapyasti | tadānīṃ cauryāya prāyatata | tadā cauryaṃ <lb> kurvāṇo rātrirakṣakairvidhṛto 'sau | te ca taṃ rājasamakṣamāninyuḥ | rājā ca vadhāya bhaṭānādiṣṭavān | <lb> gacchatainaṃ nītvā śūlaprotaṃ kuruta | tarhi prabhāvati bhavatyapi vyāharatu | kena prakāreṇātmano maraṇamanyathayat | <lb> tadā prabhāvatī vicāravatyapi nājñāsīt | tadāprākṣocchukam | so 'bravīt | ākarṇaya prabhāvati | tadā <lb> tāṃstaskaro 'bhihitavān | rājā vyāpādayitumuditavānasti | yato rājñāmeva svābhāviko 'yaṃ dharmaḥ <lb> paripālayitavyo duṣṭāśca niyamanīyā ityetādṛśaṃ sārāsāraṃ vicārayati mahīpatiḥ | tadānīmasāvai<lb>hikenāmuṣmikeṇa ca sukṛtena saṃyujyate | ata eva mayi daṇḍaṃ pātitavān | tatsamyagucitaṃ kṛtavānasi | <lb> paraṃ vijñaptirekā vidyate | ahaṃ ślokamekaṃ vyāharāmi tadākarṇanāyāvadhānaṃ dātavyam | <lb>
bhaṭṭirnaṣṭo bhāraviścāpi naṣṭo bhikṣurnaṣṭo bhīmaseno 'pi naṣṭaḥ |
bhukkuṇḍo 'haṃ bhūpatistvaṃ hi rājanpaṅktau bhasyāpyantakaḥ saṃniviṣṭaḥ ||

381,18

rājā etasya padyasyārthaṃ vyākhyāhīti vyājahāra | tato dasyuravadat | śloko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyottarapurāṇe | <lb> etasyāyamarthaḥ | teṣāmādivarṇī bhakāraḥ teṣu nāmasu paripāṭyāmantakaḥ saṃniviṣṭaḥ | bhaṭṭācāryamapi kali<lb>tavānkālaḥ | tadanu bhāravimapi nigīrṇavānkālaḥ | bhikṣuṃ tathā bhīmasenaṃ ca kalitavānkālaḥ | etāṃścaturo <lb> 'pyagrahītkālaḥ | bhukkuṇḍa iti madīyaṃ nāma bhūpatiriti tvadīyaṃ nāma | mayi nihate tvameka evāva<lb>śiṣṭo 'si | yāvadahaṃ bhavataḥ purato bhavāmi na tāvatkālakalitaṃ bhayam | yathā jānāsi tathānusaṃdhehi | <lb> tadanu nṛpatistadākarṇya manasyevameveti niścitya taṃ coramamocayat | tarhi prabhāvati etādṛśamupāyaviśeṣaṃ <lb> yadi jānīṣe tarhi vidhehi vidheyaviśeṣam || <lb> iti dviṣaṣṭikathā || 62 || <lb>

381,26

punarapi niśāsamaye vinayakandarpasaṃnidhānagamanāya prerayāmāsa patatriṇaṃ prabhāvatī | tadā śuko 'pya<lb>bhidadhe | devi devaśarmavatsaṃkīrṇāvasarāpāte yadyuttaraṃ kartuṃ pārayasi tadā yāhi | tadā prabhāvatī babhāṣe | <lb> devaśarmā kathaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ nistīrṇavānuttaraviśeṣakalpanena | vyācaṣṭāṃ bhavāniti tayā pṛṣṭaḥ śuko vyācaṣṭe | <lb> prabhāvati elānagaryāmelanāmadheyo rājā rājyaṃ praśāsti | devaśarmāsau śrīmatāmamātyabhūtaḥ | etasya cintā na kartavyā | etasya kasminnapi kārya<lb>viśeṣe viniyogo dātavyaḥ | yadi tadvidheyaṃ sattayā samarthitaṃ tadānīṃ purastādetadaṅgīkāraṃ puraskṛtyā<lb>jīvikā kalpanīyā | tadānīmamātyavacanānnagaranātho nijaprayojanasādhanāya tamādideśa | tasminpaśyati <pb> peśīdvayamānīya bhasmanā pūrayitvopari rājamudrayā mudrayitvā devaśarmāṇamāhūya tvayā śatrusūdaname<lb>dinīpatisamīpaṃ gatvā elarājena vārṣiko daṇḍaḥ prasthāpito 'stīti abhidhāya tasmai dātavyamadaḥ <lb> peśīdvayamityuktvā peśike te devaśarmaṇaḥ pāṇāvarpayāmāsa | tena rājñā samaṃ saujanyamatitarāmaidhiṣṭa | <lb> tathā vidhātavyaṃ bhavateti vyāhṛtya devaśarmāṇaṃ vyasrākṣīdelamahīpatiḥ | tadā tadādeśācchatrusūdanamahīndraṃ <lb> saṃgatya tasya purastātpeśikādvayaṃ nidhāya vijñaptavān | amuṃ vārṣikakaramelamahīpatirbhavatāṃ prasthāpayā<lb>māsa | ityabhidhāya mudrāmunmucya paśyati peśīdvayaṃ yāvatā tāvatā bhasitapūritāntaramālakṣya śatrusūdano <lb> medinīpatiḥ nā<lb>vindata | tadānīmatītāyāṃ tamasvinyāṃ śukamanvayuṅkta | tataḥ śuko vyājahāra | tadānīṃ devaśarmābhidhatte | <lb> devāsmadīyo mahīpālo yajñamakārṣīt | tatkuṇḍasaṃbhavāṃ vibhūtiṃ bhavatāmarthe prasthāpitavān | vibhūtiriyaṃ <lb> yatra vidyate tatra daivadaśā rājyābhyudayaśca yugapatsaṃbhavataḥ | grahapīḍāśca naśyanti | śatravo 'pi mitrāṇi <lb> bhavanti | āyuśca vardhate | etāvanto guṇā 382,17

punaḥ prabhāvatī abhāṣata nabhogaṃ śuko 'pyavadat | devi sumatiriva saṃkīrṇanistaraṇopāyaṃ yadi vetsyasi <lb> tadābhisāra ādriyatām | prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭastadvṛttāntaṃ śuko 'pi rarāṇa | ākarṇaya devi | maṅgalapuranāmni <lb> grāme sumatirnāma vipaṇiḥ | sa dhanārjanāyodyamamuddiśya pradeśaviśeṣe kutracidgato 'bhavat | tatra bhūridhana<lb>mārjitavānsadhanaḥ samāgacchanmadhyamārge dasyūnadrākṣīt | tarhi prabhāvati vyāhara | tadā sa kathaṃkāramupāya<lb>viśeṣaṃ viśeṣayati sma | tadā prabhāvatī vicārya nājñāsīt | tadā prātaḥ śukamaprākṣīt | śuko 'pyavocat | <lb> devi niśamyāvadhatsva | sa tu dasyūndṛṣṭvā samīpasthitaṃ gaṇeśaprāsādaṃ prāvikṣat | tatra gaṇeśamūrteḥ purastā<lb>dupaviśya draviṇapeṭikāṃ vivṛtya tadantaḥsthitaṃ dhanaṃ bahirvidhāya pañcakīkaraṇena paṅktiṣu taddhanaṃ tyaktavān | <lb> tato ghaṭikāṃ gṛhītvā gaṇādhipamabhyadhādvakṣyamāṇaprakāreṇa | deva vighnarāja idamātmīyaṃ dhanaṃ gṛhāṇa | <lb> idametāvatprathato bhavato dhanam | ayaṃ lābho jātaḥ | anenaiva saṃcarataḥ catvāri hāyanānyajāyanta mama <lb> bhavadīyāṃ sevāṃ kurvaṇasya | ahaṃ ca tava vāṇijyakartā satyamasatyaṃ sevāṃ tāvajjānāno 'smi | madīyā <lb> sevā bhavadāyattā | etādṛśāni vacāṃsi dasyava aśrauṣuḥ | tataḥ parasparamabhidadhire | ayaṃ vaṇik devasya <lb> vacanakartā | enaṃ yadi nirīkṣāmaḥ tadānīṃ devo 'pyasmākamupari kamapi tādṛśaṃ vighnamāpādayiṣyati <lb> yādṛśenāsmākaṃ sarvanāśo bhavitā | ityabhidhāya vaṇijaṃ | tatyajuḥ | yadi prabhāvati tvamapīdṛśopāya<lb>karaṇavicakṣaṇāsi tadā sādhayepsitam || <lb> iti catuḥṣaṣṭikathā || 64 || <lb> (kathās 65–67 and first part of 68 missing) <lb>

382,32

* * * tasminvaṭe ulūkā nivasanti | kadācana rātrau pāraṇāya niraguḥ samantataḥ | teṣāṃ madhyādekolūko <lb> bhrānto mārgaṃ vihāyaikasya vaṭasyopari paryapatat | tadā tatra divaso 'jāyata niṣkāsanaprakāraḥ pratyapakārasya kartuṃ śakyate yadi tarhi kriyatām | <lb> tatastadīyaṃ vacanaṃ niśamya sarve tajjātīyā bāndhavāḥ kākānnihantumudacalan | samāgatya taṃ vṛkṣamaveṣṭayan | <lb> tatravasatīnkākānsarvānnijaghnuḥ | tadanu sarve 'pyulūkā nirgatya nijadhānīṃ jagmuḥ | teṣāṃ madhyādeko vāyaso <lb> 'vatatāra | sarveṣu māryamāṇeṣu kākeṣvasāveka eva kutrāpi dalagahane nilīyātmānaṃ jugopa | tadanu tadā<lb>skandanaṃ dṛṣṭvā balipuṣṭānāmatikaṣṭāṃ daśāṃ manasyanubhūya kiṃciddhairyamavalambya parāmṛśya vimṛśya ca vidheya<lb>viśeṣaṃ kimataḥ paraṃ kartuṃ śakyate | te 'smadvairiṇo 'bhyadhāt | bhavatāṃ śaraṇamāgato 'haṃ dāsānudāsaḥ | bhavatāmeva caraṇānmanasi dhṛtvā <lb> samāyāsiṣam | ye ca duṣṭā bhavatāṃ vairiṇo 'bhūvaṃste sarve bhavadbhistu vyāpāditāḥ | idānīmahameka eva <lb> * <lb> * * iti vyājahruḥ | kramamātro 'yaṃ tarhi kiṃ nāmāyaṃ varāko vai kariṣyati kāka iti teṣāṃ pṛthaṅmatīnāṃ <lb> vacobhirantarmāyo 'sau tatraivātiṣṭhat | tadanu tatra sthitvā tānvyāhārṣīt | madīyaḥ kaścidupacāro bhavatāṃ <lb> bhavitavyaḥ | ahaṃ bhavatāṃ kṛte śayyāṃ sādhīyasīṃ kalpayiṣyāmītyabhidhāya śālmalatūlena ślakṣṇena tasya <lb> viṭapinaḥ sarvamapi koṭaraṃ pūritavān | rātrau svayaṃ dvāri 383,21

punaḥ prabhāvatī praṣṭuṃ prāvartata patatriṇam | śuko 'bhyadhāt | devi tadā sā dhūrtacakorābhihitā vārttā <lb> somadattasya mānase na sthānamātanoti | tadanu somadattastaṃ dhūrtacakoraṃ tataḥ prabhāte kuṭṭinī rājamandiramagādasyāḥ purastā<lb>dityāvedya śuko 'yaṃ nihantavyaḥ | etadīyaṃ māṃsaṃ sādhuruci paktavyam | iti tasyai nideśaṃ dattvā niragāt | <lb> tadanu dāsī kīramānīya kimapyanāgataṃ <lb> jānāmi | tadbhavatyāḥ purastādāvedayāmi tavaiva hitam | tadanu tvaṃ māṃ vyāpādaya | tadanvavādīddāsī | <lb> tarhyācaṣṭāṃ nāma bhavān | tadābhyadhātpakṣī | tvametasya māṃsasya madhye garīyasīṃ saṃpadamavāpsyasi | tvaṃ yathā <lb> cārvaṅgī bhaviṣyasi tathauṣadhaṃ dāsyāmi paścādyāsyāmi tava vaśam | tulasīdalaṃ kuśadarbhāṃścānaya gomayopa<lb>liptāyāṃ bhūmau kuśānāstīrya 384,4

punaḥ prabhāvatī praśnīkṛtavatī patatriṇam | śuko bhaṇati sma | devi tasyaiva dhūrtacakorasya śukasyeva mati<lb>ryadyātmano 'pāyamākṛṣṭumatyate tadānīmaṭatu bhavatī | tataḥ prabhāvatī provāca | tadvṛttāntaṃ vāvadītu bhavā<lb>niti | tadā tajjagāda drumasadmā | tadā tu kiṃcidulluñcitapucchaḥ śuka uḍḍīya gatavān | induvāsarenduva<lb>danā kāmasenā tatrenduśekharaprāsāde nṛtyati | tataḥ śukaḥ pūrvameva tatra gatvā liṅgasyāśraye karapraceyapattre <lb> bilvadrumakoṭare nilīya tasthau | tadanu kāmasenānṛttāvasāne saṃpūrṇe jāte śivaliṅgamahimarūpādrumamadhyā<lb>dudasthātkaścana śabdaḥ | kāmasene madīyasevāṃ gatayā tvayā bahūni divasāni atītāni | tubhyaṃ bhavatyā <lb> bhaktyatiśayabhāvanayā prasanno 'smi | āgāmini somavāre prathamapraharasamaye kāmikavimānamāruhya kailā<lb>saparvate matsaṃnidhānamavāpsyasi paśyatāṃ sakalalokānām | tāvatā bhaktyā pūrvajanane śabhajanadurantadurita<lb>nikaraparipākā dūrataḥ palāyante | tadanu saudāminītaralaṃ sakalavaibhavamarthisādvidhehi saṃbhṛtam | tadanu <lb> sarvaprāyaścittasya mukhyāṅgabhūtaṃ kṣauramapi dvābhyāṃ bhavatībhyāṃ vidhāya devasya mama prāsādāgrabhūmimāruhya <lb> sthātavyam | prathamaghaṭīcatuṣṭayādupari tatra sthitvā nṛttagītādikaṃ kurvāṇāyā yāmadvayavarivasyādatta<lb>cittāyā bhavatyāḥ savidhamāpatiṣyati vimānayugalaṃ prathamayāme pūrṇe sati | tadanu sarveṣu sāścaryaṃ dattā<lb>vadhāneṣu nārījaneṣu kāmasenā niśamya satpātrasātprakalpya <lb> śiromuṇḍanaṃ vidhāya kāṣāyavasanaṃ paridhāya devasenayā saha mṛdaṅgavādyādimaṅgalaghoṣanṛttagītādyanekā<lb>ḍambaraprasṛmarasaṃbhramotsavā yāmayugma<lb>mapyajaniṣṭa paraṃ nāgate vimāne | tadanu bilvapādapasyopari sthitaḥ pakṣī vyājahāra giraṃ sa kīraḥ | <lb>
śaṭhe pratiśaṭhaṃ kuryādādare ca tathādaram |
tvayā me luñcitāḥ pakṣāḥ mayā te muṇḍitaṃ śiraḥ ||

384,28

tarhi prabhāvati buddhiriyaṃ protsphurati yadi tadidānīṃ yātu bhavatī || <lb> iti saptatikathā || 70 || <lb>

384,30

anyedyurvinayakandarpaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ prabhāvatīmandiramiyāya | prabhāvatī ca nijamandiramāgataṃ mahīpālaṃ <lb> mahatā premabhareṇa saṃdarśanena saṃbhāvya tatropaveṣṭuṃ siṃhāsanamacīkarat | rājā ca siṃhāsanamadhyarukṣat | tadā <lb> pañjaraśāyinaṃ kīraṃ nirīkṣya taṃ jighāṃsurmārjāraḥ kriyāsamabhihāreṇa virauti sma | tato rorūyamāṇaṃ <lb> mārjāraṃ provāca śukaḥ | <lb>
kiṃ tvaṃ rodiṣi mārjāra na cārirna ca taskaraḥ |
nandabhūpakumāro 'yaṃ paranārīsahodaraḥ ||

384,36

itthaṃ kīragiramākarṇya baddhamauna eva niragādvinayakandarpaḥ || <lb> iti kathākośe śukasaptatiḥ samāptā || <lb> || śrīrastu || <lb>
